# Book of Mormon Walk вЂ” Knowledge Graph

The connection index, grown one chapter at a time. Pull from this to trace threads across the Book of Mormon and into our existing studies.

## Node types
`person` В· `place` В· `doctrine` В· `type/symbol` В· `prophecy` В· `covenant` В· `event` В· `study-link` (в†’ our 198 studies, found via `study_search` / `study_similar`)

## Edge types
`cross-ref` В· `fulfillment` (prophecyв†’event) В· `parallel` В· `typeв†’antitype` В· `covenant-thread` В· `doctrinal-development` В· `links-to-study`

## Conventions
- Stable node ids: `person:lehi`, `doctrine:tender-mercies`, `type:liahona`, `study:give-away-all-my-sins`.
- Edge line: `{from} вЂ”[type]в†’ {to}   (provenance ref; short note)`
- Append as the walk proceeds. Periodic synthesis passes (at book boundaries) surface emergent patterns into `_journal.md`.

### from 2 Nephi 20 (Isaiah 10)

- image: `axe-boasts-against-the-hewer` (instrument credits itself = misattribution, deepest pride, v15 вЂ” live for any instrument incl. AI/me) В· `the-same-fire` (light of Israel a flame, v17)
- variant: `their-indignation` (v5 BoM for KJV "mine" вЂ” minor, VERIFIED); else close to KJV

### from 2 Nephi 21 (Isaiah 11) вЂ” Restoration keystone (D&C 113; JS-H 1:40)
- isaiah: `11` (stem of Jesse + peaceable kingdom + second gathering)
- person: `stem-of-Jesse` (Christ) В· `rod`+`root` (latter-day servants, D&C 113) В· `the-recovered-remnant` В· `ephraim`+`judah` (reconciled)
- doctrine: `peace-by-knowledge` (they shall not hurt FOR earth full of knowledge, v9 вЂ” Millennium as epistemological state; D&C 130:18) В· `judge-not-by-appearance` (v3-4) В· `stem-rod-root-of-Jesse` (D&C 113) В· `second-gathering` (v11) В· `ephraim-and-judah-reconciled` (two sticks, v13)
- meta: `glory-chapters-near-identical` (Isa 9+11 ~verbatim; variants cluster in judgment chapters вЂ” BoM reworks warnings not glory)

### from 2 Nephi 22 (Isaiah 12) вЂ” doxology sealing Isaiah 2-12
- isaiah: `12` (the song of the redeemed)
- resolution: `anger-turned-away` (v1 вЂ” resolves the "his anger is not turned away" refrain of 15/19/20)
- echo: `song-of-Moses` (v2 "Jehovah my strength and song" = Ex 15:2; second-Exodus sings the first's)
- image: `wells-of-salvation` (joy as repeated drawing, v3)
- doctrine: `Holy-One-in-the-midst` (block ends at presence, v6 вЂ” Immanuel home)
- meta: near-identical to KJV (v2 verb form only) вЂ” confirms glory-chapters-faithful pattern

### from 2 Nephi 23 (Isaiah 13) вЂ” richest variant cluster in the block
- isaiah: `13` (burden of Babylon = type of the world; Day of the Lord)
- type: `babylon-is-the-world` (D&C 133:14; Rev 17-18)
- prophecy: `day-of-the-Lord-cosmic-signs` (sun/moon/stars darkened, v10 вЂ” Matt 24:29)
- doctrine: `worth-of-souls` (a man more precious than fine gold, v12)
- variant: `mercy-inserted` (v3 "anger NOT upon them that rejoice in my highness" вЂ” VERIFIED) В· `target-is-pride` (v15 "proud" for KJV "found" вЂ” VERIFIED) В· `mercy-coda` (v22 BoM adds "merciful unto my people" вЂ” VERIFIED) В· v8 omission
- META-FINDING: `judgment-variants-tilt-to-mercy` (the cluster all pulls one way вЂ” BoM's reworking of Isaiah's warnings is theological: more merciful to the faithful, more precisely aimed at pride)

### from 2 Nephi 24 (Isaiah 14) вЂ” LAST chapter of the Isaiah block (12-24 = Isa 2-14 COMPLETE)
- isaiah: `14` (fall of king of Babylon в†’ fall of Lucifer)
- person: `lucifer`/`son-of-the-morning` (pride's root) В· `the-poor` (trust in founded Zion, v32)
- doctrine: `five-I-wills` (anatomy of pride: self grasps God's throne, v13-14; Moses 4; D&C 76:25-29) В· `up-is-down-inversion` (Lucifer ascendsв†’pit; Christ descendsв†’exalted, v15) В· `mercy-on-Jacob`/restoration (v1-3)
- refrain: `hand-stretched-out` (third mode: sovereign irreversible purpose, v26-27 вЂ” angerв†’comfortв†’decree)
- image: `zion-for-the-poor` (block's last word, v32 вЂ” ground poor of ch13 now trust in Zion; bookends 12:2)
- variant: `lands-of-promise-added` (v2 вЂ” fits restoration tilt) В· `remnant/raiment` (v19) В· `bring/break` (v25); Lucifer passage shared w/ KJV
- META: `isaiah-block-complete` (arc: mountain rises в†’ all pride falls to its Luciferian root в†’ Zion for the poor)

### from 2 Nephi 25 (Nephi's plainness вЂ” block synthesis)
- person: `nephi` (the plain prophet, "I have seen his day") В· `jesus-christ` (NAMED + dated v19) В· `the-Jews` (rejectв†’crucifyв†’scatteredв†’restored on belief)
- doctrine: `plainness-as-method` (chosen vs "manner of the Jews", v1-8) В· `Christ-named-and-dated` (Jesus Christ, Son of God, 600 yrs, v19) В· `no-other-name` (v20; Acts 4:12) В· `grace-after-all-we-can-do` (v23 вЂ” effort turns toward grace, grace saves) В· `we-talk-of-Christ` (v26 вЂ” plainness distilled) В· `law-kept-but-dead` (obey the type, watch the antitype, v24-27)
- synthesis: `isaiah-block` (Nephi supplies the plain interpreter for chs 12-24)
- FLAG: 25:23 grace/works = strongest remaining 2 Ne spin-off candidate

### from 2 Nephi 26 (Nephite destruction + last days + priestcraft + inclusivity)
- person: `the-risen-Christ` (ministers to Nephites) В· `last-days-Gentiles` (pride, priestcraft, grind the poor) В· `all-mankind` (black/white, bond/free, male/female вЂ” none forbidden)
- doctrine: `all-are-alike-unto-God` (26:33 вЂ” **answers 2 Ne 5:21, same author**) В· `priestcraft-defined` (self as light + gain + praise, not Zion's welfare, v29) В· `labor-for-Zion-not-money` (v31) В· `inclusivity-grounded-in-atonement` (loveth the world, draws all, v24) В· `Spirit-will-not-always-strive` (v11)
- image: `voice-from-the-dust` (the BoM as a buried people's whisper, v15-16; Isa 29:4)
- thread: `grind-the-face-of-the-poor` (Isaiah-block carryover, v20 в†ђ 13:15)

### from 2 Nephi 27 (sealed book вЂ” Nephi's expansion of Isaiah 29)
- person: `the-unlearned-man` (Joseph Smith) В· `the-learned-man` (Anthon, by fulfillment) В· `three-witnesses`
- prophecy: `sealed-book-coming-forth` (BoM prophesies its own emergence, v6-23; Anthon fulfillment JS-H 1:64-65)

### from 2 Nephi 28 (last-days deceptions)

- doctrine: `devils-three-strategies` (rage v20 / carnal-security-"all is well" v21 / denial-"no hell" v22 вЂ” lullaby deadliest) В· `little-sin-gospel` (cheap grace, v8) В· `line-upon-line` (open revelation; "enough" forfeits, v30) В· `trust-not-arm-of-flesh` (v31)
- warning: `all-is-well-in-zion` (complacency among the faithful, v21,24) В· `humble-can-be-led-to-err` (precepts of men, v14)
- thread: `rob-the-poor-fine-sanctuaries` (v13 вЂ” grind-the-poor sharpest: 13:15 в†’ 26:20 в†’ here) В· `arm-lengthened-out` (v32 вЂ” Isaiah "hand stretched out" as lengthened mercy)

### from 2 Nephi 29 ("A Bible! A Bible!" вЂ” open canon)
- person: `the-closed-canon-Gentiles` (ingrate) В· `the-Jews` (Bible's source, hated yet not forgotten) В· `all-nations` (all writing scripture)
- doctrine: `open-canon-from-Gods-sameness` (closed canon requires a God who quit; "the same yesterday today forever, my work not finished", v9) В· `God-speaks-to-all-nations` ("more nations than one", v7,11-12) В· `two-witnesses-not-competition` (BoM corroborates the Bible, v8) В· `judged-out-of-the-books` (v11)

### from 2 Nephi 30 (covenant fulfilled + millennial peace)
- doctrine: `covenant-by-repentance-not-race` (Gentiles who repent ARE covenant; Jews who won't are cast off, v2) В· `peace-by-knowledge` (Isa 11 re-quoted, v15) В· `total-revelation` (nothing sealed but shall be loosed, v16-17) В· `Satan-bound` (v18)

- event: Nephi ends his prophesying (v18)

### from 2 Nephi 31 (the doctrine of Christ вЂ” keystone)
- doctrine: `gate-and-path` (baptism = gate/entry; endure to the end = path, v17-20) В· `is-all-done-Nay` (entering в‰  arriving, v19 вЂ” cure for 28/29 complacency) В· `Christ-the-baptized-example` (sinless one baptized to fulfil all righteousness, a fortiori, v5-9) В· `rely-wholly-on-his-merits` (press-forward is grace-powered, v19) В· `endurance-triad` (faith/hope/charity = path's fuel, v20) В· `this-is-the-way` (exclusive, no other name, v21)
- CONVERGENCE: `feast-on-the-word = hold-the-rod` (1 Ne 8:24 rod named: "feasting upon the word of Christ", v20) В· `the-gate` (= 9:41 Holy One no servant + 1 Ne 8 strait gate) вЂ” the tree-of-life dream + doctrine of Christ = same map

### from 2 Nephi 32 (doctrine of Christ continued)
- doctrine: `two-guides-for-the-path` (the word TELLS v3 + the Spirit SHOWS v5 "all things what ye should do") В· `prayerlessness-is-the-tell` (evil spirit teaches a man NOT to pray, v8) В· `ask-and-knock` (or perish in the dark, v4) В· `pray-always-consecrate-performance` (pray first, v9)
- thread: `feast=hold-the-rod` (v3 вЂ” confirms 31:20 = 1 Ne 8:24)
- lament: `refused-plainness` (Spirit stops Nephi's utterance; people won't search plainness, v7 вЂ” "we have enough" felt by the teacher)

### from 2 Nephi 33 (Nephi's farewell вЂ” closes 2 Nephi)
- doctrine: `carried-unto-not-into-the-heart` (Spirit brings truth to the door; hardened heart gives it no place, v1-2) В· `book-Christ-interlock` (believe Christ в†’ believe the words, v10) В· `doctrine-of-Christ-recapped` (reconciledв†’gateв†’pathв†’endure, v9)
- image: `nephi's-tears` (eyes water my pillow by night, v3) В· `face-to-face-at-the-bar` (writer + reader meet at judgment, v11,15) В· `voice-from-the-dust` (Nephi's farewell, v13)
- creed: `three-glories` (plainness в†’ truth в†’ my Jesus who redeemed my soul, v6)
- SYNTHESIS: **2 NEPHI COMPLETE** вЂ” doctrine of Christ rendered plain: "we talk of Christ" (25:26) в†’ "I glory in my Jesus" (33:6); opens Lehi-dying-"opposition in all things" в†’ closes Nephi-dying-"I glory in my Jesus"

## вЂ” JACOB вЂ”

### from Jacob 1
- person: `jacob` (priest, record-keeper, watchman) В· `joseph` (fellow priest) В· `nephi` (dies; name retained as throne-title) В· `the-anointed-kings` ("second Nephi") В· `the-seven-tribes`
- doctrine: `watchmans-burden` (answer the people's sins on our own heads if we don't teach with diligence, v19 вЂ” inverse of priestcraft) В· `small-plates-curation` (only most precious, for Christ's sake, v2-4) В· `discipleship-includes-the-shame` (view his death, suffer his cross, v8) В· `division-by-allegiance` (Lamanite = seeks to destroy; Nephite = friendly to Nephi, v14)
- relic: `sword-of-Laban` (Nephi wielded it; passes with kingship, v10)
- setup: `pride-and-polygamy` (David/Solomon's many wives; gold; pride, v15-16 в†’ Jacob 2-3)

### from Jacob 2 (temple sermon: pride + chastity)
- theme: `strong-wounding-the-weak` (pride persecutes the poor v13 + unchastity breaks wives' hearts v35 вЂ” one sin, two forms)
- doctrine: `order-and-intent-of-riches` (kingdom first, THEN riches for the intent to do good, v18-19) В· `free-with-your-substance` ("that they may be rich like unto you", v17) В· `one-being-as-precious` (equality, v21) В· `monogamy-standard` (one wife; David/Solomon abominable; v30 seed-raising exception, v24-30) В· `God-hears-the-wounded-wives` (v31-35)
- thread: `watchmans-burden-in-action` (bold rebuke despite wounding the innocent, v6-11 в†ђ 1:19)

### from Jacob 3 (comfort + the Lamanites "more righteous")
- reversal: `despised-are-the-standard` (the hated Lamanites "more righteous" вЂ” measure = family fidelity, v5-7)
- doctrine: `comfort-to-the-wounded` (feast on his love, balm after the daggers, v1-2) В· `revile-not-for-the-skin` (v9) В· `filthiness-is-inherited-circumstance` (came because of their fathers, v7,9)
- image: `awake-from-the-slumber-of-death` (arouse, shake yourselves, v11)
- FLAG (bin-4): `skin-curse-language` v5-9 вЂ” Jacob USES it AND empties it (dark = more righteous; reviling forbidden; filthiness inherited not personal; white-skinned the more filthy before God) в†’ **THIRD in-text datapoint for the 5:21 with-Michael study** (with 26:33 + 30:6); NOT autonomously resolved

### from Jacob 4 (law points to Christ; look beyond the mark)
- doctrine: `looking-beyond-the-mark` (blindness from disdaining plainness, seeking the obscure, v14 вЂ” negative of the plainness thread) В· `truth-is-things-as-they-really-are` (v13 в†’ D&C 93:24) В· `power-by-grace-weakness-shown` (command trees by grace, "that we may know", v7 вЂ” positive form of axe/made-thing) В· `take-counsel-from-his-hand` (don't counsel God, v10) В· `law-points-to-Christ` (Abraham-Isaac = similitude, v5) В· `reconcile-through-the-atonement` (v11)
- image: `rejected-cornerstone` (the Stone they reject = only sure foundation, v15-17 вЂ” cliffhanger в†’ Jacob 5)

### from Jacob 5 (Zenos's allegory of the olive tree)
- person: `zenos` (quoted prophet) В· `lord-of-the-vineyard` (the weeping, laboring God) В· `the-servants` (prophets/laborers, few) В· `natural-branches` (scattered Israel) В· `wild-branches` (Gentiles)
- parable: `olive-tree-scatter-and-gather` (Israel's whole history as one gardener's seasons; Rom 11)
- image: `the-vinedresser-wept` (Isaiah 5:4's question now with tears, v41) В· `hand-stretched-out-all-the-day-long` (v47 вЂ” the LABORING hand: 3rd/warmest sense of the refrain)
- doctrine: `it-grieveth-me-to-lose-this-tree` (Г—5: vv7,11,13,46,47) В· `labor-WITH-me-joy-WITH-me` (God digs alongside; joy shared, vv71-75)
- study: `jacob5_allegory-of-the-olive-tree` (spin-off DONE вЂ” **FOUR visits** = scattering/meridian/apostasy/restoration [D&C 43:28 "last time"]; **the root never corrupts** v36 "roots are good"; apostasy = overgrowth v48 "taking strength unto themselves"; "grieveth me" sustained Г—7)
- answer: resolves Jacob 4:17 (the rejected stone grafts back in the last labor)

### from Jacob 6 (application of the allegory)
- doctrine: `outstretched-hand-is-mercy` (the allegory's laboring hand 5:47 named: mercy to a gainsaying people, v4 вЂ” refrain resolves; Isa 65:2/Rom 10:21) В· `cleave-as-he-cleaves` (he's already cleaving; answer it, v5) В· `today-harden-not` ("why will ye die?", v6) В· `strait-gate-restated` (enter + continue, v11 = 2 Ne 31)
- warning: `mock-the-plan-of-redemption` (denyв†’quenchв†’mock, v7-8)
- image: `pleasing-bar-dreadful-bar` (same bar: pleasing to righteous, dread to wicked, v13 вЂ” judgment by response; cf 18:14 stone)

### from Jacob 7 (Sherem вЂ” closes Jacob)
- person: `sherem` (first named anti-Christ; learned, flattering, sign-seeker; deathbed confessor) В· `enos` (receives the plates)
- template: `anti-christ` (learned + flatter + deny Christ + "no man knows the future" + demand a sign вЂ” pattern Korihor/Nehor follow)
- doctrine: `witness-outlasts-rhetoric` ("I could not be shaken" вЂ” seen angels + heard the Lord, v4-5) В· `sign-refused-then-given` (won't tempt God; submits "thy will be done", v14) В· `lied-unto-God` (denial of KNOWN truth = the fearful sin, v19) В· `scriptures-testify-of-Christ` (v11)
- image: `deceiver-becomes-witness` (Sherem confesses the three he denied, v17-19) В· `wanderers-mourned-out-our-days` ("adieu" = Г  Dieu, v26-27)
- SYNTHESIS: **JACOB COMPLETE** вЂ” plainness against deception (glory in plainness в†’ lose it by looking beyond the mark в†’ Sherem weaponizes eloquence в†’ witness + mercy answer); opens watchman's burden в†’ closes "adieu, to God"

## вЂ” OMNI вЂ” (1-chapter book, 5 writers, COMPLETE вЂ” small plates END)

### from Omni 1

- doctrine: `offer-your-whole-souls` (the complete offering, v26) В· `good-comes-from-the-Lord` (discernment criterion, v25) В· `prosperity-covenant-negative` (NOT keep в†’ NOT prosper, v6)

## вЂ” MOSIAH вЂ” (Mormon's abridgment begins)

### from Mosiah 1

- doctrine: `record-prevents-dwindling` (without it, even our fathers would have dwindled like the Lamanites, v5 вЂ” Omni's Mulekite lesson stated outright) В· `search-diligently-to-profit` (having в‰  enough; the profit is in searching, v7) В· `name-not-blotted-out-except-by-transgression` (covenant identity, v11-13 в†’ Mosiah 5) В· `conditional-preservation` (transgress в†’ preserving power withdrawn, v13)
- relics: `four-of-the-kingdom` (brass plates + plates of Nephi + sword of Laban + Liahona = word/defense/guidance, v16) В· `liahona-heed-and-diligence` (v16-17)

### from Mosiah 2 (Benjamin's sermon: service + indebtedness)

- thread: `watchmans-burden` (rid my garments of your blood, v27-28 в†ђ Jacob 1:19)

### from Mosiah 3 (the angel's Christology + the natural man)
- person: `the-angel` В· `Lord-Omnipotent`/`Jesus-Christ` (Son + Father + Creator) В· `Mary` (named) В· `the-natural-man` (enemy в†’ saint в†’ child) В· `little-children` (saved)
- doctrine: `natural-man-yields-becomes-a-child` (v19 вЂ” surrender not achievement; saint THROUGH the Atonement; the walk's yield/give-away thread) В· `blood-from-every-pore` (Gethsemane ~124 BC, v7) В· `Christ-named-Son-and-Father-Mary` (fullest pre-Christian naming, v8 вЂ” condescension Christology) В· `no-other-name` (v17) В· `justice-calibrated-to-knowledge` (ignorant covered, knowing rebel not, v11-12) В· `little-children-saved` (v16) В· `law-insufficient-without-atonement` (v15)

### from Mosiah 4 (are we not all beggars / retaining a remission)
- person: `king-Benjamin` В· `the-people` (fallen, begging, remitted) В· `the-beggar` (mirror of the giver) В· `the-poor-who-cannot-give` (guiltless by intent) В· `God` (the Being all depend on)
- doctrine: `are-we-not-all-beggars` (v19 вЂ” charity grounded in the giver's own beggary before God; the beggar is you at God's door) В· `retain-a-remission-by-extending-it` (vv12,26 вЂ” kept day to day by humility + imparting to the poor; mercy kept by mercy extended; grace a current not a deposit) В· `run-not-faster-than-strength` (v27 вЂ” wisdom and order, diligent yet paced; **the workspace covenant pacing verse**) В· `the-poors-willingness-counts` (vv24-25 вЂ” "I would give if I had" в†’ guiltless; disposition weighed not amount) В· `belief-that-does` (v10) В· `substance-belongs-to-God` (v22)

### from Mosiah 5 (the mighty change / the name written in the heart)
- person: `king-Benjamin` (asks, names, seals the covenant) В· `the-people` (changed, covenanting, begotten, named) В· `Christ`/`Lord-God-Omnipotent` (the head, begetter, Master, sealer) В· `the-master`+`the-servant` (v13 figure) В· `the-stranger` (the unserved master's would-be servant)
- doctrine: `mighty-change-disposition-reoriented` (v2 вЂ” "no more disposition to do evil"; the change is its own witness) В· `spiritually-begotten-children-of-Christ` (v7 вЂ” born of him; Christ becomes their father) В· `take-upon-you-the-name-of-Christ` (v8 вЂ” no other name/head) В· `name-written-retained-or-blotted-out` (vv11-12 вЂ” kept in the heart by covenant; lost only by transgression) В· `know-the-master-by-serving-him` (v13 вЂ” inverse of "I never knew you") В· `steadfast-and-immovable-sealed-his` (v15) В· thread: `retain-what-is-given` (binds ch 4+5)

### from Mosiah 6 (the covenant recorded / servant-king passed on)
- person: `king-Benjamin` (records names, consecrates Mosiah, dies) В· `the-people` (covenanted, named, dismissed) В· `Mosiah` (son, consecrated king, servant-king like his father) В· `the-appointed-priests` (teachers / rememberers-keepers)
- practice: `covenant-recorded` (vv1-2 вЂ” heart-change institutionalized into a roster; the name in the heart also written down) В· `teachers-stir-up-remembrance` (v3 вЂ” even the changed need teachers to keep the oath remembered; the retain-thread built into the institution) В· `servant-king-tills-own-earth` (vv6-7 вЂ” Mosiah reproduces Benjamin's labor; righteous govt a transmissible pattern) В· event: `Benjamin-hands-off-and-dies` (a generation closes; chs 2-6 one man's farewell)

## вЂ” ZENIFF RECORD (the embedded back-fill, Mosiah 7-22) вЂ”

### from Mosiah 7 (the lost colony found / bondage as covenant-in-reverse)
- person: `king-Mosiah` (sends the expedition) В· `Ammon` (descendant of Zarahemla, leader of the 16) + `Amaleki`/`Helem`/`Hem` В· `king-Limhi` (son of Noah, son of Zeniff; in bondage) В· `the-people-of-Limhi` (taxed, mourning) В· `the-Lamanites` (oppressors) В· `Zeniff` (over-zealous founder, deceived) В· `king-Laman` (the deceiver) В· `the-unnamed-slain-prophet` (= Abinadi, v26 в†’ 17:20)
- place: `Zarahemla` В· `land/city-of-Lehi-Nephi` В· `Shilom` В· `hill-north-of-Shilom` В· `temple-of-Limhi`
- doctrine: `bondage-as-covenant-in-reverse` (vv20,25,29 вЂ” sin в†’ bondage; God withholds succor) В· `sow-filthiness-reap-the-whirlwind` (vv30-31) В· `exodus-as-grammar-of-hope` (v19) В· `turn-plus-effectual-struggle-on-Gods-timetable` (vv18,33) В· `Christ-the-God-come-down-in-flesh` (v27 вЂ” Abinadi's Christology previewed; image of God) В· event: `prophet-slain-for-testifying-of-Christ` (vv26-28)
- structure: `embedded-record-read-end-first` (Mormon splices the colony's story in; Limhi in chains seen BEFORE Zeniff's optimism в†’ dramatic irony over 9-22)

### from Mosiah 8 (a seer is greater than a prophet / the 24 plates)
- person: `Ammon` (rehearses history + Benjamin's words; expounds seership) В· `king-Limhi` (questioner; rejoices then laments) В· `the-43-man-search-party` (diligent but lost; found the ruins) В· `king-Mosiah` (the seer who can translate) В· `the-destroyed-people` (Jaredites, "numerous as the hosts of Israel")
- object: `the-24-gold-plates` (= the Jaredite record в†’ Ether) В· `the-breastplates` В· `the-rusted-swords` В· `the-interpreters` (Urim and Thummim)
- doctrine: `seer-greater-than-prophet` (vv15-17 вЂ” revelator + prophet + seer; gift just short of God's power) В· `God-provides-the-means-of-revelation` (vv13,18-19) В· `interpreters-guarded-by-commandment` (v13 вЂ” commanded or perish) В· `wisdom-refused-not-unavailable` (v20 вЂ” Lady Wisdom they won't be ruled by; the root beneath ch 7's bondage) В· image: `wild-flock-fleeing-the-shepherd` (v21) В· textual: `24-plates-origin-of-Ether` (vv8-12 вЂ” sought to know "the cause of their destruction")

### from Mosiah 9 (the Record of Zeniff begins вЂ” zeal without wisdom)
- person: `Zeniff` (good but over-zealous founder; first-person narrator; buries the dead) В· `the-austere-blood-thirsty-ruler` (first expedition) В· `Zeniff's-people` (build, prosper, warred upon) В· `king-Laman` (the patient deceiver) В· `the-Lamanites` (lazy, idolatrous, glut on others' labor)
- place: `land-of-Nephi/Lehi-Nephi` В· `Shilom` В· `the-wilderness` В· `place-where-first-army-was-slain`
- theme: `zeal-without-wisdom` (vv1-3 вЂ” self-named "over-zealous"; the negative case of Mosiah 4:27) В· `patient-predator-bondage-as-parasitism` (vv10-12 вЂ” Laman's bait; the lazy glut on others' labor) В· `slow-to-remember-awakened-by-affliction` (vv3,17) В· doctrine: `in-the-strength-of-the-Lord` (vv16-18 вЂ” 3,043 to 279) В· pattern: `leader-shares-labor-and-grief` (v19 вЂ” Zeniff buries the dead)

### from Mosiah 10 (the eternal hatred / grievance tradition)
- person: `Zeniff` (closes his record; even-handed narrator; confers the kingdom) В· `king-Laman` (died) В· `the-new-Lamanite-king` (Laman's son) В· `the-Lamanites` (wild, grievance-bound) В· `Nephi`+`Laman-&-Lemuel` (originating generation, recalled) В· `Noah` (the unnamed son who receives the kingdom)
- theme: `grievance-real-events-false-reading` (vv12-16 вЂ” facts true, interpretation false; **spin-off: mos10_lamanite-grievance-tradition**) В· `understood-not-the-dealings-of-the-Lord` (v14 вЂ” God's favor on faithfulness read as injustice) В· `hatred-taught-to-children-becomes-eternal` (v17) В· doctrine: `strength-of-the-Lord-vs-arm-of-flesh` (vv10-11) В· practice: `hear-the-enemys-case-fairly` (vv12-16) В· event: `good-father-confers-kingdom-on-Noah` (v22 вЂ” the hinge into ch 7's bondage)

### from Mosiah 11 (king Noah the anti-Benjamin / Abinadi's first prophecy)
- person: `king-Noah` (anti-Benjamin; riotous, wine-bibbing, heart on riches) В· `the-new-wicked-priests` (gold seats, flattery, lies) В· `Noah's-people` (taxed, flattered into idolatry, prideful, bloodthirsty) В· `Abinadi` (first appearance вЂ” prophet of conditional bondage) В· `the-Lamanites` (raiders)
- place: `the-palace+throne` В· `the-ornamented-temple` В· `the-gold-high-priest-seats+breastwork` В· `the-high-tower` В· `Shemlon`
- theme: `Noah-the-anti-Benjamin` (vv1-6 вЂ” wicked vs righteous monarchy, paired on purpose в†’ seed of abolishing kings ch 29) В· image: `gold-seats-and-breastwork-for-lies` (v11 вЂ” where Alma will be converted ch 12) В· `flattery-the-engine-of-corruption` (v7) В· `prides-boast-becoming-the-enemy` (v19 в†” 10:11) В· doctrine: `conditional-bondage-except-they-repent` (vv20-25 вЂ” chosen not fated; "slow to hear" fulfilled ch 21) В· `who-is-the-Lord-Pharaoh-echo` (v27) В· `prophet-reframed-as-troublemaker` (v28)

### from Mosiah 12 (Abinadi on trial вЂ” the prisoner tries the court)
- person: `Abinadi` (returns in disguise; the prisoner who tries the court) В· `king-Noah` (judge; death by fire now prophesied) В· `the-wicked-priests` (cross-examiners; false-prosperity preachers; neither keep nor teach) В· `the-Isaiah-quoting-priest` (trap-setter) В· `the-people` (accusers)
- text: `the-harder-prophecy` (detailed doom, fulfilled chs 19,21) В· `Isaiah-52:7-10` (the deferred test в†’ ch 15) В· `the-Decalogue` (begun)
- theme: `prisoner-tries-the-court` (vv19,25-27) В· structure: `deferred-answer-Isaiah-52` (vv20-24 в†’ 15:14-18; why 13-15 is one argument) В· `ye-know-that-I-speak-the-truth` (v30 вЂ” suppression not ignorance) В· `false-prosperity-gospel` (v15) В· `teachers-who-neither-keep-nor-teach` (vv28-37) В· doctrine: `law-cannot-save-by-itself` (vv31-33 в†’ 13:27-32) В· `record-as-witness-against-abomination` (v8)

### from Mosiah 13 (the shield + the law that cannot save)  [spin-off RUNNING: mos13-16_abinadi-christology]
- person: `Abinadi` (shielded, shining-faced; names his death a type) В· `king-Noah` (failed kill-order) В· `the-wicked-priests` (cannot touch him) В· `Moses` (shining-face precedent; prophet of the Messiah) В· `all-the-prophets` (unified witness)
- doctrine: `messenger-shielded-until-the-message-is-out` (vv3-9 вЂ” protection instrumental + bounded; Dan 3 courage) В· `martyrdom-as-type-and-shadow` (v10) В· `salvation-not-by-the-law-alone` (vv27-28 вЂ” only the Atonement "God himself shall make"; **the discourse thesis**) В· `law-as-remembrance-for-the-stiffnecked` (vv29-30 вЂ” pedagogy not redemption; "slow to remember" = 9:3,6:3) В· `law-as-types-of-things-to-come` (vv31-32) В· `all-prophets-testify-of-the-condescending-suffering-God` (vv33-35 вЂ” track for Isaiah 53)

### from Mosiah 14 (Isaiah 53 quoted entire вЂ” the suffering servant)
- person: `Isaiah` (quoted) В· `the-suffering-servant`/`Messiah` (despised, wounded, slain, intercessor, seed-gaining) В· `all-we` (strayed sheep) В· `Abinadi` (plants + will expound the text) В· `Noah's-priests` (courtroom audience)
- doctrine: `vicarious-substitution-the-servant` (vv4-6 вЂ” our transgressions, his stripes) В· `offering-that-gains-seed` (vv10-12 вЂ” the death is fruitful в†’ 15:10-13) В· image: `lamb-led-silent-to-the-slaughter` (v7) В· structure: `Abinadi-answers-glory-text-with-suffering-text` (Isa 52 в†” Isa 53; one Messiah two faces) В· `who-shall-declare-his-generation` (vv8,10 в†’ 15:10-13) В· pattern: `Isaiah-53-variants-broaden-the-atonement` (vv6,8,9,12 вЂ” sins pluralized, innocence generalized; God-ward tilt = atonement-chapter analogue of 2 Ne judgment-chapter mercy-tilt)

### from Mosiah 15 (the doctrinal peak вЂ” Father and Son, the seed, the trap closed)
- person: `Abinadi` (expositor) В· `Christ`/`God-himself` (Father AND Son, Mediator, founder of peace, seed-gaining Redeemer) В· `the-seed` (prophets + all who believe) В· `the-watchmen` (Isa 52) В· `the-willful-knowing-rebels` (excluded) В· `little-children`+`the-ignorant-dead` (included)
- doctrine: `Christ-Father-and-Son-condescension` (vv1-7 вЂ” Son by flesh, Father by conception + as Creator; one God by the will of the Son swallowed up in the Father; **discourse peak**) В· `Mediator-betwixt-man-and-justice` (vv8-9 вЂ” mercy pays justice) В· `atonement-makes-a-family-his-seed` (vv10-13 вЂ” Isa 53:10 answered; new-birth thread в†’ 5:7) В· structure: `Isaiah-52-trap-closed` (vv14-18,29-31 вЂ” the Lord is the beautiful-feet bringer; finishes the half-quoted passage) В· `without-redemption-all-perish` (v19) В· `first-resurrection-wide-reach` (vv20-25 вЂ” ignorant dead + little children) В· `mercy-wide-justice-exact-willful-rebel-excluded` (vv26-27 вЂ” 3:11-12 calibration)

### from Mosiah 16 (Abinadi's close вЂ” the arms of mercy extended)
- person: `Abinadi` (closes the discourse; commissions his killers) В· `Christ` (redemption, light and life, the very Eternal Father) В· `the-old-serpent` (cause of the Fall) В· `all-mankind` (lost, redeemed) В· `the-wicked/carnal-man` (refuses the extended arms) В· `Noah's-priests` (commissioned; Alma listening)
- doctrine: `redemption-universal-in-reach-conditional-in-benefit` (vv4-5 вЂ” "as though there was no redemption made"; **chapter pivot**) В· theme: `arms-of-mercy-extended-and-they-would-not` (v12 вЂ” damnation self-authored against outstretched mercy) В· `all-confess-his-judgments-are-just` (v1) В· `carnal-sensual-devilish-the-fall` (v3) В· `resurrection-swallows-the-sting-of-death` (vv7-10) В· `bar-of-God-judgment-by-works-two-resurrections` (vv10-11) В· commission: `teach-the-law-as-shadow-teach-Christ` (vv14-15 вЂ” dies handing them the work; Alma listening)

### from Mosiah 17 (Abinadi's martyrdom вЂ” one listener believed)
- person: `Abinadi` (refuses to recant; burned; seals his testimony) В· `Alma` (the ONE convert; pleads, flees, writes the words in hiding вЂ” the survival chain) В· `king-Noah` (offers the recantation deal; fears but yields) В· `the-wicked-priests` (reframe doctrine as sedition) В· `Noah's/priests'-seed` (future fire-persecutors, Alma 25) В· `the-Ammonihah-believers` (future fire-martyrs)
- theme: `one-convert-preserves-everything` (vv2-4 вЂ” only Alma believed в†’ the church; Abinadi's seed vs Noah's seed) В· `recantation-refused-words-are-true` (vv8-10) В· `doctrine-reframed-as-sedition` (vv11-12 вЂ” "he reviled the king"; truth punished as treason, the maneuver that killed Christ) В· doctrine: `martyrdom-seals-the-testimony` (vv10,20 вЂ” Heb 9:16-17) В· prophecy: `dying-curse-fulfilled-to-the-letter` (vv15-18 в†’ Alma 25, Mosiah 19) В· type: `martyr-prophet-as-type-of-Christ` (13:10 completed)

### from Mosiah 18 (the Waters of Mormon вЂ” the church founded)
- person: `Alma` (repentant priest of Noah в†’ founder; teaches, baptizes, ordains, leads the flight) В· `Helam` (first baptized) В· `the-believers` (204 baptized в†’ 450 fleeing; the church of Christ) В· `the-ordained-priests` (one per fifty; self-supporting) В· `king-Noah` (criminalizes the church)
- place: `Mormon` (fountain of pure water, thicket/forest, borders of the land)
- covenant: `baptism-bear-one-anothers-burdens` (vv8-10 вЂ” mostly horizontal; the community IS the covenant; **most-quoted BoM covenant**) В· theme: `church-founded-by-a-repentant-insider` (v1) В· `church-born-in-hiding-and-hunted` (vv4-5,30-34) В· `anti-Noah-church-order` (vv19-27 вЂ” self-supporting priests, no priestcraft) В· doctrine: `baptism-covenant-witness-Spirit-poured-out` (vv10-14) В· practice: `consecration-in-seed-proportional-giving` (vv27-29) В· theme: `hearts-knit-one-faith-one-baptism` (v21) В· `worship-criminalized-as-sedition` (v33)

### from Mosiah 19 (Noah's fall вЂ” prophecy comes due)
- person: `king-Noah` (cowardly; abandons families; burned вЂ” prophecy fulfilled) В· `Gideon` (nearly slays Noah; later peace-broker) В· `the-Lamanite-army` (invaders; charmed by the women) В· `the-loyal-men` (stayed to perish with families) В· `the-cowardly-men` (fled, then burned the king) В· `Limhi` (the just son; throne into bondage) В· `Noah's-priests` (flee в†’ the Amulonites)
- theme: `king-concerned-for-self-not-people` (vv7-11 вЂ” anti-servant-king exposed in crisis) В· prophecy: `Noah-burned-fulfilled-to-the-letter` (v20 вЂ” 12:3+13:10+17:18 converge) В· `loyalty-that-would-perish-with-is-rewarded` (vv12-14) В· `just-son-of-a-wicked-father` (vv16-17 вЂ” inverse of Noah) В· structure: `embedded-record-frame-closed` (vv15,26-28 вЂ” back-fill caught up to ch 7) В· thread: `wicked-priests-flee-and-propagate` (v21 в†’ ch 20, Alma 25)

### from Mosiah 20 (the innocent pay for the guilty / Gideon's peace)
- person: `Noah's-fugitive-priests` (abandon families, abduct 24 daughters) В· `the-Lamanite-daughters-of-Shemlon` (abducted) В· `the-Lamanites` (blame the innocent в†’ war в†’ compassion) В· `the-people-of-Limhi` (innocent; fight "like dragons") В· `Limhi` (spares the king, investigates justly) В· `the-wounded-Lamanite-king` (spared; pleads unarmed for Limhi's people) В· `Gideon` (captain; solves the mystery; reads the prophecy; brokers peace)
- theme: `wickedness-compounds-abandonment-to-abduction` (vv3-5) В· `innocent-bear-the-guilty's-sin` (vv6-16) В· `just-response-investigate-not-retaliate` (vv14-16 вЂ” contrast Noah) В· person: `Gideon-wise-counselor-and-prophecy-reader` (vv17-21 вЂ” reads bondage as Abinadi fulfilled) В· theme: `better-bondage-than-death-stop-the-bloodshed` (v22) В· `unarmed-peace-disarms-the-armed` (vv24-26 вЂ” flash-forward to Alma 24) В· `fight-for-wives-and-children-like-dragons` (v11)

### from Mosiah 21 (slow to hear, but hearing вЂ” the burden eased)
- person: `Limhi's-people` (smitten, thrice defeated, humbled, eased) В· `the-widows` (mourning; cared for) В· `the-Lamanites` (oppressors whose hearts God softens) В· `Ammon-and-brethren` (arrive, imprisoned, joyful, decline to baptize) В· `king-Limhi` (covenants; cares for widows) В· `the-lost-search-party` (found Jaredite ruins + ore record)
- doctrine: `God's-slow-yes-burden-eased-before-removed` (v15 вЂ” heard/eased/not-yet-delivered; **pastoral heart of Mosiah**) В· prophecy: `slow-to-hear-fulfilled` (vv3-4,15 в†’ 11:24, 12:2,5) В· theme: `self-deliverance-exhausted-before-humility` (vv6-14 вЂ” 3 rebellions then the dust) В· structure: `deliverance-pair-stratagem-vs-miracle` (Limhi ch22 vs Alma ch24) В· practice: `widow-care-under-bondage` (v17 вЂ” 4:26 in chains) В· `embedded-frame-rejoined` (vv22-28 вЂ” ch7 from inside) В· doctrine: `covenant-made-but-baptism-waits-for-authority` (vv33-35 вЂ” Ammon won't improvise)

### from Mosiah 22 (the escape by stratagem вЂ” Zeniff record ends)
- person: `Ammon` (leads the escape) В· `king-Limhi` (consults the people, hearkens to Gideon) В· `Gideon` (devises the escape вЂ” the deliverer) В· `the-people-of-Limhi` (escape by night with flocks + records) В· `the-drunken-Lamanite-guards` В· `king-Mosiah` (receives the people + both records)
- place: `the-back/secret-pass` В· `Shilom` В· `Zarahemla`
- structure: `deliverance-by-stratagem-completes-the-pair` (vv2-11 вЂ” vs Alma's miracle ch24) В· theme: `bondage's-own-instrument-becomes-the-escape` (vv7,10 вЂ” tribute-wine + drunk guards) В· person: `Gideon-the-deliverer-completes-his-arc` (vv3-9 вЂ” "profitable servant") В· textual: `records-gathered-to-the-seer` (v14 вЂ” Zeniff record + 24 plates в†’ ch28 в†’ Ether) В· principle: `voice-of-the-people-in-seed` (v1 в†’ ch29) В· `Zeniff-record-ends` (9-22 complete)

## вЂ” ALMA'S PEOPLE (chs 23-24) вЂ”

### from Mosiah 23 (Alma refuses the crown / the righteous in bondage)
- person: `Alma` (refuses the crown; repentant former priest; high priest/founder) В· `Alma's-people` (righteous, industrious, in bondage as trial) В· `the-Lamanite-army` (hearts softened) В· `Amulon` (Noah's priest; made king over Alma) В· `the-Lamanite-daughter-wives` (plead for the priests) В· `the-Lamanite-king` (breaks the promise; enthrones Amulon)
- place: `land/city-of-Helam` В· `Amulon`
- doctrine: `esteem-not-one-flesh-above-another` (v7 вЂ” anti-monarchy; Mosiah enacts ch29) В· theme: `refuse-power-knowing-its-corruption-firsthand` (vv9-11 вЂ” "caught in a snare") В· doctrine: `two-bondages-two-liberties-stand-fast` (vv12-14 вЂ” Gal 5:1) В· `the-Lord-chastens-the-righteous` (vv21-24 вЂ” trial not punishment; counterpoint to Limhi) В· theme: `surrender-in-faith-not-rebellion` (vv27-29) В· `love-thy-neighbor-as-the-social-order` (v15) В· `the-wicked-set-to-rule-the-righteous` (vv37-39)

### from Mosiah 24 (the burdens made light / miraculous deliverance)
- person: `Amulon` (persecutor; forbids prayer; wicked priest as task-master) В· `Alma-and-his-people` (enslaved, burdens made light, delivered) В· `king-Laman` В· `the-Lamanite-task-masters` (put to sleep) В· `king-Mosiah` (receives them)
- place: `land-of-Amulon` В· `valley-of-Alma` В· `Zarahemla`
- doctrine: `burdens-made-light-the-bearer-strengthened` (vv14-15 вЂ” **deepest BoM answer to affliction of the faithful**) В· `God-visits-his-people-IN-their-afflictions` (v14 вЂ” answers ch23 chastening) В· `the-prayer-of-the-heart` (vv11-12 вЂ” forbidden voice / poured-out heart) В· structure: `deliverance-pair-completed-Alma-by-miracle` (vv16-21 вЂ” vs Limhi's stratagem) В· theme: `faith-and-patience-draw-the-deliverance` (vv15-17) В· `skill-without-God-makes-cleverer-wickedness` (vv4-7) В· `gratitude-named-into-the-land` (vv20-22)

### from Mosiah 25 (the reunification вЂ” one people from many)
- person: `king-Mosiah` (gathers, reads the records, authorizes Alma) В· `the-Nephites+Mulekites` (merged) В· `Limhi's+Alma's-people` (baptized) В· `the-children-of-Amulon` (reject fathers' name, take Nephi's) В· `Alma` (preaches, baptizes, organizes seven churches) В· `the-Lamanites` (the outnumbering majority; objects of anguish)
- theme: `one-people-from-many-the-covenant-minority` (vv1-13) В· `records-read-form-a-people` (vv5-11 вЂ” purpose of record-keeping realized) В· `anguish-for-the-souls-of-the-lost` (v11 вЂ” seed of the missionary effort) В· `identity-by-choice-not-blood` (v12 вЂ” inverse of inherited grievance 10:17) В· doctrine: `baptism-that-waited-for-authority` (vv17-18 вЂ” ch21 patience rewarded) В· structure: `many-churches-one-church` (vv19-24) В· `king-and-prophet-distinguished` (vv14,19 вЂ” opposite of Noah; prepares reign of judges)

### from Mosiah 26 (as often as my people repent вЂ” discipline + forgiveness)
- person: `the-rising-generation` (unbelievers; uninheriting the faith) В· `the-dissenters` (flatterers eroding the church) В· `the-sinning-church-members` В· `Alma` (high priest; troubled; inquires; given eternal life) В· `king-Mosiah` (gave Alma authority; refuses to judge the church) В· `the-Lord` (reveals forgiveness + discipline)
- theme: `founding-experience-uninheritable` (vv1-4 вЂ” generational unbelief; faith not transmitted) В· `leader-inquires-rather-than-presumes` (vv9-19 вЂ” blessed FOR asking) В· doctrine: `faith-in-the-words-alone` (vv15-16 вЂ” Alma believed Abinadi with no sign) В· `forgiveness-without-a-ceiling` (v30 вЂ” "as often as"; **doctrinal heart**) В· `forgive-or-be-condemned` (v31 вЂ” D&C 64:10) В· `hear-my-voice-or-would-not-be-redeemed` (vv21-28 вЂ” "I never knew you") В· practice: `church-discipline-aimed-at-repentance` (vv32-36 вЂ” names blotted out, door held open) В· doctrine: `covenant-of-eternal-life-to-Alma` (v20 вЂ” BoM's first)

### from Mosiah 27 (Alma the younger born of God вЂ” the Damascus road)
- person: `king-Mosiah` (forbids persecution, commands equality) В· `Alma-the-younger` (wicked persecutor в†’ born of God в†’ witness) В· `the-four-sons-of-Mosiah` (Ammon, Aaron, Omner, Himni вЂ” co-converted, future Lamanite missionaries) В· `the-angel` (interrupter) В· `Alma-the-elder` (the praying father)
- doctrine: `Damascus-road-conversion-of-Alma` (vv11-16 вЂ” BoM's Paul; "why persecutest thou?") В· `a-fathers-prayers-answered-agency-preserved` (v14,16) В· `church-overthrown-only-by-its-own-transgression` (v13) В· `born-again-universal-and-necessary` (vv24-26 вЂ” new-birth thread clearest) В· theme: `before-and-after-of-redemption-snatched` (vv28-29 вЂ” abyssв†’light) В· doctrine: `every-knee-bow-every-tongue-confess` (v31) В· theme: `persecutors-become-publishers-of-peace` (vv35-37 вЂ” Isa 52:7/Abinadi 15 fulfilled; Abinadi arc closes)

### from Mosiah 28 (the mission launches / Jaredite translation / records to Alma)
- person: `the-four-sons-of-Mosiah` (beg to preach; vilest sinners в†’ missionaries; refuse the throne) В· `king-Mosiah` (inquires; translates Jaredite plates; confers records) В· `the-Lamanites` (people of the grievance, target) В· `Alma-the-younger` (receives records + interpreters) В· `the-destroyed-Jaredites` (record translated)
- object: `the-24-gold-plates` (в†’ Ether) В· `the-two-interpreter-stones` (Urim and Thummim) В· `the-brass-plates+plates-of-Nephi`
- event: `mission-to-heal-the-grievance-launches` (vv1-2 вЂ” convince of fathers' iniquity, cure the hatred; **mos10 spin-off cure begins**) В· doctrine: `could-not-bear-that-any-soul-perish` (v3 вЂ” worth of souls) В· theme: `vilest-sinners-become-most-zealous-missionaries` (v4) В· doctrine: `leadership-by-inquiry-and-deliverance-promise` (vv6-7 вЂ” governs Alma 17-26) В· textual: `Jaredite-plates-translated-origin-of-Ether` (vv11-19) В· `seer-doctrine-confirmed` (v16) В· structure: `no-heir-and-records-to-the-prophetic-line` (vv10,20 вЂ” forces reign of judges)

### from Mosiah 29 (the abolition of kings вЂ” book of Mosiah CLOSES)
- person: `king-Mosiah` (dissolves the monarchy; gives the kingdom away; dies) В· `the-sons-of-Mosiah` (declined the throne) В· `the-people` (relinquish the king; cast their voices) В· `Alma-the-younger` (first chief judge + high priest) В· `Alma-the-elder` (founder; dies) В· `king-Noah` (the case study)
- doctrine: `design-government-for-the-worst-case` (vv12-16 вЂ” "because all men are not just"; the Noah arc's payoff) В· theme: `one-wicked-king-and-the-irremovable-tyrant` (vv17-23) В· doctrine: `voice-of-the-people-and-its-caveat` (vv25-27 вЂ” only as safe as the people are righteous) В· `accountability-shifted-from-king-to-people` (vv30-34) В· structure: `checks-and-balances` (vv28-29) В· theme: `king-who-surrenders-power-is-loved-more` (v40 вЂ” servant-king culminated) В· event: `reign-of-judges-begins-book-ends` (vv42-47 вЂ” 509 yrs from Lehi)

## вЂ” ALMA (the reign of judges; longest book, 63 ch) вЂ”

### from Alma 1 (Nehor + priestcraft вЂ” the new order's first test)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (chief judge + high priest; first capital judgment) В· `Nehor` (priestcraft's introducer; anti-Christ; slays Gideon; executed) В· `Gideon` (aged deliverer, murdered for withstanding priestcraft) В· `the-church-members` (persecuted; some proud, some steadfast) В· `the-non-members` (persecutors)
- theme: `priestcraft-the-first-internal-threat` (vv3-12 вЂ” paid+popular clergy + universal-salvation-without-accountability; anti-Christ template Sheremв†’Nehorв†’Korihor) В· doctrine: `law-punishes-acts-not-belief` (vv12,17-18 вЂ” religious liberty + rule of law; tested again Korihor 30) В· `universal-salvation-without-accountability-is-false` (v4) В· `true-order-vs-priestcraft` (vv26-27 вЂ” laboring equal priesthood vs paid elevated) В· `prosperity-without-the-heart-set-on-riches` (vv29-31 вЂ” Jacob 2 distinction) В· event: `Gideon-slain-by-the-first-priestcraft` (vv7-9)

### from Alma 2 (Amlici вЂ” the voice of the people tested)
- person: `Amlici` (Nehor-follower; rejected by the voice, made king by his faction, slain by Alma) В· `the-Amlicites` (the faction; ally with Lamanites; mark themselves ch 3) В· `Alma-the-younger` (chief judge/governor/warrior) В· `the-Lamanites` (allied) В· `the-spies` (Zeram, Amnor, Manti, Limher)
- place: `hill-Amnihu` В· `river-Sidon` В· `valley-of-Gideon` В· `land-of-Minon` В· `wilderness-Hermounts`
- doctrine: `voice-of-the-people-works-but-not-self-enforcing` (vv3-10) В· theme: `heresy-becomes-insurrection` (v1 вЂ” Nehorв†’Amlici) В· `dissent-allies-with-the-enemy` (vv24-25) В· `warrior-prophet-asks-only-to-serve` (vv16,30) В· doctrine: `strengthened-by-the-Lord-after-prayer` (vv18,28,31) В· theme: `cost-of-one-mans-pride` (v19 вЂ” ~19,000 slain)

### from Alma 3 (the Amlicite mark вЂ” the curse self-authored) [BIN-4: logged for Michael, not resolved]
- person: `the-Amlicites` (Nephites by descent; mark themselves; cursed by rebellion) В· `the-Lamanites` (inherited mark from Laman & Lemuel) В· `the-Nephites` (defined by belief in the true records, not blood) В· `Alma` (wounded; sends the army)
- doctrine: `every-man-that-is-cursed-brings-it-on-himself` (v19 вЂ” chapter's thesis; **bin-4 datapoint for 2 Ne 5:21 study**) В· theme: `the-mark-is-self-imposed-and-allegiance-based` (vv4,11,13 вЂ” Nephites who chose rebellion took the mark; belief not blood) В· `mark-to-quarantine-the-destroying-tradition` (v8 вЂ” ties to grievance study) В· doctrine: `curse-conditional-removable-on-repentance` (v14 в†’ 2 Ne 30:6) В· `wages-of-the-spirit-one-obeys` (vv26-27)

### from Alma 4 (the pride cycle / Alma trades the gavel for pure testimony)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (lays down the judgment-seat to preach; keeps high priesthood) В· `Nephihah` (wise elder made chief judge by the voice of the people) В· `the-proud-church-members` (riches, costly apparel, scorn) В· `the-humble-remnant` (impart to the poor, retain a remission) В· `the-unbelievers` (stumbled by the church's hypocrisy)
- theme: `church-out-prides-the-world-stops-the-gospel` (vv9-11 вЂ” hypocrisy as stumbling-block) В· `split-community-closed-hands-vs-open-hands` (vv12-14) В· doctrine: `retaining-a-remission-by-imparting-to-the-poor` (v14 вЂ” Benjamin's phrase) В· event: `Alma-trades-the-gavel-for-pure-testimony` (vv15-20 вЂ” the great pivot) В· doctrine: `pure-testimony-the-remedy-for-pride` (v19 вЂ” word over law; sets up the great sermons) В· theme: `pride-cycle-affliction-to-pride` (vv3,6)

### from Alma 5 (the searching-questions sermon)  [spin-off RUNNING: alma5_searching-questions]
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (bears pure testimony by questions; knows "of myself") В· `the-church-at-Zarahemla` (proud, examined) В· `Alma-the-elder`+`the-fathers` (the mighty change, founding deliverance) В· `the-good-shepherd`(Christ)+`the-devil` (two shepherds) В· `the-poor` (turned away by the proud)
- method: `testimony-as-a-mirror-of-questions` (vv14-31 вЂ” pure testimony in purest form) В· doctrine: `can-ye-feel-so-now-the-change-re-verified` (v26 вЂ” faith a pulse not a deposit) В· `image-of-God-in-the-countenance` (vv14,19 вЂ” counterpoint to Alma 3 mark) В· `two-shepherds-two-folds-no-third` (vv37-42) В· `arms-of-mercy-extended-invitation-at-the-center` (vv33-34,62) В· `knowing-of-myself-by-the-Spirit` (vv45-48 вЂ” answer to Mosiah 26 unbelief) В· `command-to-the-church-invitation-to-the-world` (v62)

### from Alma 6 (after the word, the order вЂ” admin bridge)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (ordains, regulates, departs to Gideon) В· `the-repentant` (received) В· `the-unrepentant-prideful` (blotted out) В· `the-unconverted` (prayed + fasted for)
- practice: `word-first-then-order` (vv1-4) В· `church-cleansed-by-response-to-the-sermon` (vv2-3) В· doctrine: `word-liberal-to-all-anti-priestcraft` (v5) В· practice: `fasting-and-prayer-for-the-unconverted` (v6) В· `ordination-by-laying-on-of-hands-the-order-of-God` (vv1,7-8 вЂ” answers ch1 priestcraft in Gideon's valley)

### from Alma 7 (the Gideon sermon вЂ” the empathic atonement)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (preaching to Gideon; models revelatory honesty) В· `the-Gideon-church` (humble, faithful вЂ” counterpoint to Zarahemla) В· `Christ` (born of Mary; empathic + substitutionary Savior) В· `Mary` (the virgin, named)
- doctrine: `empathic-atonement-suffers-to-know-how-to-succor` (vv11-13 вЂ” **completes the Abinadi thread**; the gospel's deepest comfort) В· theme: `revelatory-honesty-I-do-not-know` (v8) В· doctrine: `born-of-Mary-in-the-land-of-Jerusalem` (v10) В· theme: `pure-testimony-adapts-to-the-people` (vv1-6,17-19 вЂ” joy for Gideon vs woe for Zarahemla) В· doctrine: `God-unchangeable-one-eternal-round` (v20) В· `filthy-remains-filthy-unclean-cannot-enter` (v21) В· theme: `faith-hope-charity-and-the-disciples-attributes` (vv23-24)

### from Alma 8 (rejected at Ammonihah / sent back / meets Amulek)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (rejected, sorrowing, sent back, obeys speedily) В· `the-people-of-Ammonihah` (Nehor stronghold; reject both his offices; conspire against liberty) В· `the-angel` (same one from Mosiah 27 вЂ” conversion + recommission) В· `Amulek` (the prepared host; fed Alma; companion) В· place: `Melek` В· `Ammonihah`
- theme: `go-back-the-hardest-obedience` (vv13-18 вЂ” return to the rejecting city) В· `same-angel-conversion-to-recommission` (v15) В· `the-prepared-host-divine-appointment-at-a-meal` (vv19-22 вЂ” Amulek's own vision) В· `hardened-heart-dismisses-every-authority` (vv11-12,17 вЂ” religious + civil) В· `power-withheld-for-Gods-timing` (v31 вЂ” sets up ch 14) В· practice: `wrestling-with-God-in-mighty-prayer` (v10)

### from Alma 9 (the warning sermon вЂ” light is the measure)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (bold warning witness) В· `the-people-of-Ammonihah` (hardened; "who is God?") В· `the-Lamanites` (less culpable by tradition; promised converts; instrument of judgment) В· `Amulek` (the second witness, about to stand)
- doctrine: `light-sinned-against-is-the-measure-of-guilt` (vv15-24 вЂ” favored = more accountable; to whom much given) В· `Lamanites-partial-exculpation-by-tradition` (v16 вЂ” **proof-text for mos10 spin-off**) В· prophecy: `Lamanite-conversion-the-grievance-cure-decreed` (v17 вЂ” ground of the sons of Mosiah's mission) В· theme: `who-is-God-Pharaoh-defiance-and-the-two-witnesses` (vv2,6 вЂ” Deut 17:6 в†’ Amulek) В· `dramatic-irony-destroyed-in-one-day` (v4 в†’ ch 16) В· doctrine: `prosperity-covenant-applied-two-edged` (vv13-18) В· theme: `love-under-the-woe` (v30)

### from Alma 10 (Amulek the second witness / the city's shield)
- person: `Amulek` (reluctant convert; "I knew, yet I would not know"; second witness; of Manasseh's line) В· `the-lawyers-of-Ammonihah` (cunning, gain-seeking) В· `Zeezrom` (foremost accuser в†’ ch 11) В· `the-righteous-remnant` (prayers shield the city)
- theme: `I-knew-yet-I-would-not-know` (vv4-10 вЂ” willful deafness of the comfortable) В· `second-witness-raised-from-within` (vv8-12 вЂ” Deut 17:6) В· doctrine: `prayers-of-the-righteous-shield-the-wicked-city` (vv22-23 вЂ” Sodom; cast them out в†’ judgment falls, ch14в†’16) В· `in-favor-of-your-law-to-your-condemnation` (v26) В· theme: `corrupt-institutions-the-foundation-of-destruction` (vv27,32 вЂ” Nehor's priestcraft in legal form) В· prophecy: `Mosiahs-warning-fulfilled-voice-chooses-iniquity` (v19) В· `Lehi-of-Manasseh-son-of-Joseph` (v3 вЂ” only explicit tribe statement)

### from Alma 11 (the bribe, the resurrection вЂ” Zeezrom trembles)
- person: `Amulek` (exposes the bribe; teaches the resurrection) В· `Zeezrom` (bribes, traps, then begins to tremble) В· `the-lawyers-of-Ammonihah` (manufacture conflict for fees) В· `Christ` (the very Eternal Father; saves from sin) В· object: `the-Nephite-coinage` В· `the-six-onties` (the bribe)
- doctrine: `saved-FROM-sin-not-IN-it` (vv34-37 вЂ” no unclean thing inherits; refutes Nehor) В· theme: `the-bribe-exposes-the-briber` (vv22-25 вЂ” loves lucre more than the God he knows is real) В· `lawyers-manufacture-conflict-for-fees` (v20) В· doctrine: `Son-is-the-very-Eternal-Father-condescension` (vv38-40) В· `universal-resurrection-conditional-salvation` (v41 вЂ” Mosiah 16:5) В· `resurrection-perfect-universal-permanent-with-recollection` (vv42-45 вЂ” bright recollection of guilt) В· event: `Zeezrom-begins-to-tremble` (v46 вЂ” conversion begins)

### from Alma 12 (chains of hell + flaming sword of mercy)  [spin-off RUNNING: alma12-13]
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (expounds beyond Amulek) В· `Zeezrom` (trembling в†’ diligent inquiry; softening spiral) В· `Antionah` (chief ruler, asks of the flaming sword) В· `Adam` (the Fall) В· `the-devil` (the chains, captivity)
- doctrine: `chains-of-hell-self-tightening-spiral` (vv9-11 вЂ” portion of word by heed; hardenв†’know nothingв†’captive; no neutral) В· `flaming-sword-was-mercy-death-as-probation` (vv21-27) В· `probationary-state-time-to-prepare-to-meet-God` (vv24,27) В· `harden-not-your-hearts-enter-into-my-rest` (vv33-37 вЂ” the hinge в†’ ch 13) В· `plan-of-redemption-laid-before-the-Fall` (vv25,30,33) В· event: `Zeezroms-softening-in-real-time` (vv1-8) В· doctrine: `judged-by-thoughts-words-and-works` (v14)

### from Alma 13 (the holy order / foreordination / the rest)  [spin-off RUNNING: alma12-13]
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (pleading preacher) В· `the-high-priests-of-the-holy-order` (called on foreknown faith; sanctified) В· `Melchizedek` (prince of peace; converted wicked Salem) В· `Abraham` (paid tithes) В· `the-angels` (declaring glad tidings)
- doctrine: `foreordination-on-foreknown-faith-not-election` (vv3-5 вЂ” same starting standing; agency-grounded) В· `sanctified-abhor-sin-new-heart-completed` (vv11-12) В· theme: `Melchizedek-converted-a-wicked-city-the-model` (vv17-19 вЂ” Ammonihah will refuse) В· doctrine: `enter-into-the-rest-the-goal-of-the-order` (vv6,12,13,16,29) В· structure: `12-13-discourse-bookended-chains-to-rest` (13:30 в†” 12:11) В· doctrine: `faith-hope-charity-the-path-into-the-rest` (v29) В· theme: `prophet-pleads-with-anxiety-even-unto-pain` (vv25,27)

### from Alma 14 (the martyrdom + the prison rent)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (restrained by the Spirit; gives the answer to suffering; delivered) В· `Amulek` (begs to save the burning) В· `the-burning-believers+children` (martyrs received in glory) В· `Zeezrom` (harrowed up; confesses; cast out) В· `the-chief-judge+Nehor-establishment` (mock, smite, then crushed)
- doctrine: `why-God-permits-the-innocent-to-suffer` (vv10-11 вЂ” glory / full accountability / blood as witness; **the BoM's hardest confrontation**) В· `the-Spirit-constrains-the-prophets-power` (vv10-11) В· `protection-lasts-only-as-long-as-the-work` (v13) В· event: `Zeezrom-harrowed-up-pains-of-hell-as-guilt` (vv6-7) В· theme: `Christic-silence-and-the-cross-echoes` (vv17-24) В· `sign-seeking-mockery-refused` (v24) В· event: `deliverance-after-the-full-measure` (vv24-29 вЂ” prison rent, establishment crushed) В· theme: `scriptures-burned-but-the-word-survives` (v8)

### from Alma 15 (Zeezrom healed вЂ” the Ammonihah arc resolves)
- person: `Zeezrom` (guilt-fevered в†’ healed by faith в†’ baptized в†’ preacher; the complete conversion) В· `Alma-the-younger` (heals Zeezrom; shelters Amulek) В· `Amulek` (forsook all вЂ” wealth, friends, father, kindred) В· `the-cast-out-believers` (at Sidom) В· `the-people-of-Ammonihah` (hardened; ascribe God's power to the devil)
- doctrine: `guilt-as-a-burning-fever-pains-of-hell-bodily` (vv3-5) В· `healed-by-faith-body-and-soul-together` (vv6-11) В· event: `complete-conversion-bribing-lawyer-to-preacher` (vv11-12) В· theme: `hardened-collective-refuses-what-the-individual-receives` (v15 вЂ” anti-Salem) В· `cost-of-discipleship-forsaking-all` (v16 вЂ” Amulek) В· `bear-the-burden-of-the-brother-who-paid-the-cost` (v18)

### from Alma 16 (Desolation of Nehors вЂ” the city destroyed in one day)
- person: `Zoram-chief-captain` (consults Alma, recovers all captives; sons Lehi + Aha вЂ” NOT the 1 Ne Zoram) В· `Alma-the-younger` (inquires of the Lord; gives the battle geography) В· `the-Lamanite-armies` (strike Ammonihah before defense can muster)
- event: `Ammonihah-destroyed-in-one-day` (vv9-11 вЂ” fulfilling the scoff of 9:4) В· place: `Desolation-of-Nehors` (v11 вЂ” land named for the *profession* that killed it) В· theme: `seek-the-prophet-vs-harden-against-him` (vv5-9, the diptych) В· doctrine: `Spirit-poured-out-to-prepare-hearts` (vv16-17 вЂ” inverse of the chains of hell) В· prophecy: `Christ-will-appear-after-his-resurrection` (v20)

## вЂ” SONS OF MOSIAH / LAMANITE MISSION (17-27) вЂ”
*The grievance-tradition CURE in action (the disease was diagnosed in mos10). Ammon в†’ Lamoni в†’ the queen + household; Aaron в†’ the over-king; the Anti-Nephi-Lehies + buried weapons. Deep study: `studies/alma17-26_lamanite-conversion-and-the-grievance-cure.md` (in progress).*

### from Alma 17 (Ammon at the waters of Sebus вЂ” the prince made servant)
- person: `Ammon` (son of Mosiah; refuses Lamoni's daughter, chooses to be a servant; the Sebus deliverance) В· `Lamoni` (king of Ishmael, descendant of Ishmael) В· `the-sons-of-Mosiah` (refused the kingdom; 14-yr mission; scriptures + fasting в†’ spirit of prophecy)
- theme: `the-tradition-is-the-target-not-the-people` (v9 вЂ” grievance-cure thesis) В· `patience-and-example-as-conversion-method` (v11) В· `preparation-precedes-power` (vv2-3) В· event: `Ammon-chooses-to-be-a-servant` (v25 вЂ” power-inversion) В· `waters-of-Sebus` (vv26-39 вЂ” well-deliverance type-scene) В· doctrine: `miracle-in-service-of-relationship-in-service-of-belief` (v29)

### from Alma 18 (Believest thou that there is a God? вЂ” Lamoni converted)
- person: `Ammon` (perceives the king's thoughts; teaches creationв†’redemption; faithful servant of v10) В· `Lamoni` (believes; cries for mercy; falls as if dead)
- theme: `faithful-in-the-ordinary-errand` (v10 вЂ” the Ammon-anchor verse) В· `wise-yet-harmless-holy-guile` (vv22-23) В· `correcting-the-grievance-history-at-the-source` (vv36-38) В· doctrine: `start-where-the-hearer-is` (vv24-28 вЂ” "Great Spirit"в†’"This is God") В· `power-according-to-faith-and-desire` (vv34-35) В· event: `Lamoni-falls-as-if-dead` (vv40-43)

### from Alma 19 (the queen's faith + Abish вЂ” first Lamanite church)
- person: `the-queen-of-Ishmael` (quiet faith "to me he doth not stink"; greatest faith of all the Nephites; testifies of Jesus) В· `Abish` (Lamanite servant, secretly converted years prior by her father's vision; gathers the crowd) В· `Lamoni` (rises: "I have seen my Redeemer"; rebukes contention, teaches)
- theme: `the-outsider-out-believes-the-covenant-people` (v10 вЂ” grievance inverted) В· `the-hidden-disciple-spent-at-the-right-moment` (vv16-29 вЂ” Abish) В· doctrine: `faith-on-testimony-alone` (vv9-10) В· `conversion-as-light-dispelling-darkness` (v6 вЂ” inverse of chains of hell) В· `his-arm-extended-to-all` (v36 вЂ” 5:21 answer) В· event: `Lamoni-rises-having-seen-the-Redeemer` (vv12-13) В· `Sebus-avenger-falls-dead` (vv22-23 вЂ” promise to Mosiah fulfilled)

### from Alma 20 (the road to Middoni вЂ” the over-king disarmed)
- person: `Lamonis-father-the-over-king` (recites the grievance; draws on his son + Ammon; spared, seeded) В· `Ammon` (pleads for the king's soul; refuses the bribe; asks nothing for self) В· `Lamoni` (refuses to enforce the grievance) В· `Aaron-Muloki-Ammah` (imprisoned at Middoni; patient in suffering)
- theme: `the-grievance-at-full-volume` (vv10-13 вЂ” Mosiah 10 by its highest exponent) В· `the-son-refuses-to-enforce-the-grievance` (v15) В· `selfless-terms-disarm-the-grievance` (vv24-26) В· `king-turns-sword-on-his-own-son` (vv14-16 вЂ” Saul/Jonathan) В· `faithfulness-measured-by-the-field-endured-not-the-fruit` (vv29-30 вЂ” Aaron vs Ammon) В· doctrine: `plead-for-the-aggressors-soul-not-just-the-victims-life` (vv17-18) В· event: `over-king-spared-and-seeded` (vv26-27)

### from Alma 21 (Aaron's harder field вЂ” the Amalekite/Amulonite Nehorites)
- person: `Aaron` (preaches the atonement into counterfeit-religious room; mocked; imprisoned; eventually fruitful) В· `the-Amalekites-Amulonites` (Nehorite apostate-dissenters; "still harder") В· `Muloki-Ammah` (Aaron's companions) В· `Lamoni` (refuses Ammon's servanthood; decrees religious freedom)
- theme: `apostates-are-the-hardest-ground` (v3) В· `denying-prophecy-to-immunize-the-present` (v8) В· `preach-the-atonement-plainly-regardless-of-reception` (vv9-10) В· `Spirit-led-mission-go-where-admitted` (vv16-17) В· doctrine: `counterfeit-religion-removes-the-need-to-repent` (v6 вЂ” Nehor's "God saves all men") В· event: `Lamoni-decrees-religious-freedom` (vv19-22)

### from Alma 22 (Aaron + the over-king вЂ” "give away all my sins")
- person: `Lamonis-father-the-over-king` (prepared by Ammon's love; converted; decrees religious freedom kingdom-wide) В· `Aaron` (reproducible conversion template; raises the king; converts the household)
- doctrine: `give-away-not-give-up-and-not-then` (v18 вЂ” Michael's study verse) В· `atonement-creed-could-not-merit-of-himself` (v14) В· theme: `the-conversion-method-is-reproducible` (vv7-23 вЂ” Aaron = Ammon's play) В· `the-seed-of-love-works-in-the-dark` (v3) В· `rich-young-ruler-rewritten` (v15) В· event: `over-king-and-whole-household-converted` (vv22-27) В· reference: `land-division-narrow-neck` (vv27-34 вЂ” Mormon's geography)

### from Alma 23 (Anti-Nephi-Lehies вЂ” never fall away, curse lifted)
- person: `the-converted-over-king` (proclaims protection; goal "all brethren") В· `the-Anti-Nephi-Lehies` (new name; never fall away) В· `the-Amalekites-Amulonites` (converted "save only one"; apostate-hard)
- doctrine: `conversion-that-lays-down-the-weapon-never-falls-away` (vv6-7) В· `the-curse-lifted-as-enmity-and-idleness-reversed` (v18 вЂ” 5:21 datapoint) В· theme: `the-grievance-dissolved-into-all-brethren` (v3) В· `apostates-dont-convert-natives-do` (v14) В· event: `new-name-Anti-Nephi-Lehies` (vv16-17)

### from Alma 24 (the weapons buried deep вЂ” the cure's deepest proof)
- person: `king-Anti-Nephi-Lehi-elder` (the burial speech; sword-logic; dies before the attack) В· `the-Anti-Nephi-Lehies` (bury weapons; 1,005 martyred unresisting) В· `the-attacking-Nehorites` (many convert mid-slaughter; unconverted = Nehorite apostates)
- doctrine: `bury-the-weapons-lest-the-cleansing-not-hold` (vv12-13) В· `martyrdom-is-net-positive` (vv26-27) В· `apostasy-from-light-is-worse-than-never-knowing` (v30 вЂ” capstone) В· theme: `covenant-as-threefold-reversal-of-the-grievance` (v18) В· `buried-weapons-covenant-echoes-forward` (vv17-19 в†’ Hel 15) В· event: `unresisting-martyrdom-converts-the-killers` (vv21-25)

### from Alma 25 (Abinadi's fire fulfilled вЂ” the law read as type)
- person: `seed-of-Amulon` (burn believers, then hunted + slain вЂ” Abinadi's prophecy fulfilled) В· `the-new-Lamanite-converts` (join Anti-Nephi-Lehies, bury weapons, keep the law as type)
- doctrine: `prophecy-fulfilled-as-a-pattern-across-generations` (vv9-12 вЂ” Abinadi Mosiah 13) В· `law-of-moses-as-type-not-salvation` (vv15-16) В· theme: `sin-and-its-judgment-both-have-descendants` (vv4-9) В· `the-cure-spreads-through-the-war` (vv13-14) В· `counterfeit-forms-vs-forms-that-point-to-Christ` (vv15-16 vs 21:6)

### from Alma 26 (Ammon's psalm вЂ” the arc's doxology)
- person: `Ammon` (the psalm; "I am nothing... in his strength I can do all things") В· `Aaron` (the peer rebuke on boasting)
- doctrine: `boast-in-God-not-self-strength-through-nothing` (vv11-12 вЂ” BoM Philip 4:13) В· `chains-of-hell-loosed` (vv14-15 вЂ” Alma 12 reversed) В· `only-the-penitent-knows` (vv21-22) В· `God-mindful-of-every-people` (vv36-37 вЂ” 5:21 datapoint) В· theme: `the-sword-vs-the-saving` (vv24-26) В· `Lamanite-love-exceeds-Nephite-love` (vv33-34) В· event: `Ammon-almost-turned-back` (v27)

### from Alma 27 (the people of Ammon вЂ” arc close, chapters 17-27)
- person: `the-people-of-Ammon` (formerly Anti-Nephi-Lehies; migrate to Jershon; "firm... even unto the end") В· `Ammon` (joy exhausts his strength) В· `the-king-Anti-Nephi-Lehi` (offers his people as slaves in restitution; refused) В· `the-Nephites-voice-of-the-people` (receive former enemies; bear the sword for them)
- theme: `protect-the-pacifist-without-arming-him` (vv5-12) В· `the-armed-bear-the-sword-for-the-unarmed-by-conscience` (vv22-24 вЂ” seeds the stripling warriors) В· `firm-in-the-faith-even-unto-the-end` (v27) В· doctrine: `you-cannot-repay-murder-only-be-received` (vv6-9) В· `joy-proportional-to-repentance` (vv17-18) В· `resurrection-empties-death-of-terror` (v28) В· event: `new-name-the-people-of-Ammon` (v26)

### from Alma 28 (the cost counted вЂ” the two mournings)
- event: `the-tremendous-battle` (vv1-3 вЂ” greatest since Lehi; tens of thousands slain)
- theme: `Mormon-lingers-on-the-cost` (vv4-6 вЂ” the cry of widows) В· `sorrow-and-joy-held-together` (v14) В· `the-call-to-labor-in-the-vineyard` (v14) В· doctrine: `the-two-mournings-fear-vs-hope` (vv11-12) В· `inequality-is-self-made-not-God-imposed` (v13 вЂ” 5:21 thread)

### from Alma 29 (O that I were an angel вЂ” ambition corrected to contentment)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (the soliloquy; holy-ambition-corrected)
- doctrine: `wanting-more-than-your-allotment-is-sin` (vv3-6 вЂ” Mosiah 4:27 from inside) В· `God-grants-according-to-desire` (vv4-5) В· `God-teaches-every-nation-in-its-own-tongue` (v8 вЂ” 5:21-adjacent) В· theme: `scale-ambition-to-one-soul-through-your-calling` (vv6-9) В· `joy-fuller-in-others-success` (vv14-16)

### from Alma 30 (Korihor the anti-Christ)
- person: `Korihor` (anti-Christ; full secular-materialist creed; struck dumb; "I always knew"; trodden down) В· `Alma-the-younger` (refutes by argument first, sign last; discerns willful unbelief) В· `Giddonah` (high priest at Gideon)
- doctrine: `no-law-against-belief-punish-crimes-not-faith` (vv7-11) В· `all-things-denote-there-is-a-God` (v44 вЂ” design argument) В· `argument-before-sign-reason-first` (vv37-47) В· `unbelief-as-chosen-lie-believed-through-success` (vv42, 52-53) В· theme: `the-complete-anti-Christ-creed` (vv13-18) В· `accusation-by-projection-priestcraft` (vv27-35) В· `the-devil-abandons-his-children` (v60)

### from Alma 31 (the Rameumptom вЂ” false worship)
- person: `the-Zoramites-Zoram` (dissenters; Rameumptom worship; deny Christ; elect-by-pride) В· `Alma-the-younger` (heartbroken; prays for strength + the lost) В· place: `Rameumptom` (the high one-man stand)
- theme: `false-worship-as-inversion-of-true` (vv12-23) В· `the-two-prayers-self-vs-others` (vv16-18 vs 30-35) В· doctrine: `election-by-pride-vs-mercy` (vv16-18, 24-25) В· `the-word-more-powerful-than-the-sword` (v5) В· `affliction-swallowed-in-the-joy-of-Christ` (vv36-38)

### from Alma 32 (the seed вЂ” faith as experiment)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (faith sermon; reads the poor's affliction as preparation) В· `the-poor-cast-out` (barred for apparel; humbled, ready)
- doctrine: `faith-is-hope-in-unseen-things-which-are-true` (v21) В· `the-entry-bar-is-only-desire` (v27) В· `the-seed-experiment` (vv28-35 вЂ” discernible light) В· `experimental-knowledge-of-that-thing-not-all` (v34) В· `faith-must-be-nourished-or-it-withers` (vv37-41) В· `compelled-vs-voluntary-humility` (vv13-16) В· theme: `worship-not-confined-to-building-or-week` (vv10-11) В· `the-word-comes-through-the-overlooked` (v23 вЂ” men, women, children)

### from Alma 33 (Zenos, worship everywhere, the brazen serpent)
- person: `Zenos` (lost prophet; worship-everywhere prayer; mercy "because of thy Son") В· `Zenock` (lost prophet; testified of the Son; stoned) В· `Moses-brazen-serpent` (the type raised in the wilderness)
- doctrine: `worship-is-bound-to-no-place` (vv3-11) В· `every-mercy-is-because-of-the-Son` (v11) В· `the-scandal-of-the-simple-look` (vv19-21) В· `the-seed-is-the-word-of-Christ` (vv22-23) В· theme: `burdens-made-light-through-the-joy-of-the-Son` (v23)

### from Alma 34 (Amulek вЂ” infinite atonement, mercy + justice, "this life is the time")
- person: `Amulek` (atonement sermon; personal testimony; hypocrisy rebuke)
- doctrine: `the-atonement-must-be-infinite` (vv9-14) В· `mercy-satisfies-justice-encircles-in-safety` (vv15-16 вЂ” seed of Alma 42) В· `the-law-every-whit-points-to-the-sacrifice` (vv13-14) В· `prayer-without-mercy-to-the-needy-is-hypocrisy` (vv28-29 вЂ” "dross" reversed) В· `this-life-is-the-time-to-prepare` (vv31-33) В· `the-spirit-you-die-with-persists` (vv34-35) В· theme: `prayer-everywhere-over-everything-continually` (vv17-27) В· `dont-let-the-casting-out-make-you-like-them` (vv40-41)

### from Alma 35 (Zoramite block close вЂ” refugees become refuge; pivot to the sons)
- person: `the-Zoramite-leaders` (angry the word destroyed their craft; secret purge) В· `the-people-of-Ammon` (former refugees now shelter cast-out Zoramites) В· `the-new-Zoramite-converts` (expelled; take up arms вЂ” not under the Ammonite oath) В· `Alma-the-younger` (grieved; pivots to his sons)
- theme: `the-word-destroys-craft` (vv3-6) В· `the-sheltered-become-shelterers` (vv8-9) В· `pacifism-was-a-covenant-not-a-blanket-rule` (vv13-14) В· `offended-by-the-strictness-of-the-word` (v15) В· `pivot-from-public-mission-to-private-stewardship` (v16 вЂ” opens 36-42)

## вЂ” ALMA'S COUNSEL TO HIS SONS (36-42) вЂ”
*Each charge given "separately" (35:16): Helaman (36-37), Shiblon (38), Corianton (39-42). The book's most personal block вЂ” fatherhood after the wide field hardened.*

### from Alma 36 (to Helaman вЂ” the conversion told whole, chiastic)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (conversion paradigm; persecutorв†’preacher) В· `Helaman` (the son receiving the charge)
- structure: `chiasmus-centered-on-the-cry` (vv1-30, pivot vv17-18) В· doctrine: `pains-of-hell-are-memory-in-Gods-presence` (vv13-16) В· `a-different-memory-is-the-rescue` (v17) В· `the-cry-stripped-to-the-name-and-mercy` (v18) В· `joy-exactly-as-deep-as-the-pain` (vv20-21) В· `conversion-becomes-vocation` (v24) В· `reproducible-conversion-tasted-eye-to-eye` (v26) В· event: `longing-replaces-the-wish-to-be-banished` (vv15, 22)

### from Alma 37 (to Helaman cont. вЂ” records, small means, the Liahona)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` В· `Helaman` (entrusted with records + interpreters) В· object: `the-sacred-records-Liahona-24-plates`
- doctrine: `by-small-and-simple-things` (vv6-7) В· `scriptures-preserve-memory-and-convert` (vv8-9) В· `teach-the-fruit-of-evil-not-the-recipe` (vv21-32) В· `counsel-with-the-Lord-in-all-thy-doings` (vv35-37) В· `the-Liahona-as-type-of-the-word` (vv38-46) В· theme: `the-failure-is-despising-the-easy-way` (vv41, 46)

### from Alma 38 (to Shiblon вЂ” the steady son)
- person: `Shiblon` (steady, faithful; suffered among the Zoramites; receives approval) В· `Alma-the-younger`
- doctrine: `bridle-passions-that-ye-may-be-filled-with-love` (v12 вЂ” restraint as precondition for love) В· `no-other-way-but-Christ` (v9) В· `conversion-is-pain-until-the-cry-then-peace` (vv6-8) В· theme: `three-sons-three-different-words` (vv2-3) В· `inoculate-the-faithful-son-against-pride` (vv11-14 вЂ” publican vs Rameumptom)

### from Alma 39 (to Corianton вЂ” the grieved father confronts)
- person: `Corianton` (strayed вЂ” boasted, forsook ministry, went after Isabel) В· `Alma-the-younger` (rebuke framed by love) В· `Isabel` (the harlot at Siron)
- doctrine: `the-sin-started-in-pride-not-appetite` (v2) В· `sexual-sin-ranks-third-because-of-the-power-it-misuses` (vv5-6) В· `the-representatives-sin-costs-others-their-belief` (v11) В· `repentance-includes-restitution-and-counsel` (vv10-13) В· theme: `harrowing-the-soul-for-its-good` (vv7-8) В· `rebuild-the-belief-under-the-behavior` (vv15-19 в†’ 40-42)

### from Alma 40 (the resurrection вЂ” answer to the worried son)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (revelation-vs-opinion honesty) В· `Corianton` (worried about the resurrection)
- doctrine: `the-space-and-the-intermediate-state` (vv11-14 вЂ” paradise/rest, outer darkness/fearful-looking-for) В· `the-resurrection-restores-the-perfect-frame` (v23 вЂ” not a hair lost) В· `resurrection-certain-the-floor-under-repentance` (vv4-21) В· `universal-resurrection-divergent-destinies` (vv25-26) В· theme: `prophetic-intellectual-honesty-revelation-vs-opinion` (vv5, 20) В· `resurrection-makes-mortality-matter-forever` (vv21, 26)

### from Alma 41 (the restoration вЂ” "wickedness never was happiness")
- person: `Corianton` (wrested "restoration" into self-justifying universalism) В· `Alma-the-younger`
- doctrine: `wickedness-never-was-happiness` (vv10-11 вЂ” contradictory natures) В· `restoration-is-reciprocity-not-reset` (vv12-13) В· `you-are-restored-to-the-self-your-desires-built` (vv3-7) В· `what-you-send-out-returns` (vv14-15) В· theme: `bad-theology-cleared-the-way-for-bad-behavior` (vv1, 9) В· `the-doctrine-condemns-the-unrepentant-and-saves-the-repentant` (v15)

### from Alma 42 (justice & mercy вЂ” the Corianton block climax)
- person: `Corianton` (denied God's justice to excuse his sin) В· `Alma-the-younger`
- doctrine: `the-expulsion-was-mercy-it-created-the-space-to-repent` (vv2-7) В· `law-punishment-repentance-chain` (vv16-22) В· `God-himself-pays-justice-so-mercy-can-act` (v15) В· `mercy-cannot-rob-justice` (vv23-25) В· `two-kinds-of-trouble-destructive-vs-redemptive` (v29) В· theme: `attacking-Gods-justice-to-excuse-oneself` (vv1, 30) В· `repentance-is-the-start-of-the-real-ministry` (v31)

## вЂ” THE WAR CHAPTERS (43-62) вЂ”
*Captain Moroni; the title of liberty (46); Moroni's character (48); the Amalickiah/Ammoron wars; Helaman's stripling warriors (53, 56-58); the Moroni-Pahoran epistles (60-61). The gospel under siege вЂ” liberty, covenant, and faith tested by war.*

### from Alma 43 (Captain Moroni вЂ” the better cause)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (chief captain at 25; armor, revelation, stratagem, mercy) В· `Zerahemnah` (Lamanite commander; apostate captains preserve hatred) В· `Lehi-captain` (encircling army at Sidon) В· `Alma-the-younger` (consulted for strategy)
- doctrine: `the-better-cause-defensive-not-conquest` (vv45-47) В· `the-law-of-war-bear-the-offense-then-defend` (vv46-47 вЂ” D&C 98) В· theme: `Moroni-prepares-armor-as-a-moral-act` (vv18-21, 37-38) В· `revelation-and-strategy-together` (vv23-24, 30) В· `mercy-in-victory-stop-when-the-threat-is-contained` (v54) В· `dissenters-drive-the-war` (vv6-8)

### from Alma 44 (Zerahemnah surrenders вЂ” conditional protection)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (conditional-protection doctrine; keeps his word; repeated mercy) В· `Zerahemnah` (credits armor not God; refuses then accepts the oath; scalped)
- doctrine: `conditional-protection-faithful-or-fall` (v4) В· theme: `two-readings-of-the-same-victory` (vv3 vs 9 вЂ” providence vs armor) В· `Moronis-word-binds-him` (vv10-11) В· `mercy-with-a-limit-spare-the-person-not-the-threat` (vv6, 11) В· `repeated-mercy-stop-the-killing-when-the-enemy-yields` (v20) В· event: `end-of-Almas-record` (v24)

### from Alma 45 (Alma's prophecy + departure вЂ” Helaman's record begins)
- person: `Alma-the-younger` (final prophecy, blessing, translation-like departure) В· `Helaman` (reaffirms belief; receives records; takes up ministry)
- prophecy: `Nephite-extinction-400-years` (vv10-14) В· event: `Almas-translation-like-departure` (vv18-19 вЂ” "even as Moses") В· doctrine: `the-conditional-land-covenant` (v16) В· theme: `the-prophecy-sealed-until-fulfilled` (v9) В· `the-pride-cycle-reignites-the-moment-deliverance-passes` (vv1, 23-24) В· `Mormon-lives-the-fulfillment-he-records` (vv10-14)

### from Alma 46 (the title of liberty)
- person: `Amalickiah` (the flatterer; cunning + flattering words; bids for kingship) В· `Captain-Moroni` (rends coat into title of liberty; prays before proclaiming) В· object: `the-title-of-liberty` ("our God, our religion, and freedom, and our peace, our wives, and our children")
- doctrine: `the-inner-threat-of-flattery-and-ambition` (vv4-10) В· `the-self-maledictory-covenant-of-liberty` (vv19-22) В· `conditional-protection-destroyed-only-by-our-transgressions` (v18) В· theme: `how-quick-to-forget-after-deliverance` (vv7-8) В· `prayer-before-the-banner` (v13) В· `the-Joseph-remnant-typology-refuses-to-flatter` (vv23-27) В· `the-hard-edge-of-wartime-liberty` (v35) В· event: `Christians-named` (vv14-15)

### from Alma 47 (Amalickiah's treachery вЂ” "come down from the mount")
- person: `Amalickiah` (master of treachery; flatteryв†’commandв†’betrayalв†’poisonв†’murderв†’throne) В· `Lehonti` (lured off the mount, poisoned by degrees) В· `the-Lamanite-king` (trusts the token of peace, stabbed)
- theme: `come-down-from-the-mount` (vv7-13 вЂ” lured off secure ground) В· `poison-by-degrees` (v18) В· `treachery-weaponizes-trust` (vv10-35) В· `accuse-the-innocent-of-your-own-crime` (vv24-30) В· `Amalickiah-as-anti-Moroni` (secrecy/fraud vs transparency/prayer) В· doctrine: `apostate-worse-strange-to-relate` (v36)

### from Alma 48 (the portrait of Moroni)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (fullest character portrait вЂ” greatness of character not capacity) В· `Amalickiah` (power by fraud, the foil) В· `Helaman-the-preachers` ("no less serviceable")
- theme: `greatness-is-character-not-capacity` (v7) В· `the-general-and-the-preacher-are-equals` (vv18-19) В· `the-reluctant-warrior-grieves-the-unprepared-dead` (vv23-24) В· `competence-in-service-of-love-not-the-reverse` (vv11-13) В· doctrine: `if-all-men-were-like-Moroni-hell-would-be-shaken` (v17) В· `the-Nephite-war-faith-defense-never-offense` (vv14-16)

### from Alma 49 (fortified cities tested вЂ” preparation pays off)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (fortifies the weak city most; anticipates enemy's logic) В· `Amalickiah` (curses God + Moroni for the faithfulness that beat him) В· `Lehi-captain` (commands Noah; feared) В· `Corianton` (restored, now preaching)
- theme: `preparation-defeats-numbers-and-is-how-God-works` (vv2-23) В· `anticipate-the-enemys-logic-fortify-the-weak-point-most` (vv14-15) В· `two-responses-to-one-deliverance` (vv27-28) В· `Amalickiah-hates-God-because-faithfulness-works` (v27) В· event: `Corianton-restored-among-the-preachers` (v30)

### from Alma 50 (expansion, prosperity, Morianton)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (fortifies all cities; happiest-time era) В· `Morianton` ("man of much passion"; undone by beating a maidservant) В· `the-maidservant` (abused, exposes the plan, saves the nation) В· `Teancum` (introduced; slays Morianton) В· `Pahoran-Nephihah` (righteous chief judges)
- doctrine: `the-Lehi-covenant-verified-as-historical-law` (vv19-22) В· theme: `the-happiest-time-was-readiness-plus-faithfulness` (v23) В· `private-cruelty-betrays-the-public-scheme` (vv30-31) В· `the-overlooked-person-is-the-hinge` (v31) В· reference: `the-oath-of-good-governance` (vv37-40)

### from Alma 51 (king-men + Amalickiah's death)
- person: `the-king-men` (high-birth faction seeking monarchy; seditious in defeat) В· `the-freemen-Pahoran` (free government by the voice of the people) В· `Captain-Moroni` (crushes internal sedition) В· `Amalickiah` (dies by Teancum's javelin asleep) В· `Teancum` (the night raid)
- theme: `sedition-born-from-factional-spite` (v13) В· `internal-division-opens-the-door-to-conquest` (vv22-27) В· `the-nations-own-fortifications-turned-against-it` (v27) В· `the-hard-edge-of-wartime-sedition-law` (vv15-21) В· `the-pit-digger-falls-into-his-own-pit` (vv9-10, 33-37)

### from Alma 52 (Ammoron + Mulek retaken by decoy)
- person: `Ammoron` (Amalickiah's brother; inherits throne + war) В· `Captain-Moroni` (the decoy; mercy in the trap; wounded) В· `Teancum` (the bait force) В· `Lehi-captain` (the fresh pincer) В· `Jacob-Zoramite` (fights to the death; killed)
- theme: `organized-evil-outlives-its-leader` (vv3-4) В· `dont-fight-on-the-enemys-terms` (vv5, 17) В· `the-decoy-and-the-pincer` (vv21-31 вЂ” ambush of Ai) В· `mercy-maximizes-surrenders-not-kills` (vv37-40) В· `the-dissenters-ferocity-destroys-him` (vv33-40)

### from Alma 53 (the stripling warriors rise)
- person: `the-people-of-Ammon` (covenant-keepers; want to break the oath out of love, restrained) В· `Helaman` (restrains the fathers; leads the 2000 sons) В· `the-two-thousand-stripling-warriors` (sons not under the oath; faithfulness their defining trait) В· `Captain-Moroni-Lehi` (prisoner-wall)
- doctrine: `keeping-the-covenant-while-watching-others-bleed-for-it` (vv13-15) В· `faithfulness-true-in-whatsoever-entrusted-is-the-defining-trait` (vv20-21) В· theme: `the-next-generation-takes-up-what-the-parents-could-not` (vv16-18) В· `internal-dissension-costs-ground-again` (vv8-9) В· `the-captives-build-their-own-prison-wall` (vv4-5)

### from Alma 54 (Moroni-Ammoron letters)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (letter grounded in God/justice/repentance + honest anger) В· `Ammoron` (letter grounded in grievance/revenge/agnostic evasion)
