- theme: `two-foundations-conscience-vs-grievance` (whole ch) В· `agnosticism-as-moral-evasion` (vv21-22) В· `the-tell-of-half-belief` (v22) В· `grievance-mutated-into-a-political-claim` (vv17, 24) В· `the-borrowed-grievance` (vv23-24 вЂ” Zoramite wearing Lamanite grievance) В· `honest-anger-vs-cold-dismissal` (vv13, 22)

### from Alma 55 (Gid taken without blood)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (bloodless victory; refuses to kill the helpless) В· `Laman-Nephite-scout` (executes the wine stratagem) В· `Ammoron` (knows his cause unjust, fights anyway)
- doctrine: `refusing-to-kill-the-helpless-even-when-you-could` (vv18-19 вЂ” David/sleeping-Saul) В· theme: `the-stratagem-that-serves-mercy` (vv4-24) В· `the-enemys-own-appetite-is-the-weapon` (vv10-14) В· `angriest-at-the-knowingly-false` (v1) В· `remember-God-and-dont-fall-for-your-own-trick` (vv30-32)

### from Alma 56 (Helaman's epistle вЂ” the stripling warriors fight)
- person: `Helaman` (writes epistle; leads + protects the 2000 "sons") В· `the-two-thousand-stripling-warriors` (fearless faith; none slain) В· `the-mothers-of-Ammon` (taught "if ye doubt not, God will deliver") В· `Antipus` (commander; falls, "happy")
- doctrine: `faith-taught-by-believing-mothers` (v47) В· `believing-on-the-words-of-a-trusted-witness` (v48 вЂ” "we do not doubt our mothers knew it") В· theme: `courage-that-is-a-function-of-faith-not-bravado` (vv45-47) В· `reluctance-even-in-the-young-warriors` (v46) В· event: `not-one-of-the-two-thousand-slain` (vv55-56)

### from Alma 57 (campaign continues вЂ” exactness + the deepened miracle)
- person: `Helaman` (counts the wounded) В· `the-two-thousand-and-sixty-stripling-warriors` (exact obedience; all wounded, none slain) В· `Gid` (prisoner-guard; reports the rebellion)
- doctrine: `obedience-with-exactness-as-the-form-of-faith` (v21) В· `faith-preserves-through-the-wounds-not-from-them` (vv25-26) В· `preservation-is-a-particular-sign-not-a-universal-rule` (vv26, 36) В· theme: `minds-firm-trust-continually` (v27) В· `the-honest-horror-of-even-a-righteous-war` (vv14, 32-33 вЂ” surrendered prisoners slain in rebellion)

### from Alma 58 (siege of Manti вЂ” peace to the soul; refuse to murmur)
- person: `Helaman` (receives peace; refuses to murmur when abandoned) В· `Gid-Teomner` (the ambush that takes Manti) В· `the-stripling-warriors` (stand fast; none slain)
- doctrine: `God-speaks-peace-to-the-soul-before-the-deliverance` (vv10-11) В· `peace-and-faith-are-the-strengthening-not-a-consolation-prize` (vv11-12) В· theme: `refuse-to-murmur-when-your-own-side-fails-you` (vv34-37) В· `Helaman-vs-Moroni-two-responses-to-neglect` (vv35-37 vs ch 60) В· `wisdom-adapts-against-a-learning-enemy` (vv1, 13-28) В· `preservation-was-the-sign-daily-faithfulness-the-substance` (vv39-40)

### from Alma 59 (Nephihah falls вЂ” Moroni's anger kindles)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (rejoices, then doubts, then angry at the government) В· `Pahoran` (assumed indifferent вЂ” wrongly) В· `Helaman` (the foil)
- event: `the-fall-of-Nephihah` (vv5-10) В· doctrine: `prevention-is-cheaper-than-recovery` (v9) В· theme: `even-Moroni-doubts` (vv11-12) В· `doubt-curdling-into-anger-at-the-wrong-target` (v13) В· `judging-a-matter-before-hearing-it` (v13)

### from Alma 60 (Moroni's furious epistle)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (accusatory letter вЂ” right doctrine + heart, wrong judgment) В· `Pahoran` (accused of "thoughtless stupor"/treason вЂ” falsely)
- doctrine: `the-righteous-slain-are-not-lost-and-not-proof-of-their-wickedness` (vv12-13) В· `death-of-the-righteous-condemns-the-negligent-not-the-dead` (vv10-13) В· `cleanse-the-inward-vessel-first` (vv23-24) В· `internal-corruption-defeats-before-the-enemy-does` (vv15-16) В· `fear-God-not-power-seek-to-pull-power-down` (vv28, 36) В· theme: `right-doctrine-pure-heart-wrong-judgment-of-a-person` (vv7, 18, 33)

### from Alma 61 (Pahoran's gracious reply)
- person: `Pahoran` (falsely accused, driven out by rebels; responds with grace) В· `Captain-Moroni` (the accuser whose harsh letter still carried a true word) В· `the-king-men-rebels` (overthrew Zarahemla, allied with Lamanites)
- doctrine: `receive-false-accusation-by-blessing-the-heart-behind-it` (v9) В· `a-flawed-message-can-still-carry-a-true-word` (vv19-20) В· `liberty-subordinated-to-obedience-to-God` (vv12-13) В· theme: `the-assume-the-best-instinct-vindicated` (vv3-8 вЂ” Helaman right, Moroni wrong) В· `take-the-truth-let-the-tone-go` (vv9, 19-20) В· `conflict-that-deepens-the-friendship` (vv9, 21)

### from Alma 62 (the war ends; same affliction hardens / softens)
- person: `Captain-Moroni` (retakes the cities; retires in peace to Moronihah) В· `Pahoran` (restored to the judgment-seat) В· `Teancum` (kills Ammoron in a final solo raid, slain вЂ” "a true friend to liberty") В· `Helaman` (rebuilds the church; dies in the 35th year)
- doctrine: `the-same-affliction-hardens-some-and-softens-others` (v41 вЂ” suffering a catalyst, not a cause) В· `remembering-is-the-antidote-to-the-pride-cycle` (vv49-50 вЂ” prosperity without pride because they remembered) В· `the-prayers-of-the-righteous-spare-the-many` (v40) В· theme: `righteous-anger-unbridled-carries-a-cost` (vv35-37 вЂ” Teancum dies on anger's errand) В· `the-great-captain-exits-in-peace-not-glory` (v43) В· `the-grievance-cure-still-working` (vv27-29 вЂ” prisoners become free people of Ammon)

### from Alma 63 (close of the book of Alma вЂ” continuity, not climax)
- person: `Shiblon` (the steady, just son; receives the records, confers on Helaman) В· `Corianton` (the restored son; sails north carrying provisions вЂ” laboring, not given the records) В· `Helaman (son of Helaman)` (receives the records вЂ” chain into the book of Helaman) В· `Captain-Moroni` (dies, one verse) В· `Hagoth` ("an exceedingly curious man"; ships north) В· `Moronihah` (defeats the Lamanite incursion)
- doctrine: `the-sacred-record-passes-through-chosen-faithful-hands` (vv1-2, 11-17 вЂ” generation to generation, Alma 37 fulfilled) В· theme: `the-restored-son-serves-the-steady-son-keeps` (vv2, 10) В· `the-great-are-remembered-by-deeds-not-death-notices` (v3 вЂ” Moroni's one-line death) В· `a-record-honest-about-the-limits-of-its-knowledge` (v8 вЂ” "whither she did go we know not")

## вЂ” THE BOOK OF HELAMAN (great reversal: righteous Lamanites / wicked Nephites; rise of the Gadianton robbers) вЂ”

### from Helaman 1 (peace collapses inward; the secret combination is born)
- person: `Pahoran-the-second` (chief judge, murdered on the judgment-seat) В· `Paanchi` (seditious brother, executed) В· `Pacumeni` (third brother, chief judge, slain against the wall) В· `Kishkumen` (the assassin, founder-figure of the secret band) В· `Coriantumr` (Nephite dissenter, takes Zarahemla, overextends and is slain) В· `Tubaloth` (son of Ammoron) В· `Moronihah`/`Lehi` (cut Coriantumr off, retake Zarahemla)
- doctrine: `the-secret-combination-is-the-anti-covenant` (1:11 вЂ” oath sworn in God's name to conceal murder) В· theme: `the-deadliest-threat-is-internal-not-external` (1:1-18) В· `complacency-leaves-the-center-undefended` (1:18, 26) В· `audacity-without-depth-of-position-destroys-itself` (1:22-32) В· `the-great-reversal-righteous-Lamanites-wicked-Nephites` (book heading)

### from Helaman 2 (Gadianton named; the servant foils the band)
- person: `Helaman (son of Helaman)` (chief judge, assassination target, records the book) В· `Gadianton` ("expert in many words and in his craft"; the named destroyer of the nation) В· `Kishkumen` (drawn out and slain by the servant) В· `the-unnamed-servant-of-Helaman` (infiltrates, learns the sign, kills Kishkumen)
- doctrine: `flattery-and-craft-are-the-combination's-door` (2:4-5 вЂ” words before violence) В· theme: `the-combination's-program-is-to-capture-the-state-for-the-insiders` (2:5) В· `the-counter-to-the-secret-is-one-faithful-person-who-enters-it` (2:6-9) В· `anonymous-faithfulness-saves-what-the-named-cannot` (2:6-9) В· `Mormon-names-the-ending-in-advance` (2:13-14 вЂ” the seed that overthrows the whole nation)

### from Helaman 3 (two growths in one season; the word divides the snares; sanctification by yielding)
- person: `Helaman (son of Helaman)` (judge with justice; dies v37) В· `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (eldest, named for founder; succeeds) В· `Gadianton` (combinations grow unseen by government, v23)
- doctrine: `the-word-of-God-divides-asunder-the-snares-of-the-devil` (3:29-30 вЂ” antidote to the combination's craft) В· `sanctification-comes-by-yielding-the-heart-to-God` (3:35 вЂ” give-away-all-my-sins core) В· `the-gate-of-heaven-is-open-unto-all-who-will` (3:27-28) В· theme: `two-growths-in-one-season-rot-and-word` (3:23-26) В· `persecution-is-the-occasion-of-the-humble's-sanctification` (3:34-35) В· `pride-enters-the-professors-not-the-church` (3:33) В· `the-Nephite-end-foretold-they-become-Lamanites` (3:16)

### from Helaman 4 (the fall; left in their own strength)
- person: `Moronihah` (regains half the lands on repentance; can obtain no more) В· `Nephi and Lehi (sons of Helaman)` (preach + prophesy of the iniquities)
- doctrine: `boast-in-your-own-strength-and-you-are-left-in-it` (4:13 вЂ” self-sufficiency granted, found man-for-man insufficient) В· `the-Spirit-dwells-not-in-unholy-temples` (4:24 вЂ” withdrawal as incompatibility) В· `defeat-is-traced-to-wickedness-not-the-enemy` (4:11, D&C 82:10) В· `repentance-immediately-restores-prosperity` (4:15) В· theme: `the-pride-that-destroys-is-the-pride-that-oppresses-the-poor` (4:12) В· `in-the-space-of-not-many-years` (4:26) В· `the-reversal-completed-Nephites-as-wicked-as-the-Lamanites` (4:22-26)

### from Helaman 5 (remember, remember; the rock; the prison of fire)
- person: `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (gives up the seat to preach; imprisoned; encircled by fire) В· `Lehi (son of Helaman)` (co-missionary) В· `Helaman (father)` (the "remember" / rock-of-the-Redeemer charge) В· `Aminadab` (dissenter who sees the shining faces, teaches the way out of darkness)
- doctrine: `build-on-the-rock-of-the-Redeemer-and-the-storm-cannot-drag-you-down` (5:12) В· `Christ-redeems-from-sins-not-in-sins` (5:10 вЂ” death of cheap grace) В· `remembering-is-the-foundation-of-discipleship` (5:6-12 вЂ” answer to ch4's fall) В· `names-are-a-call-to-remember-and-become` (5:6-7) В· `the-still-voice-of-perfect-mildness-shakes-the-earth` (5:30-31) В· theme: `the-fire-that-protects-instead-of-burns` (5:23-24, 43-44) В· `cry-unto-the-voice-until-the-darkness-disperses` (5:41-42) В· `the-word-recovers-what-the-sword-could-not` (5:50-52)

### from Helaman 6 (reversal complete; secret-combination theology; opposite responses)
- person: `Cezoram` (chief judge murdered on the seat; his son too) В· `Gadianton`/`Kishkumen` (founders, Satan's instruments) В· `Satan (the author of all sin)` (the one being behind Eden, Cain, Babel, Jaredites, Gadianton) В· `Nephi and Lehi (sons of Helaman)`
- doctrine: `the-Spirit-follows-the-heart-not-the-lineage` (6:34-36 вЂ” withdraws from the hard, pours on the willing; final answer to 2 Ne 5) В· `easiness-and-willingness-to-believe-is-the-whole-qualification` (6:36) В· `secret-combinations-are-Satan's-one-continuous-project` (6:26-30 вЂ” author of all sin) В· theme: `prolonged-prosperity-not-affliction-is-the-occasion-of-the-fall` (6:16-17 вЂ” dark twin of 62:41) В· `same-cancer-opposite-responses-opposite-fates` (6:37-38) В· `the-combination-offers-escape-from-consequence` (6:21, 24 вЂ” inverse of the gospel) В· `the-combination-builds-a-state-within-the-state` (6:22-24, 39)

## вЂ” THE PROPHECY OF NEPHI (Helaman 7-16: Nephi's tower lament в†’ the murder of the chief judge в†’ the sealing power в†’ Samuel the Lamanite) вЂ”

### from Helaman 7 (Nephi's tower lament; these are my days)
- person: `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (rejected in the north; pours out his soul on the garden tower; cries repentance)
- theme: `these-are-my-days-faithfulness-in-the-age-you-are-given` (7:7-9) В· `the-prophet's-grief-becomes-the-sermon` (7:11-15) В· `forgetting-God-in-the-very-day-of-deliverance` (7:20) В· `judicial-corruption-when-the-combination-captures-the-courts` (7:4-5) В· doctrine: `greater-knowledge-greater-accountability` (7:23-24 вЂ” the key to the reversal) В· `God's-forsaking-is-self-caused-by-hardened-hearts` (7:17-18)

### from Helaman 8 (the prophet-chain testimony of Christ; the murder revealed)
- person: `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (recites the prophet-chain; reveals the murder) В· `the Gadianton judges` (incite the crowd; fear the people not God) В· `the faithful remnant` ("let this man alone... he is a good man")
- doctrine: `all-the-prophets-testified-of-Christ` (8:13-23 вЂ” scripture is one testimony) В· `look-upon-the-Son-of-God-and-live` (8:14-15 вЂ” brazen serpent, the simple gaze) В· `fulfilled-prophecy-is-evidence-for-prophecy-not-yet-fulfilled` (8:20-21 вЂ” Mulekites as proof) В· `unbelief-against-total-evidence-is-willful-not-honest` (8:24) В· theme: `corruption-fears-the-people-not-God-and-acts-through-the-mob` (8:4-7) В· `brother-kills-brother-for-the-seat-Cain-runs-again` (8:27-28)

### from Helaman 9 (the murder mystery; Seantum named by sign)
- person: `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (accused of conspiracy; vindicated by the sign; deflects glory to God) В· `the five` (verify, jailed as murderers, converted in prison) В· `Seantum` (the fratricide; confesses by the sign) В· `the Gadianton judges` (invent the conspiracy theory; bribe + threaten)
- theme: `overwhelming-evidence-met-with-a-manufactured-alternative` (9:16 вЂ” motivated unbelief) В· doctrine: `true-prophecy-is-specific-and-falsifiable` (9:25-37 вЂ” the step-by-step Seantum sign) В· `the-faithful-messenger-deflects-glory-to-God` (9:36) В· theme: `the-crowd-deifies-the-messenger` (9:41 вЂ” the error Nephi forestalled) В· `the-corrupt-assume-everyone-has-a-price` (9:20 вЂ” the bribe) В· `judgment-by-appearance-convicts-the-innocent` (9:6-9)

### from Helaman 10 (the sealing power given)
- person: `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (given the sealing power in the valley; turns straight back to preach; carried by the Spirit)
- doctrine: `the-condition-of-unlimited-power-is-a-will-that-will-not-ask-amiss` (10:5 вЂ” the blank check made safe) В· `the-sealing-power-bind-and-loose-on-earth-and-in-heaven` (10:7, Matt 16:19) В· `unwearyingness-is-the-commended-virtue` (10:4-5) В· theme: `the-blessing-comes-in-the-valley-not-the-mountaintop` (10:2-4) В· `the-power-serves-the-ministry-not-the-prophet` (10:11-12) В· `thou-art-Nephi-and-I-am-God-the-line-that-humbles-and-protects` (10:6 вЂ” corrects the ch9 deification)

### from Helaman 11 (a famine instead of the sword; the cycle in fast-forward)
- person: `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (asks the famine; prays back the rain) В· `Lehi (his brother)` ("not a whit behind him")
- doctrine: `the-prophet-asks-for-affliction-as-mercy` (11:4 вЂ” famine not sword) В· `affliction-drives-to-remembrance-where-the-word-could-not` (11:7) В· `real-repentance-sweeps-the-cancer-away-not-just-the-consequence` (11:10) В· `the-intercessor-reasons-from-God's-own-promise` (11:14-16) В· theme: `the-pride-cycle-in-fast-forward` (11:1-37) В· `the-tragedy-of-temporary-remembrance` (11:36 вЂ” "again" they forget) В· `the-combination-cannot-be-defeated-by-force-alone` (11:28-33)

### from Helaman 12 (Mormon's great lament on the human heart)
- person: `Mormon (narrator)` (the editorial meditation)
- doctrine: `man-is-less-than-the-dust-because-the-dust-obeys` (12:7-8 вЂ” the cutting nothingness) В· `prosperity-is-the-moment-of-forgetting` (12:2) В· `chastening-is-the-only-reliable-teacher-of-the-forgetful-heart` (12:3 вЂ” the "why affliction" capstone) В· `the-heart's-asymmetry-quick-to-evil-slow-to-good` (12:4-5) В· `the-root-rebellion-is-not-wanting-God-to-rule` (12:6 вЂ” inverse of Nephi's surrendered will 10:5) В· `the-creation-obeys-God's-voice-instantly` (12:8-17, incl. heliocentric aside v15) В· `repentance-was-declared-that-men-might-be-saved` (12:22 вЂ” door after the doom)

## вЂ” THE PROPHECY OF SAMUEL THE LAMANITE (Helaman 13-15: the outsider prophet on the wall; the signs of Christ's birth + death; the great reversal preached) вЂ”

### from Helaman 13 (Samuel on the wall; the slippery treasures; happiness sought where it cannot be)
- person: `Samuel the Lamanite` (the outsider prophet on the wall вЂ” cast out, sent back, prophesies destruction + the signs of Christ)
- doctrine: `happiness-sought-in-iniquity-is-structurally-impossible` (13:38 вЂ” contrary to the nature of righteousness; Alma 41:10 as ontology) В· `the-curse-is-the-heart-set-on-riches-not-the-riches` (13:21-22) В· `the-righteous-are-what-hold-back-destruction` (13:12-14) В· `procrastinating-salvation-until-everlastingly-too-late` (13:38) В· theme: `the-slippery-treasures` (13:31-37 вЂ” fulfilled Mormon 1:18) В· `the-outsider-prophet-God-sends-the-messenger-you'd-reject` (13:2-4) В· `tomb-builders-honor-dead-prophets-kill-living-ones` (13:24-26) В· `the-flatterer-is-welcomed-the-truth-teller-killed` (13:27-28)

### from Helaman 14 (the dated signs; the two deaths; ye are free)
- person: `Samuel the Lamanite` (the dated signs of Christ's birth + death; the two redemptions; agency)
- doctrine: `the-two-deaths-and-the-two-tiered-redemption` (14:16-18 вЂ” first death universal/free, second death conditional) В· `the-resurrection-redeems-all-mankind-unconditionally` (14:16-17) В· `ye-are-free-God-hath-made-you-free` (14:30-31 вЂ” the agency climax) В· `agency-requires-knowledge-freedom-and-real-consequence` (14:30-31) В· `whosoever-perisheth-perisheth-unto-himself` (14:30) В· theme: `the-dated-falsifiable-signs-leave-no-cause-for-unbelief` (14:2-28, fulfilled 3 Ne 1+8) В· `remember-that-you-are-free` (14:30 вЂ” the Helaman refrain on agency)

### from Helaman 15 (Samuel's close: chastening as love; the steadfast converts)
- person: `Samuel the Lamanite` (closes his prophecy)
- doctrine: `chastening-is-the-proof-of-love-not-its-absence` (15:3 вЂ” "chastened them because he loveth them"; the affliction-arc capstone) В· `the-converts-from-darkness-hold-the-light-more-firmly-than-the-born-in` (15:5-10) В· `the-curse-tracks-deeds-rooted-in-tradition-not-blood` (15:4 вЂ” with-Michael 2 Ne 5 thread) В· `the-latter-day-mercy-and-restoration-of-the-Lamanite-remnant` (15:11-13) В· `less-light-more-faith-the-privileged-convicted-by-the-deprived` (15:14-15, Matt 11:21) В· theme: `love-fully-exercised-can-still-end-in-the-beloved's-destruction` (15:3, 16-17) В· `the-two-destinies-sealed` (15:16-17 вЂ” fulfilled)

### from Helaman 16 (the close; the miracle reassigned to the devil)
- person: `Samuel the Lamanite` (protected on the wall; flees, never heard of again) В· `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (baptizing, working miracles before Christ's coming)
- doctrine: `when-the-miracle-cannot-be-denied-the-hardened-heart-reassigns-its-source` (16:6 вЂ” "he hath a devil") В· `the-purpose-of-prophecy-is-remembrance-that-becomes-future-faith` (16:4-5) В· theme: `the-modern-rationalizations-against-prophecy` (16:16-21) В· `religion-as-a-control-mechanism-the-clerical-control-suspicion` (16:20-21) В· `depending-on-one's-own-wisdom-is-the-root-of-the-rationalizing` (16:15, Isa 5:21) В· `opposition-intensifies-as-the-evidence-intensifies` (16:13-23)

## вЂ” THE BOOK OF 3 NEPHI (the signs fulfilled в†’ the great destruction в†’ CHRIST DESCENDS в†’ the Sermon at Bountiful в†’ the Nephite Zion) вЂ”

### from 3 Nephi 1 (the sign of Christ's birth; the last-hour deliverance)
- person: `Nephi (son of Nephi, son of Helaman)` (keeps the records; prays all day; receives the voice) В· `Nephi (son of Helaman)` (departs, "whither he went no man knoweth") В· `the premortal Christ` (speaks from heaven the night before His birth) В· `Lachoneus` (chief judge)
- doctrine: `the-God-who-speaks-from-heaven-is-the-God-about-to-be-born` (1:13-14) В· `Christ-is-both-Father-and-Son` (1:14 вЂ” "the Father because of me, and of the Son because of my flesh"; Is-Jesus-Christ-God study) В· `the-law-of-Moses-not-abolished-before-Christ-fulfills-it` (1:24-25) В· theme: `faith-tested-to-the-death-deadline-and-the-last-hour-deliverance` (1:9-15) В· `the-sign-fulfilled-every-whit-prophecy-vindicated` (1:15-21) В· `the-persecutor's-plan-of-destruction-frustrated` (1:16) В· `Satan-works-to-make-people-disbelieve-what-they-saw` (1:22) В· `the-rising-generation-lost-to-flattery-righteousness-not-inherited` (1:29-30)

### from 3 Nephi 2 (the forgetting of the signs; the curse lifted on covenant)
- person: `Nephi (son of Nephi)` (keeper of records) В· `the converted Lamanites` (united, numbered + called Nephites, curse lifted)
- doctrine: `familiarity-dulls-the-miracle-the-three-stage-forgetting` (2:1 вЂ” less astonished в†’ hard/blind в†’ disbelieve) В· `the-curse-is-lifted-on-covenant-affiliation` (2:14-16 вЂ” with-Michael 2 Ne 5 thread; literal-skin residue for Michael) В· theme: `the-calendar-remembers-what-the-heart-forgets` (2:7-8 вЂ” time reckoned from Christ) В· `the-dissolution-of-race-into-covenant` (2:11-16) В· `Christ-comes-to-a-people-who-forgot-the-sign` (2:19)

### from 3 Nephi 3 (Giddianhi's letter; Gidgiddoni's defensive war)
- person: `Giddianhi` (Gadianton chief; the inverted-conscience epistle) В· `Lachoneus` (just governor; refuses fear + negotiation) В· `Gidgiddoni` (the prophet-general)
- doctrine: `God-delivers-the-defender-not-the-aggressor` (3:20-21 вЂ” even against evil men, no offensive war) В· `the-righteous-response-to-threat-is-prayer-plus-preparation-plus-repentance` (3:12-16) В· theme: `the-inverted-conscience-calling-evil-good` (3:9 вЂ” "the works thereof I know to be good") В· `the-aggressor-reframes-himself-as-the-victim` (3:10-11) В· `the-prophet-general-military-command-joined-to-spiritual-gift` (3:18-19) В· `the-combination-recruits-as-brotherhood` (3:6-7)

### from 3 Nephi 4 (the great battle; the song of the delivered)
- person: `Gidgiddoni` (defensive strategy vindicated) В· `Giddianhi` (slain fleeing) В· `Zemnarihah` (the siege-layer; hanged, the tree felled)
- doctrine: `fear-of-God-displaces-fear-of-men-the-un-terrorizable-heart` (4:8-10) В· `in-the-strength-of-the-Lord-not-their-own` (4:10, 33 вЂ” inverse of Hel 4:13) В· `the-delivered-give-all-the-glory-to-God-and-credit-repentance` (4:31-33) В· theme: `starve-the-parasite-deny-the-host` (4:1-6, 16-22) В· `provisioning-as-the-prudence-that-makes-deliverance-possible` (4:4, 18) В· `vigilance-not-victory-is-the-permanent-posture-against-the-combinations` (4:28-29)

### from 3 Nephi 5 (Mormon steps forward; the gathering of Israel)
- person: `Mormon` (the abridger steps forward by name; disciple of Christ) В· `Nephi (son of Nephi)` (whose record Mormon abridges)
- doctrine: `the-record-is-a-disciple's-testimony-for-a-salvific-purpose` (5:12-18) В· `the-combination-is-ended-by-the-dual-method-mercy-to-the-repentant-justice-to-the-unrepentant` (5:4-6 вЂ” Hel 6:37 finally applied) В· `the-gathering-of-Israel-is-the-book's-purpose` (5:21-26 вЂ” the remnant brought to Christ) В· `the-spiritual-gathering-precedes-the-geographic` (5:26) В· theme: `the-abridger-writes-toward-a-future-scattered-reader` (5:14-26)

### from 3 Nephi 6 (the tragic turn: inequality, class, the fall of the republic)
- person: `Lachoneus (the son)` (governor in the collapse year) В· `the inspired prophets` (testify of Christ, murdered) В· `the corrupt judges/lawyers/high priests` (murder the prophets, revive the combination)
- doctrine: `the-only-thing-that-can-stop-a-prospering-people-is-their-own-sin` (6:5) В· `inequality-of-wealth-and-learning-breaks-up-the-church` (6:12-14 вЂ” the inverse of the 4 Ne Zion) В· `willful-rebellion-against-known-light-is-the-graver-sin` (6:18) В· theme: `the-same-railing-makes-some-rail-back-and-others-grow-penitent` (6:13) В· `the-establishment-is-angriest-at-the-prophets` (6:21-23) В· `the-combination's-endgame-is-to-overthrow-the-republic-and-install-a-king` (6:28-30)

### from 3 Nephi 7 (the nation fragments; Nephi's ministry in the anarchy)
- person: `Nephi (son of Nephi)` (ministers; angels daily; raises his brother from the dead) В· `Jacob` (anti-Christ king of the combination, flees north)
- doctrine: `society-fragments-into-tribalism-when-the-binding-loyalty-is-lost` (7:2-6) В· `the-relapse-is-worse-than-never-having-known-the-dog-to-its-vomit` (7:8) В· `order-without-righteousness-civil-peace-with-stoned-prophets` (7:14) В· `undeniable-power-provokes-anger-not-faith-in-the-hardened` (7:18-20) В· theme: `faith-so-great-that-angels-minister-daily` (7:15, 18) В· `the-gospel's-ordinances-hold-even-when-the-society-collapses` (7:24-25)

### from 3 Nephi 8 (the great destruction; three days of darkness)
- person: `Nephi (son of Nephi)` (the "just man" keeper; his miracles vouch for the record)
- doctrine: `the-record's-reliability-rests-on-the-moral-purity-of-its-keeper` (8:1) В· `power-in-Christ's-name-requires-purity` (8:1) В· `the-creation-convulses-at-the-death-of-its-Creator` (8:5-18) В· `when-the-Light-of-the-world-died-the-world-went-dark-enough-to-feel` (8:20-23) В· theme: `the-destruction-fulfills-Samuel's-sign-exactly` (8:5-23, Hel 14) В· `the-too-late-repentance-the-recognition-that-comes-when-it-can-no-longer-save` (8:24-25) В· `delayed-repentance-is-never-only-about-the-self` (8:25)

### from 3 Nephi 9 (the voice of Christ from the darkness)
- person: `Jesus Christ (the voice in the darkness)` (pronounces the wo, declares His divinity, gives the invitation + new covenant)
- doctrine: `the-same-voice-pronounces-the-wo-and-extends-the-arm-of-mercy` (9:2-14 вЂ” mercy the final word) В· `Christ's-full-divinity-declared-in-his-own-voice` (9:15-18 вЂ” Creator/eternal/one with the Father/light+life/Alpha+Omega; Is-Jesus-Christ-God study) В· `the-broken-heart-and-contrite-spirit-replace-animal-sacrifice` (9:19-20 вЂ” the new covenant) В· `the-baptism-of-fire-can-come-unfelt` (9:20) В· `receiving-Christ-makes-one-a-son-of-God` (9:17) В· `come-as-a-little-child` (9:22) В· theme: `the-city-is-destroyed-when-there-are-none-righteous-left` (9:11, 13) В· `the-Creator-came-to-his-own-and-was-rejected-by-what-he-made` (9:15-16)

### from 3 Nephi 10 (the hen-gathering lament; the light returns)
- person: `Jesus Christ (the voice)` (the hen-lament; the promise to manifest His body)
- doctrine: `the-hen-gathering-her-chickens-the-tenderest-image-of-Christ` (10:4-6) В· `the-three-tenses-of-Christ's-gathering` (10:4-6 вЂ” have/would have/will gather) В· `ye-would-not-the-willingness-of-Christ-defeated-only-by-the-human-refusal` (10:5) В· theme: `mourning-turned-into-joy-the-third-day-morning` (10:9-10) В· `the-spared-are-those-who-received-the-prophets` (10:12) В· `we-are-the-remnant-of-the-seed-of-Joseph` (10:16-17) В· `the-promise-of-the-descent` (10:18-19)

### from 3 Nephi 11 (CHRIST DESCENDS вЂ” the heart of the book)
- person: `Jesus Christ (descended)` (the risen Lord in white; declares His Atonement; gives the doctrine) В· `the Father` (the voice: "my Beloved Son... hear ye him") В· `Nephi (son of Nephi)` (kisses His feet; given power to baptize)
- doctrine: `the-Father-always-points-to-the-Son-hear-ye-him` (11:7) В· `the-still-small-voice-understood-only-when-the-hearer-attunes` (11:3-6) В· `the-resurrected-Christ-keeps-the-wounds-the-marks-of-the-Atonement-are-eternal` (11:14-15) В· `Christ-meets-souls-one-by-one-not-as-a-mass` (11:15) В· `contention-is-of-the-devil-the-father-of-contention` (11:28-30) В· `the-doctrine-of-Christ-the-rock-believe-repent-be-baptized-become-as-a-child` (11:31-39) В· `declare-more-or-less-than-the-doctrine-and-it-comes-of-evil` (11:40) В· `the-Godhead-are-one` (11:27, 36 вЂ” Is-Jesus-Christ-God study)

## вЂ” THE SERMON AT THE TEMPLE (3 Nephi 12-14: the post-resurrection counterpart to the Sermon on the Mount, Matt 5-7, with Nephite variants) вЂ”

### from 3 Nephi 12 (Sermon at the Temple I: Beatitudes, higher law, be perfect)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (delivers the Sermon) В· `the twelve Nephite disciples` (called, power to baptize)
- doctrine: `the-Beatitudes-are-wrapped-in-the-doctrine-of-Christ` (12:1-6) В· `more-blessed-are-they-who-believe-the-witnesses-words-without-seeing` (12:2 вЂ” reaches the latter-day reader) В· `the-law-is-now-fulfilled-old-things-done-away-all-things-new` (12:18, 46-47) В· `the-higher-law-governs-the-heart-not-just-the-act` (12:21-44) В· `the-higher-law-on-anger-comes-right-after-contention-named-as-of-the-devil` (12:22 вЂ” "without a cause" omitted) В· `be-perfect-even-as-I-the-resurrected-Christ-adds-himself-as-the-standard` (12:48, teleios) В· theme: `salt-and-light-as-gift-and-commission` (12:13-16)

### from 3 Nephi 13 (Sermon at the Temple II: secret worship, treasures, take-no-thought)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (the inward worship, the Lord's Prayer, the take-no-thought charge) В· `the twelve` (addressed directly in v25 as the called ministers)
- doctrine: `they-have-their-reward-the-human-applause-is-the-hypocrite's-full-wage` (13:2, 5, 16) В· `where-your-treasure-is-there-will-your-heart-be-the-heart-follows-the-treasure` (13:21) В· `the-single-eye-and-the-two-masters-undivided-devotion` (13:22-24) В· `take-no-thought-is-the-charge-to-the-called-twelve-not-blanket-counsel` (13:25-34 вЂ” the Nephite interpretive key) В· `seek-ye-first-the-kingdom-and-all-these-things-shall-be-added` (13:33) В· `forgiveness-is-conditioned-on-our-forgiving` (13:14-15)

### from 3 Nephi 14 (Sermon at the Temple III, close: golden rule, fruits, "I never knew you", the rock)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (completes the Sermon)
- doctrine: `cast-the-beam-from-your-own-eye-first-then-help-your-brother` (14:1-5) В· `the-Father-gives-good-gifts-lesser-to-greater` (14:7-11) В· `the-golden-rule-is-the-law-and-the-prophets-stated-actively` (14:12) В· `the-strait-gate-the-narrow-way-the-few` (14:13-14) В· `by-their-fruits-ye-shall-know-them` (14:15-20) В· `I-never-knew-you-salvation-is-relational-not-the-works-resume` (14:21-23) В· `the-house-on-the-rock-is-hearing-AND-doing` (14:24-27 вЂ” the storm beats both houses)

### from 3 Nephi 15 (the law fulfilled; "I am he that gave the law"; the other sheep)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (declares Himself the Lawgiver/Jehovah; reveals the other sheep) В· `the twelve` ("a light unto this people, a remnant of the house of Joseph")
- doctrine: `I-am-he-that-gave-the-law-Christ-is-Jehovah` (15:5 вЂ” the God of Sinai is the risen Christ; Is-Jesus-Christ-God study) В· `the-law-of-Moses-ended-in-Christ-but-the-covenant-continues` (15:4-8) В· `I-am-the-law-the-law-replaced-by-a-Person-look-unto-me` (15:9) В· `other-sheep-one-fold-one-shepherd-the-flock-spans-the-earth` (15:17, 21) В· theme: `Christ-came-in-person-to-the-other-sheep-they-were-not-second-class` (15:24) В· `iniquity-shrinks-the-capacity-to-receive-truth` (15:18) В· `Israel-separated-because-of-iniquity-judgment-and-preservation-in-one-act` (15:19-20)

### from 3 Nephi 16 (the record to the Gentiles; the conditional fulness; Zion brought again)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (reveals the lost tribes; commands the record; warns the Gentiles; quotes Isaiah) В· `the lost tribes` (the other other sheep)
- doctrine: `the-record-made-for-the-Gentiles-to-reach-the-remnant` (16:4 вЂ” the Book of Mormon's purpose/route) В· `the-gospel-comes-to-the-Gentiles-first-in-the-latter-days` (16:6-7, Rom 11) В· `the-fulness-can-be-taken-away-if-the-Gentiles-reject-it-in-pride` (16:10-15 вЂ” a contemporary indictment) В· `the-repentant-Gentiles-are-numbered-among-Israel` (16:13) В· theme: `the-Gentile-reader-is-the-bridge-not-the-destination` (16:4) В· `contention-healed-in-Zion-the-watchmen-see-eye-to-eye` (16:18, Isa 52:8) В· `the-gathering-ends-in-a-song-not-a-judgment` (16:18-20, Isa 52:9-10)

### from 3 Nephi 17 (the tenderest chapter: compassion, the children, the angels of fire)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (compassion, healing, the unwritable prayer, weeping, blessing the children) В· `the little children` (blessed one by one, encircled with fire, ministered by angels вЂ” the climax)
- doctrine: `compassion-changed-His-plan-He-stayed-for-a-weeping-people` (17:1-7) В· `my-bowels-are-filled-with-compassion-the-visceral-love-that-acts` (17:6-9) В· `Christ-paces-His-teaching-to-our-capacity` (17:2-3) В· `they-are-not-lost-unto-the-Father-nothing-is-lost-to-God` (17:4) В· `the-prayer-that-cannot-be-written-the-boundary-of-language` (17:14-17) В· theme: `Christ-wept-twice-from-fullness-not-grief` (17:21-22) В· `the-children-are-the-climax-angels-of-fire-for-the-least` (17:21-24) В· `the-tenderest-scene-is-also-the-most-carefully-witnessed` (17:25 вЂ” 2,500)

### from 3 Nephi 18 (the sacrament instituted; watch and pray; the light to hold up)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (institutes the sacrament; gives the charges; confers the Holy Ghost; ascends) В· `the twelve disciples` (given power to give the Holy Ghost, touched one by one)
- doctrine: `the-sacrament-always-remember-me-and-ye-shall-have-my-Spirit` (18:7, 11) В· `watch-and-pray-always-Satan-desires-to-sift-you-as-wheat` (18:15-18) В· `pray-in-your-families` (18:21) В· `I-am-the-light-which-ye-shall-hold-up-the-borrowed-light` (18:24) В· `forbid-the-unworthy-from-the-sacrament-but-never-cast-out-the-person` (18:28-32) В· theme: `discipleship-is-a-continuous-posture-not-discrete-acts` (18:7-21 вЂ” the recurring "always") В· `the-commandments-are-the-cure-for-contention` (18:34)

### from 3 Nephi 19 (the disciples filled with fire; the prayer to Jesus; made white as He is)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (the intercessory prayer; transfigures the disciples) В· `the twelve disciples` (named; baptized; filled with the Holy Ghost + fire; made white as Christ)
- doctrine: `the-disciples-prayed-to-Jesus-as-their-Lord-and-their-God` (19:18, 22 вЂ” worship of Christ; Is-Jesus-Christ-God study) В· `the-unity-prayer-believers-drawn-into-the-oneness-of-Father-and-Son` (19:23, 29) В· `purified-by-faith-Christ-glorified-in-the-believer` (19:28-29) В· `the-prayer-beyond-words-understood-in-the-open-heart` (19:32-34) В· `faith-unlocks-miracles-unbelief-constrains-even-Christ` (19:35) В· `Spirit-prompted-prayer-it-was-given-them-what-to-pray` (19:24) В· theme: `the-disciples-made-white-as-Christ-transfiguration-glory-not-race` (19:25, 30)

### from 3 Nephi 20 (the miraculous sacrament; the prophet like Moses; the gathering + Isaiah 52)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (provides the sacrament miraculously; the prophet like Moses; quotes Isaiah 52)
- doctrine: `the-miraculous-sacrament-the-bread-of-life-that-fills-the-soul-forever` (20:3-9, John 6) В· `the-Father-and-I-are-one-appended-to-Isaiah` (20:35 вЂ” Is-Jesus-Christ-God study) В· `Christ-is-the-prophet-like-unto-Moses` (20:23, Deut 18) В· `the-blessing-of-Abraham's-seed-is-being-turned-from-iniquity` (20:25-27) В· `Israel-blessed-first-to-carry-the-blessing-to-all-kindreds` (20:26-27) В· theme: `the-remnant-as-a-lion-and-the-New-Jerusalem` (20:16-22, Micah 5) В· `the-redemption-of-Zion-the-beautiful-feet-awake-be-clean` (20:32-45, Isa 52)

### from 3 Nephi 21 (the sign of the gathering: the Book of Mormon; the New Jerusalem)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (gives the sign; prophesies the servant, the New Jerusalem) В· `the marred servant` (brings forth the book, preserved in the Lord's hand)
- doctrine: `the-Book-of-Mormon's-coming-forth-is-the-sign-the-gathering-has-begun` (21:1-7 вЂ” the reader is inside the sign) В· `a-free-nation-established-providentially-so-the-book-could-come-forth` (21:4) В· `the-marred-but-preserved-servant-Gods-wisdom-greater-than-the-devils-cunning` (21:10) В· `the-two-Gentile-destinies-cut-off-or-numbered-among-Jacob` (21:14-22) В· theme: `the-repentant-Gentiles-become-co-builders-of-the-New-Jerusalem` (21:23-25) В· `the-gathering-of-all-the-dispersed-not-in-haste-God-before-and-behind` (21:26-29, Isa 52:12)

### from 3 Nephi 22 (Isaiah 54: the forsaken-then-gathered wife)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (quotes Isaiah 54 to comfort the Nephites about the gathering)
- doctrine: `for-a-small-moment-forsaken-with-everlasting-kindness-gathered-the-asymmetry` (22:7-8) В· `the-covenant-of-peace-is-more-permanent-than-the-mountains` (22:10) В· `God-is-Israel's-husband-the-covenant-as-marriage` (22:5-6) В· `all-thy-children-shall-be-taught-of-the-Lord` (22:13, new covenant) В· `no-weapon-formed-against-thee-shall-prosper-righteousness-of-me` (22:17) В· theme: `the-barren-woman-who-sings-the-desolate-made-most-fruitful` (22:1-3) В· `hope-enlarges-the-tent-before-the-children-come` (22:2-3)

### from 3 Nephi 23 (great are the words of Isaiah; the record audited)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (commands the search of Isaiah; audits the record; expounds the scriptures) В· `Nephi (son of Nephi)` (brings the record; remembers the omission; writes the correction)
- doctrine: `great-are-the-words-of-Isaiah-search-diligently` (23:1-3) В· `Christ-audits-the-record-for-completeness-and-accuracy` (23:6-13 вЂ” resonant with read-before-quoting) В· `the-record-must-preserve-fulfillment-not-just-prophecy` (23:9-13) В· `Christ-expounds-the-scriptures-in-one-then-the-disciples-teach` (23:14) В· theme: `the-right-response-to-a-found-gap-is-acknowledge-and-correct` (23:11-13)

### from 3 Nephi 24 (Malachi 3 вЂ” messenger, refiner's fire, "prove me," book of remembrance)
- person: `Jesus Christ (the messenger of the covenant)` (dictates Malachi; came suddenly to the temple, will come again) В· `Heavenly Father` ("the words which the Father had given unto Malachi") В· `Malachi` (the prophet c. 430 BC the Nephites never had)
- doctrine: `Christ-supplies-the-prophecy-the-Nephites-never-had` (24:1 вЂ” completes the record forward as ch 23 completed it backward) В· `Christ-the-messenger-of-the-covenant-came-suddenly-to-his-temple` (24:1 вЂ” dramatic irony + dual horizon) В· `the-refiners-fire-purifies-not-only-punishes` (24:2-3) В· `God-is-a-swift-witness-against-oppression-of-the-vulnerable` (24:5) В· `God-changes-not-therefore-Jacob-is-not-consumed` (24:6 вЂ” immutability as mercy) В· `prove-me-now-herewith-the-one-invited-test-tithing` (24:8-12) В· `God-keeps-a-book-of-remembrance-of-those-who-fear-him` (24:16-18 вЂ” heavenly record mirrors ch 23's earthly audit) В· theme: `they-that-feared-the-Lord-spake-often-one-to-another` (24:16)

### from 3 Nephi 25 (Malachi 4 вЂ” the day that burns and heals; Elijah)
- person: `Jesus Christ (the Son of Righteousness)` (reads the prophecy that names Himself; the risen Son with healing in His wings) В· `Elijah` (sent before the great and dreadful day to turn hearts) В· `Moses` (the law given at Horeb, remembered though fulfilled)
- doctrine: `one-day-two-destinies-the-same-fire-burns-and-heals` (25:1-2) В· `the-Son-of-Righteousness-arises-with-healing-in-his-wings` (25:2 вЂ” KJV "Sun"в†’"Son" variant) В· `remember-the-law-of-Moses-fulfilled-but-not-despised` (25:4) В· `Elijah-turns-the-hearts-of-the-generations-lest-the-earth-be-cursed` (25:5-6 вЂ” sealing power) В· image: `the-faithful-grow-up-as-calves-released-from-the-stall` (25:2-3) В· theme: `the-last-word-of-the-prophets-is-family-not-wrath` (25:6)

### from 3 Nephi 26 (the lesser part to try faith; babes utter marvelous things; church established)
- person: `Jesus Christ (who was before the world began)` (expounds all things; looses the children's tongues) В· `Mormon` (writes only the lesser part, forbidden the greater) В· `the children/babes of the multitude` (revelators of things greater than the adults received)
- doctrine: `Christ-expounds-all-things-from-the-beginning-to-the-last-day` (26:1-5) В· `the-record-is-given-for-future-generations-by-the-Fathers-command` (26:2) В· `the-lesser-part-is-given-first-to-try-faith-belief-unlocks-the-greater` (26:6-11 вЂ” the load-bearing doctrine; BoM = entrance exam for the sealed portion) В· `out-of-the-mouth-of-babes-the-children-become-revelators` (26:14, 16) В· `the-church-of-Christ-established-baptism-Holy-Ghost-all-things-common` (26:17-21 вЂ” seed of 4 Nephi's Zion) В· theme: `unspeakable-things-not-lawful-to-be-written` (26:18)

### from 3 Nephi 27 (the name + the gospel defined; "even as I am")
- person: `Jesus Christ` (names the church, defines His gospel, sets "even as I am," rejoices and sorrows) В· `the twelve Nephite disciples` (united in fasting; commanded to write + be judges; asked "what manner of men ought ye to be?")
- doctrine: `the-church-must-bear-Christs-name-AND-be-built-on-his-gospel` (27:5-12 вЂ” two requirements) В· `the-gospel-defined-by-Christ-himself` (27:13-21 вЂ” fullest definition in scripture) В· `what-manner-of-men-ought-ye-to-be-even-as-I-am` (27:27 вЂ” becoming like Christ) В· `out-of-the-books-shall-the-world-be-judged` (27:23-26 вЂ” record's ultimate function) В· image: `washed-their-garments-in-my-blood` (27:19) В· theme: `Christ-has-fulness-of-joy-and-real-sorrow-at-once` (27:30-32) В· `enter-at-the-strait-gate-while-it-is-day` (27:33)

### from 3 Nephi 28 (the heart's desire; the three Nephites; translation)
- person: `Jesus Christ` (asks each disciple's desire; grants each according to his heart) В· `the nine disciples` (desire rest, granted at 72) В· `the three Nephites` (desire to tarry and bring souls; translated) В· `John the Beloved` (whose tarrying desire the three shared) В· `Mormon` (writes "I know not," inquires, corrects the record openly)
- doctrine: `the-question-of-the-hearts-desire-reveals-the-soul` (28:1-9) В· `the-more-blessed-desire-is-to-keep-bringing-souls-not-to-rest-sooner` (28:7-9) В· `the-chain-of-oneness-disciple-as-Christ-Christ-as-Father-Father-and-Son-one` (28:10-11 вЂ” major is-jesus-christ-god datapoint) В· `transfiguration-is-the-enabling-condition-of-beholding-God` (28:15) В· `the-doctrine-of-translation-sanctified-in-the-flesh-but-not-yet-resurrected` (28:38-40) В· theme: `Mormon-models-the-honest-record-I-know-not-then-I-have-inquired` (28:17, 36-37) В· `the-OT-deliverance-types-multiplied-in-the-three-Nephites` (28:19-22)

- `doctrine:know-the-master-by-serving-him` вЂ”[can't bear a name whose master you've never served; inverse of "I never knew you"]в†’ 5:13 (Matt 7:21-23; John 10:14; Mosiah 26:24-27)

### в†і Abinadi-Christology spin-off folded back (mos13-16; verified) вЂ” cross-chapter links
- `link:Christology-is-consistent-Nephite-tradition` вЂ”[the "Father of heaven and earth / very Eternal Father" title cluster is identical in Benjamin's angel (3:8), Ammon's summary of Abinadi (7:27), and Abinadi himself (15:4) в†’ not Abinadi's invention but an established Nephite Christology]в†’ 3:8 в†” 7:27 в†” 15:4 (1 Ne 11:16-21 вЂ” the "condescension" vocabulary origin)
- `link:Father-Son-dual-description-not-dual-being` вЂ”[15:2-4 gives TWO grounds for ONE person: Father by divine conception + as Creator, Son by the flesh; "one God" = the incarnate Christ holding both, not modalism, not the Elohim/Christ relationship]в†’ 15:2-4 (standard Restoration reading; held without overclaiming)
- `link:seed-forward-and-backward` вЂ”[Benjamin: covenant в†’ spiritually begotten FORWARD (5:7); Abinadi: atoning death в†’ posterity BACKWARD (15:10-13); two angles on the one spiritual-posterity doctrine; the prophets derive their identity FROM Christ, not the reverse]в†’ 5:7 в†” 15:10-13
- `link:Abinadi-survives-only-through-Alma` вЂ”[the entire discourse survives because ONE listener believed, pled, fled, and "did write all the words which Abinadi had spoken" in hiding (17:2-4) в†’ Waters of Mormon + the church (18); the doctrinal block and the church's founding are causally linked through one converted heart]в†’ 16:14-15 в†’ 17:2-4 в†’ 18 вЂ” Abinadi delivered one soul; that soul kept everything
- `link:Alma-extends-Abinadi-empathic-atonement` вЂ”[Alma's later Christology (Alma 7:9-13) is a direct extension of Abinadi's, adding the empathic dimension: Christ takes flesh/infirmities "that he may know according to the flesh how to succor his people"]в†’ Alma 7:11-13 в†ђ Mosiah 15:1-9 (the traceable transmission line)

### from Mosiah 17

### from Mosiah 18
- `covenant:baptism-bear-one-anothers-burdens` вЂ”[the defining baptismal covenant is mostly horizontal: bear burdens (light by sharing), mourn with mourners/comfort, stand as witnesses; the community IS the covenant]в†’ 18:8-10 (Gal 6:2; Rom 12:15; Mosiah 4:16-26; 2:17) вЂ” **the most-quoted covenant in the BoM**

- `doctrine:baptism-covenant-witness-Spirit-poured-out` вЂ”[baptized in the name of the Lord as witness of the covenant to serve + keep commandments; promise = the Spirit poured out more abundantly]в†’ 18:10-14 (2 Ne 31:13-17; D&C 20:37; Acts 2:38)
- `practice:consecration-in-seed-proportional-giving` вЂ”[impart according to what one has; more from more, to him that had not should be given; free-will; the economic form of bearing burdens]в†’ 18:27-29 (Mosiah 4:16-26; 4 Ne 1:3; Acts 4:32-35; D&C 42:30)
- `theme:hearts-knit-one-faith-one-baptism` вЂ”[no contention; look forward with one eye, hearts knit in unity and love; the relational fruit of the covenant]в†’ 18:21 (Eph 4:3-6; 1 Sam 18:1; John 17:21; 4 Ne 1:15)
- `theme:worship-criminalized-as-sedition` вЂ”[Noah reads the gathering as "rebellion"; the church's first corporate act is flight from a state that outlaws it]в†’ 18:33-34 (Mosiah 17:12; Luke 23:2; Acts 17:6) вЂ” the charge that burned Abinadi, now against Alma

### from Mosiah 19
- `theme:king-concerned-for-self-not-people` вЂ”[Noah invokes "my people" to save himself, then commands the men to abandon wives and children; the anti-servant-king exposed in crisis]в†’ 19:7-11 (Mosiah 2:12-14; John 10:11-13; Ezek 34:2-6) вЂ” crisis exposes character
- `prophecy:Noah-burned-fulfilled-to-the-letter` вЂ”[the king who burned the prophet "with faggots" is himself made to suffer death by fire; 12:3+13:10+17:18 converge; burned by the men he betrayed]в†’ 19:20 (Mosiah 12:3; 17:13-18; Alma 25:9; Gal 6:7)
- `theme:loyalty-that-would-perish-with-is-rewarded` вЂ”[the men who "had rather stay and perish with them" vs Noah's command to flee; their willingness to die together saves them all]в†’ 19:12-14 (1 Sam 30:18-19; John 15:13)
- `theme:just-son-of-a-wicked-father` вЂ”[Limhi knew his father's iniquities + loved him + was "a just man"; the inverse of Noah; righteousness runs by choice, not blood]в†’ 19:16-17 (Mosiah 11:1; Ezek 18:14-20; 2 Kgs 22:1-2)
- `structure:embedded-record-frame-closed` вЂ”[the half-tribute + guards = exactly Limhi's bondage in ch 7; the back-fill (9-19) has caught up to its frame; the dramatic irony complete]в†’ 19:15,26-28 (Mosiah 7:15,22; 9:10; 11:21)
- `thread:wicked-priests-flee-and-propagate` вЂ”[Noah's priests escape the fire в†’ kidnap the Lamanite daughters (ch 20) в†’ the Amulonites burn believers (Alma 25); Abinadi's "thy seed" set in motion]в†’ 19:21 (Mosiah 20:3-5; Alma 25:4-12; 17:15)

### from Mosiah 20
- `theme:wickedness-compounds-abandonment-to-abduction` вЂ”[the priests forsook their own families, then stole others'; sin unrepented escalates; done from "secret places"]в†’ 20:3-5 (Mosiah 19:11,21; Judg 21:20-23)
- `theme:innocent-bear-the-guilty's-sin` вЂ”[Limhi's people nearly destroyed for the priests' crime while the guilty hide safely; sin's spillover onto the innocent]в†’ 20:6-16 (Mosiah 27:13; Ezek 18:20; Deut 24:16)
- `theme:just-response-investigate-not-retaliate` вЂ”[Limhi spares the captured king and vows to search out the actual guilty; contrast Noah]в†’ 20:14-16 (Prov 18:13; 1 Sam 24:10-12; Mosiah 19:8)
- `person:Gideon-wise-counselor-and-prophecy-reader` вЂ”[solves the mystery (the priests), de-escalates, and reads the bondage as Abinadi's prophecy fulfilled "because we would not hearken"]в†’ 20:17-21 (Mosiah 12:1-8; 17:15; Alma 1:8)
- `theme:better-bondage-than-death-stop-the-bloodshed` вЂ”[Gideon's counsel: keep the oath, accept tribute, survive; a time to fight and a time to bend]в†’ 20:22 (Mosiah 7:15; 21:13; Eccl 3:8)
- `theme:unarmed-peace-disarms-the-armed` вЂ”[truth + disarmament + the king's intercession ends the war; "when they saw... without arms, they had compassion"]в†’ 20:24-26 (Alma 24:18-25; Matt 5:9; Rom 12:18) вЂ” flash-forward to the Anti-Nephi-Lehies
- `theme:fight-for-wives-and-children-like-dragons` вЂ”[the outnumbered defenders' strength is what they protect]в†’ 20:11 (Mosiah 19:12; Alma 43:45; 46:12)

### from Mosiah 21
- `doctrine:God's-slow-yes-burden-eased-before-removed` вЂ”[slow to hear (consequence) / nevertheless heard (mercy persists) / burdens eased (partial relief) / not yet delivered; God answers WITHIN the bondage before answering the bondage]в†’ 21:15 (Mosiah 11:24; Ex 3:7-9; D&C 101:7-9) вЂ” **the pastoral heart of Mosiah**: not always out, but always with
- `prophecy:slow-to-hear-fulfilled` вЂ”[Abinadi's 11:24 lands: "slow to hear their cry because of their iniquities"; smitten on cheeks, burdens, driven like a dumb ass (12:2,5)]в†’ 21:3-4,15 (Mosiah 11:24; 12:2,5)
- `theme:self-deliverance-exhausted-before-humility` вЂ”[three failed rebellions by the arm of flesh, THEN humbled "even to the dust"; deliverance begins where self-deliverance ends]в†’ 21:6-14 (Mosiah 9:17; Hel 12:3; 29:20)
- `structure:deliverance-pair-stratagem-vs-miracle` вЂ”[Limhi's people humbled the hard way в†’ eased + escape by stratagem (ch 22); Alma's already humble в†’ swift miracle + burdens lightened (24); calibrated to the heart]в†’ 21:5,15 (Mosiah 22; 24:14-25)
- `practice:widow-care-under-bondage` вЂ”[every man imparts to the widows + children even while oppressed; Benjamin's 4:26 lived in chains]в†’ 21:17 (Mosiah 4:16-26; 18:27; James 1:27)
- `structure:embedded-frame-rejoined` вЂ”[Ammon's arrival = ch 7 retold from inside; the back-fill (9-21) circles back to the frame's present; the two ends meet]в†’ 21:22-28 (Mosiah 7:6-15; 8:9)
- `doctrine:covenant-made-but-baptism-waits-for-authority` вЂ”[Limhi's people covenant now; Ammon will NOT baptize without authority ("unworthy servant"); do it right over do it now]в†’ 21:32-35 (Mosiah 18:13; 25:17-18; D&C 20:73)

### from Mosiah 22
- `structure:deliverance-by-stratagem-completes-the-pair` вЂ”[Limhi's humbled-the-hard-way people escape by wit + effort (drunk guards, back pass); Alma's already-humble people by straight miracle (24); God meets each where their heart is]в†’ 22:2-11 (Mosiah 21:5,15; 24:19-25; 7:18)
- `theme:bondage's-own-instrument-becomes-the-escape` вЂ”[the tribute-wine of their servitude + the guards' drunkenness (the oppressor's vice) open the back door; the mechanism of bondage turned against it]в†’ 22:7,10 (Alma 55:8-17; Prov 20:1; Judg 7)
- `person:Gideon-the-deliverer-completes-his-arc` вЂ”[sword on Noah (19) в†’ peace-broker (20) в†’ prophecy-reader (20) в†’ deliverer (22); strength yoked to wisdom, at the people's service; "profitable servant"]в†’ 22:3-9 (Mosiah 2:21; 19:4; 20:17; Alma 1:8)
- `textual:records-gathered-to-the-seer` вЂ”[Mosiah receives the Zeniff record (9-22) AND the 24 Jaredite plates; both converge in the one with the gift to translate в†’ ch 28 в†’ Ether]в†’ 22:14 (Mosiah 8:9; 28:11-19; Ether 1:1-2)
- `principle:voice-of-the-people-in-seed` вЂ”[even the escape is decided by gathering "the voice of the people"; the principle Mosiah institutionalizes in ch 29; righteous leadership consults]в†’ 22:1 (Mosiah 29:25-29; 7:9)
- `structure:Zeniff-record-ends` вЂ”[chs 9-22 close; the back-fill complete; the main narrative (Alma's people 23-24, reunification 25) resumes]в†’ 22:13-14 (Mosiah 9:1; 25:1-7)

### from Mosiah 23
- `doctrine:esteem-not-one-flesh-above-another` вЂ”[Alma refuses the crown: kingship institutionalizes the lie that one flesh outranks another; just-king ideal vs unjust-king risk (Noah the proof)]в†’ 23:7-8 (Mosiah 29:12-23; 1 Sam 8:5-18; Matt 23:8-12) вЂ” the doctrine Mosiah enacts in ch 29
- `theme:refuse-power-knowing-its-corruption-firsthand` вЂ”[Alma "caught in a snare" as Noah's priest; refuses the crown as one who felt power deform him; does not glory]в†’ 23:9-11 (Mosiah 17:2; 18:1; Alma 36:6; 1 Tim 1:13)
- `doctrine:two-bondages-two-liberties-stand-fast` вЂ”[freed from Noah (political) AND the bands of iniquity (spiritual); stand fast in liberty (Gal 5:1); guard against tyrant + false teacher]в†’ 23:12-14 (Gal 5:1; 2 Ne 28:19; Isa 58:6)
- `doctrine:the-Lord-chastens-the-righteous` вЂ”[Alma's GOOD people in bondage as TRIAL of patience + faith, not consequence; the counterpoint to Limhi's bondage-as-judgment; same affliction, opposite meaning by the heart]в†’ 23:21-24 (Heb 12:6-11; D&C 122:7; Job 23:10; Mosiah 24:14) вЂ” affliction is not proof of sin
- `theme:surrender-in-faith-not-rebellion` вЂ”[Alma's already-humble people deliver themselves up trusting God; contrast Limhi's 3 failed rebellions]в†’ 23:27-29 (Mosiah 24:13-21; 21:6-14; Ex 14:13)
- `theme:love-thy-neighbor-as-the-social-order` вЂ”[every man love his neighbor as himself в†’ no contention; the baptismal covenant (18:8) as the society's constitution]в†’ 23:15 (Mosiah 18:21; Lev 19:18; 4 Ne 1:15)
- `theme:the-wicked-set-to-rule-the-righteous` вЂ”[Amulon (Noah's priest) made king over Alma (righteous founder); the promise broken; bondage to the wickedness fled вЂ” the trial at its cruelest]в†’ 23:37-39 (Mosiah 24:8-11; Alma 25:4; Eccl 4:1)

### from Mosiah 24
- `doctrine:burdens-made-light-the-bearer-strengthened` вЂ”[God does NOT remove the burden first; He strengthens them to bear it "with ease... even while you are in bondage"; same weight made light by changing the bearer]в†’ 24:14-15 (Matt 11:28-30; Isa 46:3-4; 2 Cor 12:9; Alma 33:23) вЂ” **the deepest BoM answer to the affliction of the faithful**
- `doctrine:God-visits-his-people-IN-their-afflictions` вЂ”[present in the suffering before the rescue; the answer to ch 23's chastening вЂ” chastened AND visited, the same God's two hands]в†’ 24:14 (Ex 3:7-9; Mosiah 23:21; D&C 122:7; Ps 23:4)
- `doctrine:the-prayer-of-the-heart` вЂ”[vocal prayer forbidden on pain of death; they "pour out their hearts" silently and God "knows the thoughts of their hearts"; prayer cannot be outlawed because it is interior]в†’ 24:11-12 (Dan 6:7-10; 1 Sam 1:13; Ps 139:1-4; Matt 6:6) вЂ” forbidden silent cry в†’ free vocal praise (v22)
- `structure:deliverance-pair-completed-Alma-by-miracle` вЂ”[Alma's already-humble people delivered by sheer miracle (deep sleep), no effort but obedience; vs Limhi's stratagem (ch 22); manner reveals the heart]в†’ 24:16-21 (Mosiah 22:2-11; 21:15; 1 Sam 26:12)
- `theme:faith-and-patience-draw-the-deliverance` вЂ”[cheerful patient bearing of the eased burden в†’ "so great was their faith and patience" в†’ "on the morrow I will deliver you"; submission as the faith that draws the rescue]в†’ 24:15-17 (Rom 5:3-5; James 1:3-4; Ex 3:12)
- `theme:skill-without-God-makes-cleverer-wickedness` вЂ”[the Amulonites teach the Lamanites language, literacy, trade, worldly wisdom вЂ” but not God; a literate prosperous godless people delights more in wickedness]в†’ 24:4-7 (Omni 1:18; 2 Ne 9:28-29; 4 Ne 1:43-46)
- `theme:gratitude-named-into-the-land` вЂ”[the valley of Alma named for the deliverer; total thanksgiving, even the children who could speak; free praise inverts the forbidden cry]в†’ 24:20-22 (Mosiah 18:30; Ex 15:1-21; Ps 107:1)

### from Mosiah 25
- `theme:one-people-from-many-the-covenant-minority` вЂ”[five streams (Nephite, Mulekite, Limhi's, Alma's, repentant Amulonite children) made one "people of God"; yet always outnumbered вЂ” security in God, not numbers]в†’ 25:1-13 (Omni 1:13-19; Hel 6:10; 3 Ne 2:14)
- `theme:records-read-form-a-people` вЂ”[Mosiah reads the records aloud; the people moved through wonder/joy/grief/thanks/anguish; scripture read together makes a community]в†’ 25:5-11 (Mosiah 1:3-7; Neh 8:1-12; Deut 31:11-13)
- `theme:anguish-for-the-souls-of-the-lost` вЂ”[pain for the Lamanites' "sinful and polluted state"; seed of the great missionary effort (ch 27-28)]в†’ 25:11 (Mosiah 28:3; Alma 13:27; D&C 18:10-15)
- `theme:identity-by-choice-not-blood` вЂ”[the children of Amulon refuse their fathers' name and TAKE the name of Nephi; the exact inverse of the inherited "eternal hatred" (10:17); the lie taught in from fathers, broken by the children's choice]в†’ 25:12 (Mosiah 5:8; 10:17; Ezek 18:14-20)
- `doctrine:baptism-that-waited-for-authority` вЂ”[Limhi's people, unbaptizable in ch 21 for lack of authority, baptized now by Alma "after the manner of the waters of Mormon"; patience rewarded]в†’ 25:17-18 (Mosiah 21:33-35; 18:8-17; D&C 20:73)
- `structure:many-churches-one-church` вЂ”[seven churches, too many for one assembly, yet "all one church" вЂ” unified by one doctrine (repentance + faith), not one location]в†’ 25:19-24 (Mosiah 18:17; 4 Ne 1:1; Eph 4:4-6; 1 Cor 1:10)
- `structure:king-and-prophet-distinguished` вЂ”[Mosiah authorizes Alma to organize the church but does not lead it; civil + religious authority kept distinct; the opposite of Noah; prepares the reign of judges]в†’ 25:14,19 (Mosiah 26:8-12; 29:11; contrast 11:5)

### from Mosiah 26
- `theme:founding-experience-uninheritable` вЂ”[the rising generation "could not understand... being little children" at Benjamin's sermon; faith of the fathers does not transmit automatically; each generation must believe for itself]в†’ 26:1-4 (Mosiah 2:1; Judg 2:10; 28:1-3)
- `theme:leader-inquires-rather-than-presumes` вЂ”[Alma faces an unprecedented case, does NOT improvise, "feared he should do wrong," inquired вЂ” blessed FOR asking (v19)]в†’ 26:9-19 (James 1:5; D&C 9:8; 1 Kgs 3:7-9) вЂ” opposite of Noah ruling by "the desires of his own heart"
- `doctrine:faith-in-the-words-alone` вЂ”[Alma believed Abinadi's words ALONE, no sign; the people believed Alma's words alone; the purest faith, which founded the church]в†’ 26:15-16 (Mosiah 17:2; John 20:29; Heb 11:1; Rom 10:17)
- `doctrine:forgiveness-without-a-ceiling` вЂ”[God forgives the sincerely repentant "as often as my people repent"; no quota; the only condition is real repentance]в†’ 26:29-30 (Moroni 6:8; Luke 17:3-4; Matt 18:21-22) вЂ” **the doctrinal heart**
- `doctrine:forgive-or-be-condemned` вЂ”[the reciprocity: God forgives us without limit, therefore we MUST forgive the repentant; to withhold is to condemn ourselves]в†’ 26:31 (D&C 64:9-10; Matt 6:14-15; 18:23-35) вЂ” the one who won't forgive becomes the greater debtor
- `doctrine:hear-my-voice-or-would-not-be-redeemed` вЂ”[the sheep are those who HEAR; the lost "would not be redeemed" and are told "I never knew you"; knowing God = hearing his voice; the loss is self-authored]в†’ 26:21-28 (John 10:14-27; Matt 7:21-23; Mosiah 16:12)
- `practice:church-discipline-aimed-at-repentance` вЂ”[the unrepentant "not numbered... names blotted out," but redemptive вЂ” door open "as often as they repent"; written down so judgment is by revealed principle not whim]в†’ 26:32-36 (Ex 32:33; Moroni 6:7; D&C 20:80)
- `doctrine:covenant-of-eternal-life-to-Alma` вЂ”[the BoM's first explicit promise of eternal life to a named individual; comes after humble inquiry, not a miracle]в†’ 26:20 (2 Pet 1:10; Hel 10:4-7; D&C 131:5)

### from Mosiah 27
- `event:Damascus-road-conversion-of-Alma` вЂ”[the chief persecutor stopped by an angel mid-attack, asked "why persecutest thou the church?", struck down, converted; the BoM's Paul вЂ” chief enemy в†’ chief witness]в†’ 27:11-16 (Acts 9:1-9; 22:6-11; Alma 8:15)
- `doctrine:a-fathers-prayers-answered-agency-preserved` вЂ”[the angel comes because Alma the elder "prayed with much faith concerning thee"; the conversion answers faithful prayer вЂ” yet the son must still choose]в†’ 27:14,16 (Mosiah 28:4-6; Alma 36:17; James 5:16; Enos 1:9) вЂ” prayer opens the door; the other walks through
- `doctrine:church-overthrown-only-by-its-own-transgression` вЂ”[the church cannot be destroyed from outside; only its members' sin can overthrow it; the persecutor is never the real danger]в†’ 27:13 (Mosiah 26:32; D&C 1:14; Hosea 13:9)
- `doctrine:born-again-universal-and-necessary` вЂ”[ALL mankind must be born again, "changed from their carnal and fallen state"; not just the notoriously wicked; "in nowise inherit" without it]в†’ 27:24-26 (John 3:3-5; 2 Cor 5:17; Mosiah 5:7; 15:10-13; Alma 5:14) вЂ” the new-birth thread at its clearest
- `theme:before-and-after-of-redemption-snatched` вЂ”[abyss в†’ marvelous light, eternal torment в†’ pained no more, burning в†’ snatched; the felt reality of redemption, all passive (done TO him)]в†’ 27:28-29 (Alma 36:6-24; Isa 38:17; 1 Pet 2:9; Jude 1:23)
- `doctrine:every-knee-bow-every-tongue-confess` вЂ”[all will confess he is God at the judgment, even those who lived without God]в†’ 27:31 (Philip 2:9-11; Mosiah 16:1; D&C 88:104)
- `theme:persecutors-become-publishers-of-peace` вЂ”[the wreckers become rebuilders "repairing all the injuries"; "how blessed... they did publish peace" = Isaiah 52:7 / Abinadi 15:14-18 FULFILLED in these converts в†’ the Lamanite mission]в†’ 27:35-37 (Mosiah 15:14-18; Isa 52:7; Alma 17-26) вЂ” the Abinadi arc closes its loop

### from Mosiah 28
- `event:mission-to-heal-the-grievance-launches` вЂ”[the sons go to "convince them of the iniquity of their fathers" + "cure them of their hatred" вЂ” going-to the people of the inherited lie to re-teach the true story; the grievance healing begins]в†’ 28:1-2 (Mosiah 10:12-17; Jacob 7:24; Hel 15:7; Alma 17-26) вЂ” **mos10 spin-off: the cure begins here**
- `doctrine:could-not-bear-that-any-soul-perish` вЂ”[missionary zeal at root is the inability to bear a soul lost; worth of souls; grown from 25:11's anguish]в†’ 28:3 (Mosiah 25:11; D&C 18:10-16; Moses 7:41; Matt 18:14)
- `theme:vilest-sinners-become-most-zealous-missionaries` вЂ”[the spared "vilest of sinners" can't bear that anyone else perish; forgiven much в†’ love much; the snatched pull others out]в†’ 28:4 (Mosiah 27:8-10; Alma 26:17; Luke 7:47; 1 Tim 1:13)
- `doctrine:leadership-by-inquiry-and-deliverance-promise` вЂ”[Mosiah inquires before sending his sons; the Lord's fourfold promise governs all of Alma 17-26]в†’ 28:6-7 (Mosiah 26:13; Alma 17:35; 19:22)
- `textual:Jaredite-plates-translated-origin-of-Ether` вЂ”[Mosiah translates the 24 plates with the interpreters; creation в†’ great tower в†’ Jaredite destruction; Moroni abridges as Ether; record-as-warning]в†’ 28:11-19 (Mosiah 8:8-13; Ether 1:1-5; Gen 11:6-9; JS-H 1:35)
- `doctrine:seer-doctrine-confirmed` вЂ”[whosoever has the interpreters "is called seer, after the manner of old times"; ch 8's definition realized]в†’ 28:16 (Mosiah 8:13-18; Ex 28:30; Abr 3:1)
- `structure:no-heir-and-records-to-the-prophetic-line` вЂ”[no son will take the throne (mission over crown) в†’ forces the reign-of-judges question (ch 29); records pass to Alma the convert, not a royal heir]в†’ 28:10,20 (Mosiah 29:1-3; 23:7; Alma 37:1-12)

### from Mosiah 29
- `doctrine:design-government-for-the-worst-case` вЂ”[the just king is best IF guaranteed (Benjamin), but "because all men are not just" you cannot risk a king; build for the wicked ruler you might get]в†’ 29:12-16 (Mosiah 23:7-8; 1 Sam 8:4-22; D&C 121:39) вЂ” the Noah arc's payoff: never again, by design
- `theme:one-wicked-king-and-the-irremovable-tyrant` вЂ”[one wicked king = vast destruction, "cannot be dethroned save... the shedding of much blood"; remember Noah]в†’ 29:17-23 (Mosiah 11; 1 Kgs 12:1-16; Prov 29:2)
- `doctrine:voice-of-the-people-and-its-caveat` вЂ”[govern by common consent (majority tends right, minority is the danger) вЂ” BUT only as safe as the people are righteous: "if the voice of the people doth choose iniquity, then... the judgments of God"]в†’ 29:25-27 (Alma 2:3; Hel 5:2; 3 Ne 7:1-7; D&C 26:2) вЂ” the reform rests on virtue, not structure
- `doctrine:accountability-shifted-from-king-to-people` вЂ”[under a king the people's sins are answered on the king's head; under judges "answered upon their own heads," every man bearing his part]в†’ 29:30-34 (AoF 1:2; 2 Ne 9:7; Ezek 18:20)
- `structure:checks-and-balances` вЂ”[lower judges judged by higher, higher judges judged by a panel of lower by the voice of the people; self-correction without bloodshed]в†’ 29:28-29 (Ex 18:13-26; Deut 17:8-9)
- `theme:king-who-surrenders-power-is-loved-more` вЂ”[Mosiah dissolves his own dynasty for the people's good; loved "beyond measure," not a tyrant seeking gain; servant-king culminated вЂ” the negative of Noah]в†’ 29:40 (Mosiah 2:12-14; 6:7; Matt 20:25-28)
- `event:reign-of-judges-begins-book-ends` вЂ”[Alma the younger = first chief judge + high priest (civil + religious, distinct, one man); kings end; Mosiah + Alma die; 509 years from Lehi; Mosiah closes]в†’ 29:42-47 (Alma 1:1; 2:16)

### from Alma 1
- `theme:priestcraft-the-first-internal-threat` вЂ”[the reign of judges' first crisis is a preacher, not an army: paid+popular clergy + universal-salvation-without-accountability; "would prove their entire destruction"]в†’ 1:3-12 (2 Ne 26:29; Jacob 7:2; Alma 30; Mosiah 11:5) вЂ” error that enriches + flatters dissolves the self-governance the new order needs
- `doctrine:law-punishes-acts-not-belief` вЂ”[Nehor executed for MURDER + enforcing priestcraft by the sword, NOT false doctrine; "the law could have no power on any man for his belief"; religious liberty + rule of law]в†’ 1:12,17-18 (Alma 30:7-11; AoF 1:11; D&C 134:4) вЂ” believe anything, but you may not murder
- `doctrine:universal-salvation-without-accountability-is-false` вЂ”[Nehor's "all men shall have eternal life... need not fear nor tremble" removes the moral stakes]в†’ 1:4 (Alma 30:17; 2 Ne 28:7-9; Morm 8:31)
- `doctrine:true-order-vs-priestcraft` вЂ”[true priests labor + return to work, "no better than the hearer," all equal "according to his strength," give to the poor; priestcraft is paid, elevated, taking]в†’ 1:26-27 (Mosiah 18:24-26; 27:3-5; 4:27; Acts 20:33) вЂ” ministry as giving not getting
- `doctrine:prosperity-without-the-heart-set-on-riches` вЂ”[the church grows rich but "did not set their hearts upon riches; liberal to all... no respect to persons"; proof = no naked/hungry sent away; Jacob 2's distinction]в†’ 1:29-31 (Jacob 2:17-19; Mosiah 4:16-26; D&C 42:30)
- `event:Gideon-slain-by-the-first-priestcraft` вЂ”[the aged deliverer of Limhi's people murdered for withstanding Nehor "with the words of God"; his blood makes the crime capital]в†’ 1:7-9 (Mosiah 22:3-9; Alma 6:7) вЂ” error preached is free; error enforced is death

### from Alma 2
- `doctrine:voice-of-the-people-works-but-not-self-enforcing` вЂ”[the majority rightly rejects Amlici (confirming 29:26), but his faction defies the verdict and makes him king by force; a ballot defeats a demagogue, not his army]в†’ 2:3-10 (Mosiah 29:25-27; Hel 1:1-13)
- `theme:heresy-becomes-insurrection` вЂ”[Amlici is "after the order of" Nehor; priestcraft (ch 1) flows into the kingship-bid (ch 2); same pride-seeking-dominion in two forms; ~19,000 dead trace to Nehor's gospel]в†’ 2:1 (Alma 1:2-15; 46:1-10) вЂ” bad doctrine left to grow ends in mass graves
- `theme:dissent-allies-with-the-enemy` вЂ”[the Amlicites, unable to win at home, join the Lamanites; apostasy enlists the foe; the war worsens]в†’ 2:24-25 (Alma 60:32; 43:13; 47-48) вЂ” Amlicites become Lamanites (ch 3)
- `theme:warrior-prophet-asks-only-to-serve` вЂ”[Alma fights Amlici but prays to be "an instrument... to save and preserve this people," not for himself; the inverse of Amlici who sought power OVER them]в†’ 2:16,29-31 (Alma 4:18-20; Mosiah 23:6-13)
- `doctrine:strengthened-by-the-Lord-after-prayer` вЂ”[vastly outnumbered ("sands of the sea"), the Nephites prevail only "strengthened by the hand of the Lord" after praying mightily]в†’ 2:18,28,31 (Mosiah 9:17; Alma 43:48; 1 Sam 17:45; Deut 31:6)
- `theme:cost-of-one-mans-pride` вЂ”[12,532 Amlicites + 6,562 Nephites slain in a day; dissent that began as flattering doctrine ends in a field of corpses]в†’ 2:19 (Alma 3:1-2; 28:2-3)

### from Alma 3  [BIN-4: 2 Ne 5:21 family вЂ” logged for Michael, not resolved]
- `doctrine:every-man-that-is-cursed-brings-it-on-himself` вЂ”[the chapter's explicit thesis: the Amlicites "brought upon themselves the curse"; a curse is self-authored consequence of rebellion, not arbitrary divine branding]в†’ 3:18-19 (2 Ne 5:21-25; Mosiah 16:12; Hel 14:30)
- `theme:the-mark-is-self-imposed-and-allegiance-based` вЂ”[the Amlicites (Nephites by descent) "marked themselves"; the line is belief/chosen-tradition (v11), not blood; a Nephite who rebels takes the mark]в†’ 3:4,11,13 (Mosiah 25:12; Jacob 1:13-14; Alma 2:11)
- `theme:mark-to-quarantine-the-destroying-tradition` вЂ”[the mark's stated purpose: preserve the people from "incorrect traditions which would prove their destruction"; about the false tradition, not the blood]в†’ 3:8 (Mosiah 10:12-17; 1:5; Alma 9:16) вЂ” ties to the grievance-tradition spin-off
- `doctrine:curse-conditional-removable-on-repentance` вЂ”[the separation stands "except they repent... and turn to me that I may have mercy"; not fated, lifts on repentance]в†’ 3:14 (2 Ne 30:6; Alma 23:18; 3 Ne 2:14-16)
- `doctrine:wages-of-the-spirit-one-obeys` вЂ”[reap rewards by works, "according to the spirit which they listed to obey"; every man paid by the master he chooses]в†’ 3:26-27 (Rom 6:16; Mosiah 2:32-33; Alma 5:41) вЂ” the eternal form of self-authorship

### from Alma 4
- `theme:church-out-prides-the-world-stops-the-gospel` вЂ”[the church's pride "exceed[s]" the world's; its hypocrisy a "stumbling-block" so "the church began to fail in its progress"; the proud example preaches against the gospel]в†’ 4:9-11 (Hel 4:11-12; Rom 2:24; Matt 5:13-16) вЂ” nothing stops growth like the members' pride
- `theme:split-community-closed-hands-vs-open-hands` вЂ”[the proud "turn their backs upon the needy"; the humble "impart their substance to the poor"; the dividing line within the covenant people is generosity]в†’ 4:12-14 (Jacob 2:17-19; Mosiah 4:16-26; Alma 1:27)
- `doctrine:retaining-a-remission-by-imparting-to-the-poor` вЂ”[the faithful keep the remission by succoring the needy; Benjamin's exact phrase]в†’ 4:14 (Mosiah 4:12,26; Alma 5:26; D&C 20:31)
- `event:Alma-trades-the-gavel-for-pure-testimony` вЂ”[the chief judge/governor lays down the judgment-seat to confine himself "wholly to... the testimony of the word"; the most powerful man gives up the worldly office for the necessary spiritual work]в†’ 4:15-20 (Mosiah 29:40; Alma 7:1; Matt 20:25-28) вЂ” the great pivot
- `doctrine:pure-testimony-the-remedy-for-pride` вЂ”[pride can't be legislated away; "no way... save it were in bearing down in pure testimony"; the word does what the law cannot]в†’ 4:19 (Alma 5:1; 31:5; Heb 4:12; Jacob 2:8) вЂ” sets up the great sermons (5, 7, 12-13, 32-34)
- `theme:pride-cycle-affliction-to-pride` вЂ”[affliction humbles в†’ remembrance; peace + prosperity в†’ pride; pride в†’ the next affliction; a disease of the heart no government cures]в†’ 4:3,6 (Hel 12:1-6; Deut 8:11-18; 4 Ne 1:24)

### from Alma 5
- `method:testimony-as-a-mirror-of-questions` вЂ”[Alma doesn't accuse the proud; he asks ~40 questions whether they could stand before God now; you can argue a declaration, not a question to your own conscience; the Spirit convicts, not the preacher]в†’ 5:14-31 (Alma 4:19; Heb 4:12; 2 Cor 13:5) вЂ” **spin-off: alma5_searching-questions**
- `doctrine:can-ye-feel-so-now-the-change-re-verified` вЂ”[the mighty change is not a past transaction to remember but a present state to verify; faith is a pulse, not a deposit]в†’ 5:26 (Mosiah 4:12,26; Alma 4:14; Rev 2:4)
- `doctrine:image-of-God-in-the-countenance` вЂ”[the new birth shows on the face; "received his image in your countenances"; the inverse of Alma 3's mark of rebellion]в†’ 5:14,19 (Mosiah 5:2; Moses 6:65; 2 Cor 3:18) вЂ” what a soul becomes is written on its face
- `doctrine:two-shepherds-two-folds-no-third` вЂ”[good shepherd calls "in his own name, the name of Christ"; refuse his voice and "the devil is your shepherd"; you follow the voice whose works you bring forth; membership is not the question]в†’ 5:37-42 (John 10:11-27; Mosiah 5:8; Alma 3:26-27)
- `doctrine:arms-of-mercy-extended-invitation-at-the-center` вЂ”[for all the woes, the center is invitation: "the arms of mercy are extended... Come unto me and partake of the fruit of the tree of life"; Alma wounds to heal]в†’ 5:33-34,62 (Mosiah 16:12; 1 Ne 8:10; Matt 11:28; Alma 32:40)
- `doctrine:knowing-of-myself-by-the-Spirit` вЂ”[Alma's witness is personal revelation, not inheritance or office: "fasted and prayed many days that I might know these things of myself"; the pattern he presses on them]в†’ 5:45-48 (Mosiah 26:13; Moroni 10:4-5; John 7:17) вЂ” answer to the rising-generation unbelief (Mosiah 26)
- `doctrine:command-to-the-church-invitation-to-the-world` вЂ”[higher accountability for the covenant people ("command"); open door for the rest ("invitation"); much given, much required]в†’ 5:62 (Mosiah 26:32; Luke 12:48; 2 Cor 6:17)

#### в†і alma5 spin-off folded back (verified) вЂ” cross-chapter links
- `link:43-searching-questions` вЂ”[the sermon is built of 43 distinct questions (densest vv14-31); pure testimony executed almost entirely as interrogation of the conscience]в†’ Alma 5 whole (Alma 4:19 mandate)
- `link:three-generation-conversion-chain` вЂ”[Abinadi в†’ Alma the elder (5:11-12) в†’ the fathers в†’ Alma the younger himself (Mosiah 27:24-28); in ch 5 Alma re-asks his congregation his OWN conversion question]в†’ 5:11-14 в†” Mosiah 13-16 в†” Mosiah 27:24-28 в†” Mosiah 5:2 ("mighty change," exact phrase)
- `link:image-in-countenance-restores-Gen-1-image` вЂ”[the new birth restores the divine image the Fall obscured; Webster cites Gen 1:27 under *image*; held as interpretive inference]в†’ 5:14,19 (Gen 1:26-27; 2 Cor 3:18; Moses 6:65)
- `link:sermon-bracketed-by-mercy` вЂ”[opens with memorial questions (vv6-9), closes with the invitation (v62); the scouring questions framed by the open door]в†’ 5:6-9 в†” 5:33-34,62

### from Alma 6
- `practice:word-first-then-order` вЂ”[Alma bears pure testimony (ch 5) to reach the heart, THEN sets the church in order; testimony convicts the heart, order regulates the body вЂ” both needed]в†’ 6:1-4 (Alma 5; Mosiah 18:17-22; 1 Cor 14:40)

### from Alma 7
- `doctrine:empathic-atonement-suffers-to-know-how-to-succor` вЂ”[Christ takes our pains/infirmities not only to pay but "that he may know according to the flesh how to succor"; the omniscient Spirit "knoweth all things," yet the Son enters the suffering to know it from inside; bowels filled with mercy "according to the flesh"]в†’ 7:11-13 (Mosiah 14:3-5; 15:1-9; Heb 2:18; 4:15; D&C 122:8) вЂ” **completes the Abinadi thread (mos13-16): substitution + empathy**; the deepest comfort in the gospel
- `theme:revelatory-honesty-I-do-not-know` вЂ”[Alma marks the boundary of his knowledge: won't claim what "the Spirit hath not said... as to this thing I do not know"; bold on the confirmed, silent on the rest; his caution proves correct]в†’ 7:8 (Alma 40:8; 1 Ne 11:17; D&C 76:114)
- `doctrine:born-of-Mary-in-the-land-of-Jerusalem` вЂ”[a century before Bethlehem: the mother named, virgin conception, the place clarified as the LAND (region) of Jerusalem; consistent Nephite Christology]в†’ 7:10 (Mosiah 3:8; 1 Ne 11:13-21; Isa 7:14; Luke 1:27)
- `theme:pure-testimony-adapts-to-the-people` вЂ”[the prophet who flayed proud Zarahemla with questions (ch 5) comes to humble Gideon with joy + affirmation; woe to the proud, comfort to the faithful]в†’ 7:1-6,17-19 (Alma 5; Mosiah 28:8)
- `doctrine:God-unchangeable-one-eternal-round` вЂ”[no crooked paths, no shadow of turning, "one eternal round"; the ground of trust AND the reason filthiness cannot enter; the constancy cuts both ways]в†’ 7:20-21 (James 1:17; D&C 3:2; Morm 9:9; Mal 3:6)
- `doctrine:filthy-remains-filthy-unclean-cannot-enter` вЂ”[no unclean thing received into the kingdom; "he who is filthy shall remain in his filthiness"; mercy lifts out of the filth but doesn't redefine the kingdom to admit it]в†’ 7:21 (1 Ne 15:33; 2 Ne 9:16; Rev 22:11; Mosiah 2:37)
- `theme:faith-hope-charity-and-the-disciples-attributes` вЂ”[the new-birth life: humble, gentle, patient, temperate, thankful; "faith, hope, and charity, and then ye will always abound in good works"; fruits, not entry-fees]в†’ 7:23-24 (1 Cor 13:13; Moroni 7:33-48; Gal 5:22)

### from Alma 8

### from Alma 9

### from Alma 10

I knew... yet I would not know"; reached only by an angel + hungry prophet at his door]в†’ 10:4-10 (Alma 5:37; John 9:41; Matt 23:37) вЂ” reluctant convert в†’ bold witness
