- `theme:Lehi-of-Manasseh-son-of-Joseph` вЂ”[the only explicit statement of Lehi's tribe: Manasseh, through Joseph sold into Egypt]в†’ 10:3 (1 Ne 5:14; Gen 41:51; 49:22-26)

### from Alma 11
- `doctrine:saved-FROM-sin-not-IN-it` вЂ”[Christ "shall not" save people in their sins; salvation = inheriting the kingdom; "no unclean thing can inherit"; cleansed not excused; refutes Nehor's universal salvation]в†’ 11:34-37 (Hel 5:10; 1 Ne 15:33; Alma 7:21; 1 Cor 6:9; Alma 1:4) вЂ” the Atonement makes the unclean clean, not the kingdom unclean
- `theme:the-bribe-exposes-the-briber` вЂ”[Zeezrom would pay to make Amulek deny a God Zeezrom KNOWS is real вЂ” "thou lovest that lucre more than him"; the offer a trap never meant to be paid; "the righteous yieldeth to no such temptations"]в†’ 11:22-25 (Acts 8:18-23; Luke 16:13; Titus 1:11) вЂ” paying to have the truth denied proves you believe it
- `theme:lawyers-manufacture-conflict-for-fees` вЂ”[paid per suit, "for the sole purpose to get gain... they did stir up the people to riotings" to multiply disputes; a profession profiting from the strife it exists to resolve]в†’ 11:20 (Alma 10:27,31-32; Luke 11:46; Prov 28:8)
- `doctrine:Son-is-the-very-Eternal-Father-condescension` вЂ”[Amulek meets the trap by affirming plainly: "Yea, he is the very Eternal Father of heaven and of earth"; the Abinadi/Benjamin Christology holds under hostile cross-examination]в†’ 11:38-40 (Mosiah 15:1-5; 3:8; Isa 9:6; Ether 3:14)
- `doctrine:universal-resurrection-conditional-salvation` вЂ”[bands of death loosed for ALL; but beyond that "the wicked remain as though there had been no redemption made"]в†’ 11:41 (Mosiah 16:5; Alma 42:23; 2 Ne 9:7-13)
- `doctrine:resurrection-perfect-universal-permanent-with-recollection` вЂ”[spirit+body reunited "in its perfect form," not a hair lost; all rise; "die no more"; "a bright recollection of all our guilt" carried into the resurrection]в†’ 11:42-45 (Alma 40:23; 2 Ne 9:13-14; Mosiah 3:25; 1 Cor 15:42-54)
- `event:Zeezrom-begins-to-tremble` вЂ”[the corrupt lawyer who came to trap "began to tremble"; the knowing of God overpowering the loving of lucre; the great conversion begins]в†’ 11:46 (Alma 12:1-7; 15:3-12; Acts 24:25)

### from Alma 12
- `doctrine:chains-of-hell-self-tightening-spiral` вЂ”[knowledge by "heed and diligence"; harden в†’ lesser portion в†’ "know nothing" в†’ captive by the devil = chains of hell; soften в†’ greater portion в†’ "know in full"; self-forged, no neutral]в†’ 12:9-11 (2 Ne 28:27-30; Matt 13:12; 25:29; D&C 50:24; John 8:34) вЂ” **spin-off: alma12-13**
- `doctrine:flaming-sword-was-mercy-death-as-probation` вЂ”[barring the tree of life preserved the "space... in which he might repent"; without death the fallen state would be eternal; the apparent curse is the gift of probation]в†’ 12:21-27 (Gen 3:22-24; 2 Ne 2:15-21; Alma 42:2-5; Moses 4:31) вЂ” mortality is the chance, not the catastrophe
- `doctrine:probationary-state-time-to-prepare-to-meet-God` вЂ”["this life became a probationary state; a time to prepare to meet God"; death + the time to repent are the plan's mercy]в†’ 12:24,27 (Alma 34:32-35; 42:4-13; Heb 9:27; 2 Ne 2:21)
- `doctrine:harden-not-your-hearts-enter-into-my-rest` вЂ”[the hinge: repent + harden not в†’ mercy through the Only Begotten в†’ "enter into my rest"; the same verb governs the portion of light AND the rest]в†’ 12:33-37 (Alma 13:6-29; Heb 3:7-4:11; Ps 95:8-11; D&C 84:24) вЂ” runs into the priesthood discourse (ch 13)
- `doctrine:plan-of-redemption-laid-before-the-Fall` вЂ”[the redemption "laid from the foundation of the world," prepared before the problem; a designed economy, not an improvised rescue]в†’ 12:25,30,33 (Mosiah 4:6; 15:19; Alma 42:8; Moses 6:62; 1 Pet 1:20)
- `event:Zeezroms-softening-in-real-time` вЂ”[the corrupt lawyer trembling "under a consciousness of his guilt" turns the right way вЂ” "began to inquire diligently... that he might know more"; the reverse spiral enacted in the man hearing it]в†’ 12:1-8 (Alma 11:46; 15:3-12)
- `doctrine:judged-by-thoughts-words-and-works` вЂ”[the whole person condemns or clears; the guilty wish the mountains would hide them from God's presence]в†’ 12:14 (Matt 12:36; Mosiah 4:30; Rev 6:16; Hosea 10:8)

### from Alma 13
- `doctrine:foreordination-on-foreknown-faith-not-election` вЂ”[called "from the foundation of the world according to the foreknowledge of God, on account of their exceeding faith... in the first place left to choose"; "same standing with their brethren"; fore-ordination grounded in agency, not predestination]в†’ 13:3-5 (Alma 12:30; Abr 3:22-23; D&C 138:55; Jer 1:5; Eph 1:4) вЂ” **spin-off: alma12-13**
- `doctrine:sanctified-abhor-sin-new-heart-completed` вЂ”[the fully sanctified "could not look upon sin save it were with abhorrence"; not just forgiven but the appetites remade; the mighty-change thread's terminus]в†’ 13:11-12 (Mosiah 5:2; Alma 5:21; 19:33; Moses 6:59) вЂ” clean desire, not just a clean record
- `theme:Melchizedek-converted-a-wicked-city-the-model` вЂ”[Salem "had waxed strong in iniquity... all gone astray," yet Melchizedek's mighty faith brought them to repent + peace; the greatest high priest succeeding at Alma's task; the model Ammonihah will refuse]в†’ 13:17-19 (Gen 14:18-20; Heb 7:1-4; D&C 84:14; Alma 16) вЂ” a wicked city CAN repent
- `doctrine:enter-into-the-rest-the-goal-of-the-order` вЂ”[priesthood, ordinances ("type of his order"), sanctification, faith-hope-charity вЂ” all FOR entering "the rest of the Lord"; the discourse's destination]в†’ 13:6,12,13,16,29 (Alma 12:34-37; Heb 3:7-4:11; D&C 84:24)
- `structure:12-13-discourse-bookended-chains-to-rest` вЂ”[ch 12 opens with the chains of hell (12:11), ch 13 closes pleading against them (13:30); the whole framed between harden-into-the-chains or soften-into-the-rest; the structure is the message]в†’ 13:30 (Alma 12:11,16; 2 Ne 28:19)
- `doctrine:faith-hope-charity-the-path-into-the-rest` вЂ”[faith on the Lord + hope of eternal life + the love of God in the heart в†’ lifted up + enter the rest]в†’ 13:29 (Alma 7:24; 1 Cor 13:13; Moroni 7:33-48)
- `theme:prophet-pleads-with-anxiety-even-unto-pain` вЂ”[Alma's raw close: "with great anxiety even unto pain... procrastinate not"; "would to God it might be in my day... let it be sooner or later, in it I will rejoice" вЂ” bold hope, submitted timing]в†’ 13:25,27 (Mosiah 28:3; 25:11; Alma 7:8)

#### в†і alma12-13 spin-off folded back (verified) вЂ” cross-chapter links
- `link:chains-of-hell-defined-epistemically` вЂ”[12:11 is an explicit DEFINITION ("this is what is meant by the chains of hell"); the captivity is epistemic before moral вЂ” the devil inherits a vacancy left by the narrowing of received word]в†’ 12:9-11 (D&C 93:39 вЂ” "lesser portion")
- `link:cherubim-enable-the-plan-of-redemption` вЂ”[the flaming sword is the *enabling condition* of redemption, not punishment: without it "no preparatory state... the plan of redemption would have been frustrated" (12:26)]в†’ 12:21-27 (Gen 3:24; 2 Ne 2:15-21)
- `link:rest-of-the-Lord-named-first-in-ch12` вЂ”["enter into my rest" appears first in 12:34, before the priesthood apparatus of ch 13; ch 12 names the destination, ch 13 the institutional means; 8 occurrences across both chapters]в†’ 12:34,37 в†” 13:6,12,13,16,29 (D&C 84:24 вЂ” the rest = "the fulness of his glory")
- `link:foreordination-anti-Calvinist-three-times` вЂ”[13:3-5 insists on equal standing 3Г—: others "might have had as great privilege," all "same standing," the separation from "hardness of their hearts"; Webster's Milton: "Foreknowledge had no influence on their fault"]в†’ 13:3-5 (Abr 3:22-23; D&C 138:55-56)
- `link:12-13-is-a-verbal-ring` вЂ”["chains of hell" opens ch 12 (vv6,11) and closes ch 13 (v30); everything between (Fall, cherubim, probation, redemption, holy order, Melchizedek) is one argument for why the not-hardened heart reaches rest; a textual fact]в†’ 12:6,11 в†” 13:30

### from Alma 14
- `doctrine:why-God-permits-the-innocent-to-suffer` вЂ”[Alma's three reasons, given while watching it: the martyrs "received up unto himself in glory"; he suffers it "that the judgments... may be just" (the wicked complete their guilt); "the blood of the innocent shall stand as a witness"; non-intervention is the intersection of glory, accountability, and testimony]в†’ 14:10-11 (Alma 60:13; D&C 122:5-9; Rev 6:9-11; Heb 11:35) вЂ” **the BoM's hardest confrontation with suffering**, given through tears
- `doctrine:the-Spirit-constrains-the-prophets-power` вЂ”[Amulek could save the burning; "the Spirit constraineth me that I must not stretch forth mine hand"; the power is real but submitted to God's purpose, not the compassion-impulse]в†’ 14:10-11 (Alma 8:31; Matt 26:53) вЂ” the costliest restraint
- `doctrine:protection-lasts-only-as-long-as-the-work` вЂ”["our work is not finished; therefore they burn us not"; the believers' work WAS finished (received in glory); preservation by mission, not favoritism]в†’ 14:13 (Alma 8:31; John 7:30; 8:20; Acts 16:25)
- `event:Zeezrom-harrowed-up-pains-of-hell-as-guilt` вЂ”[the corrupt lawyer "harrowed up under a consciousness of his own guilt... encircled by the pains of hell"; the chains-of-hell (12:11) as awakened guilt; "I am guilty, these men are spotless," and pleads at cost]в†’ 14:6-7 (Alma 12:11; 36:12-16; Mosiah 2:38) вЂ” healed ch 15
- `theme:Christic-silence-and-the-cross-echoes` вЂ”[Alma + Amulek "answered him nothing" (Matt 27:12-14); "deliver yourselves if ye have power" (Matt 27:40), "I have power to deliver you" (John 19:10); the martyrdom patterned on the Passion]в†’ 14:17-24 (Matt 27:12-43; Mark 15:3-5; Isa 53:7; John 19:9-10)
- `theme:sign-seeking-mockery-refused` вЂ”["if ye have the power... deliver yourselves, and then we will believe"; the prophets will not stage a miracle on a mocker's dare]в†’ 14:24 (Matt 12:39; Luke 23:35-39; Alma 30:43-52)
- `event:deliverance-after-the-full-measure` вЂ”[the power comes only "when the last had spoken" вЂ” every tormentor's guilt full; the prison rent, the whole Nehor establishment crushed, the two unhurt; the withheld power (8:31) finally shown]в†’ 14:24-29 (Acts 12:6-10; 16:26; Hel 5:21-50; Alma 14:11)
- `theme:scriptures-burned-but-the-word-survives` вЂ”[the records "which contained the holy scriptures" burned with the believers; copies burn, the word does not]в†’ 14:8 (Jer 36:21-28)

### from Alma 15
- `doctrine:guilt-as-a-burning-fever-pains-of-hell-bodily` вЂ”[Zeezrom's sin "did harrow up his mind... scorched with a burning heat"; unresolved guilt (esp. over harming others) sickens the body; the pains of hell (14:6) made literal]в†’ 15:3-5 (Alma 14:6; 36:12-16; Ps 32:3-4; 38:3-8)
- `doctrine:healed-by-faith-body-and-soul-together` вЂ”[the fever caused by guilt is cured by "faith which is in Christ"; the redemption that cleanses the conscience heals the flesh it scorched; salvation and healing one act]в†’ 15:6-11 (Mark 9:23; 2:1-12; Acts 3:1-8; Alma 7:11-13)
- `event:complete-conversion-bribing-lawyer-to-preacher` вЂ”[Zeezrom: bribe в†’ tremble в†’ inquire в†’ harrowed guilt + confession в†’ fever в†’ healed в†’ baptized в†’ "began to preach"; the chief accuser becomes a herald]в†’ 15:11-12 (Alma 11-14; Mosiah 27; Acts 9) вЂ” no one too far gone
- `theme:hardened-collective-refuses-what-the-individual-receives` вЂ”[Zeezrom turns from the depths; Ammonihah "ascribing all the power... to the devil" (Matt 12:24, the Beelzebub move); the anti-Salem]в†’ 15:15 (Matt 12:24-32; Alma 13:18; 16:9-11) вЂ” the difference is the hardening (12:10-11)
- `theme:cost-of-discipleship-forsaking-all` вЂ”[Amulek "forsaken all his gold, silver... rejected by once-friends and by his father and his kindred"; the reluctant convert paid everything once he stopped refusing]в†’ 15:16 (Luke 14:33; 18:28-30; Matt 19:29; Alma 10:4)
- `theme:bear-the-burden-of-the-brother-who-paid-the-cost` вЂ”[Alma takes the bereft Amulek "to his own house... strengthened him in the Lord"; the baptismal covenant (Mosiah 18:8) lived between the missionaries]в†’ 15:18 (Mosiah 18:8-9; Gal 6:2; 2 Tim 1:16)

### from Alma 16
- `event:Ammonihah-destroyed-in-one-day` вЂ”[the scoff of 9:4 fulfilled in its own unit; the city "which they said God could not destroy" left desolate in one day; "every living soul" reckons 14:11]в†’ 16:9-11 (Alma 9:4; 14:8-11; Jer 19:7)

- `theme:seek-the-prophet-vs-harden-against-him` вЂ”[Zoram consults Alma and recovers every captive ("not one soul... lost"); Ammonihah hardened against the same prophet and perished]в†’ 16:5-9 (Alma 9:1-6; 2 Kgs 6:8-12)
- `doctrine:Spirit-poured-out-to-prepare-hearts` вЂ”[the inverse of the chains of hell (12:9-11): God softens the soil *before* the word, that hearts "might not be hardened... but receive the word with joy, and as a branch be grafted into the true vine"]в†’ 16:16-17 (Acts 16:14; Jacob 5:24; Alma 12:9-11; Mosiah 18:27)
- `prophecy:Christ-will-appear-after-his-resurrection` вЂ”[the 3 Nephi visit preached as settled hope in the peace years]в†’ 16:20 (Alma 7:8; 2 Ne 26:9; 3 Ne 11:8)

### from Alma 17
- `theme:the-tradition-is-the-target-not-the-people` вЂ”[the mission prays to dislodge "the baseness of the traditions of their fathers, which were not correct" вЂ” the grievance narrative, not the blood]в†’ 17:9 (Alma 3:11; Mosiah 10:12-17) вЂ” cure to the mos10 disease

- `doctrine:miracle-in-service-of-relationship-in-service-of-belief` вЂ”[Ammon's heart "swollen with joy" at the scattered flocks: the rescue is to "win the hearts... that I may lead them to believe in my words"; the defense is a sermon's prologue]в†’ 17:29 (2 Kgs 5:8; Alma 18)
- `event:waters-of-Sebus` вЂ”[the well-deliverance type-scene; the stranger proves himself at the water and is brought into the household; restraint inside power вЂ” "slew none save... their leader," smote off arms]в†’ 17:26-39 (Ex 2:17; Mosiah 28:7; Alma 19:22-23)

### from Alma 18

- `event:Lamoni-falls-as-if-dead` вЂ”[believes в†’ "O Lord, have mercy... upon me, and my people" в†’ falls as if dead two days; sets the pattern his father repeats]в†’ 18:40-43 (Alma 19:1; 22:18; Acts 9:4)

### from Alma 20

### from Alma 21

- `theme:denying-prophecy-to-immunize-the-present` вЂ”["We do not believe in these foolish traditions... neither do we believe that... our fathers did know concerning... that which is to come"; cut the cord to revelation so the future can't indict you]в†’ 21:8 (Jacob 7:2; Alma 30:13-16; 2 Pet 3:3-4)

- `event:Lamoni-decrees-religious-freedom` вЂ”[the convert-king refuses Ammon's servanthood (relationship transfigured) and legislates "the liberty of worshiping the Lord their God according to their desires"; the gospel that freed his soul becomes law freeing his people's worship]в†’ 21:19-22 (Alma 17:25; A of F 1:11; D&C 134:1-4)

### from Alma 22
- `doctrine:give-away-not-give-up-and-not-then` вЂ”["I will give away all my sins to know thee, and that I may be raised"; "give away" (discard) not "give up" (surrender); the conjunction is and-not-then вЂ” repentance and revelation one motion, not a bargain; struck down instantly]в†’ 22:18 (study:give-away-all-my-sins; Matt 13:46; Alma 5:14)
- `theme:the-conversion-method-is-reproducible` вЂ”[Aaron repeats Ammon's exact play on a second king: Great Spirit в†’ God в†’ creation в†’ fall в†’ plan of redemption в†’ struck down в†’ raised в†’ household converted; the method is the plan taught from where the hearer stands]в†’ 22:7-23 (Alma 18:24-39; Acts 2:37)
- `theme:the-seed-of-love-works-in-the-dark` вЂ”[the king "troubled in mind because of the generosity and the greatness of the words of thy brother Ammon" before Aaron spoke; the ch 20 selfless love had already turned the soil]в†’ 22:3 (Alma 20:26; 1 Cor 3:6)
- `theme:rich-young-ruler-rewritten` вЂ”["I will give up all that I possess, yea, I will forsake my kingdom"; the king volunteers the kingdom the rich young ruler couldn't part with]в†’ 22:15 (Matt 19:16-22; 13:44-46; Luke 18:28-30)
- `doctrine:atonement-creed-could-not-merit-of-himself` вЂ”["since man had fallen he could not merit anything of himself; but the sufferings and death of Christ atone... the sting of death should be swallowed up in the hopes of glory"; grace + resurrection in two breaths]в†’ 22:14 (Eph 2:8-9; 1 Cor 15:55; 2 Ne 9:8-9; Alma 34:9)
- `event:over-king-and-whole-household-converted` вЂ”[raised by Aaron ("Stand"), the king ministers, "his whole household were converted," then decrees religious freedom kingdom-wide]в†’ 22:22-27 (Alma 19:29-30; 21:21-22; 23:1-4)
- `reference:land-division-narrow-neck` вЂ”[Mormon orients the reader: Nephite/Lamanite division, the narrow strip + "small neck of land," Bountiful/Desolation; Desolation = the Jaredite death-land]в†’ 22:27-34 (Mosiah 8:7-12; 28:17-19; Ether 6-7; Alma 50:34)

### from Alma 23
- `doctrine:conversion-that-lays-down-the-weapon-never-falls-away` вЂ”["as many... as were converted unto the Lord, never did fall away" вЂ” bound directly to "they did lay down the weapons of their rebellion"; belief that buries the sword can't reverse, belief that keeps it stays reversible]в†’ 23:6-7 (Alma 24:17-19; 27:27; Luke 9:62)
- `theme:the-grievance-dissolved-into-all-brethren` вЂ”[the king who recited the grievance now legislates "that they might be convinced that they were all brethren" вЂ” the exact negation of "sons of a liar"]в†’ 23:3 (Alma 20:10-13; Mosiah 10:12-17; 28:2)
- `theme:apostates-dont-convert-natives-do` вЂ”["the Amalekites were not converted, save only one; neither were any of the Amulonites," while thousands of born-Lamanites convert and never fall away; the apostate-Nehorite harder than the native]в†’ 23:14 (Alma 21:3; Mosiah 23:31-39; 24:30)
- `event:new-name-Anti-Nephi-Lehies` вЂ”[the converts take a name "that they might be distinguished," "no more called Lamanites"; renouncing the grievance-identity Laman's name carried, aligning toward Nephi and Lehi the faithful founders]в†’ 23:16-17 (Jacob 1:13; Alma 24:1; Mosiah 5:7-8)
- `doctrine:the-curse-lifted-as-enmity-and-idleness-reversed` вЂ”["industrious... friendly with the Nephites... the curse of God did no more follow them"; three markers all behavioral/relational, not physical; the chapter's own footnote ties it to 2 Ne 30:6 (curse taken away в†’ "pure")]в†’ 23:18 (2 Ne 5:24; 30:6; 1 Ne 2:23; 3 Ne 2:15) вЂ” 5:21-study datapoint: curse = enmity/idleness, removed on conversion

### from Alma 24
- `doctrine:bury-the-weapons-lest-the-cleansing-not-hold` вЂ”[forgiven of murder, they fear "if we should stain our swords again they can no more be washed bright through the blood of the Son"; absolute pacifism from people who know what their hands did]в†’ 24:12-13 (D&C 42:18; Heb 10:26; Rev 1:5)
- `theme:covenant-as-threefold-reversal-of-the-grievance` вЂ”["rather than shed the blood of their brethren they would give up their own lives; and rather than take away from a brother they would give unto him; and rather than spend their days in idleness they would labor"; every grievance-vice inverted]в†’ 24:18 (Alma 17:14; 23:18; Mosiah 10:12-17)
- `event:unresisting-martyrdom-converts-the-killers` вЂ”[they prostrate and "praised God even in the very act of perishing"; the attackers, "stung for the murders," throw down their weapons and convert; you cannot keep killing people who lie down and praise God]в†’ 24:21-25 (Matt 5:39; Luke 23:34; Acts 7:60)
- `doctrine:martyrdom-is-net-positive` вЂ”["the people of God were joined that day by more than the number who had been slain"; 1,005 dead, "more than a thousand brought to the knowledge of the truth"; the buried sword converted more than the drawn sword ever did]в†’ 24:26-27 (Isa 57:1; Rev 14:13; John 12:24)
- `doctrine:apostasy-from-light-is-worse-than-never-knowing` вЂ”["after a people have been once enlightened... and then have fallen away... they become more hardened... worse than though they had never known"; killers are Nehorite apostates, converts are native Lamanites]в†’ 24:28-30 (Heb 10:26; 2 Pet 2:20-21; Matt 12:45; Alma 47:36)
- `theme:buried-weapons-covenant-echoes-forward` вЂ”[the oath binding the fathers; remembered in Helaman's day as the mark of true conversion; the sons not under it become the stripling warriors]в†’ 24:17-19 (Hel 15:7-9; Alma 53:11; 56:47)

### fold-back: studies/alma17-26_lamanite-conversion-and-the-grievance-cure.md (Sonnet spin-off, all 6 load-bearing quotes verified vs own fetch)
- `study:alma17-26-grievance-cure` вЂ”[thesis: the four-century grievance tradition broke because the missionaries did four things it had no defense for вЂ” went as SERVANTS not conquerors (inverting the power-relation it was built on), told the TRUE story incl. Laman/Lemuel's rebellions (not counter-accusation), REFRAMED the wound via creation-fall-redemption (making Nephite-vs-Lamanite secondary), and the converts REFUSED THE SWORD (24) so the tradition could no longer call them bloodthirsty]в†’ Alma 17-26 (builds on studies/mos10 grievance diagnosis)
- `study:alma17-26-grievance-cure` вЂ”[load-bearing verified quotes]в†’ 17:11 (patient/long-suffering) В· 19:9 (faith on testimony alone) В· 22:13 (creationв†’redemption reframe) В· 22:18 (give away all my sins) В· 24:18 (rather give up own lives) В· 24:25 (killers stung, throw down weapons)

### from Alma 25
- `doctrine:prophecy-fulfilled-as-a-pattern-across-generations` вЂ”[Abinadi's "what ye shall do unto me shall be a type of things to come" вЂ” his death by fire prefigured the priests' seed burning believers, then "scattered... as a sheep having no shepherd"; ran true ~60 years later]в†’ 25:9-12 (Mosiah 13:10; 17:15-20; Matt 9:36)
- `theme:sin-and-its-judgment-both-have-descendants` вЂ”[the seed of the men who burned Abinadi burn believers in turn, then are hunted and slain; the violence the priests introduced propagated down their line and consumed them]в†’ 25:4-9 (Mosiah 23:35; Ex 20:5; Alma 24:30)
- `doctrine:law-of-moses-as-type-not-salvation` вЂ”["they did not suppose that salvation came by the law of Moses; but the law of Moses did serve to strengthen their faith in Christ"; the converts grasp the forms-as-type the Nehorites never did]в†’ 25:15-16 (Gal 3:24; 2 Ne 11:4; Jacob 4:5; Mosiah 13:27-33)
- `theme:the-cure-spreads-through-the-war` вЂ”[the defeated Lamanites come home, join the people of God, "bury their weapons of war, according as their brethren had"; every wave of violence yields more converts]в†’ 25:13-14 (Alma 24:26; 23:6; 17:9)
- `theme:counterfeit-forms-vs-forms-that-point-to-Christ` вЂ”[the Amalekites kept synagogues/worship as an end (21:6); the converts keep the law knowing it is "a type of his coming"; same ritual, opposite direction]в†’ 25:15-16 (Alma 21:6; 2 Ne 25:24-27)

### from Alma 26
- `doctrine:boast-in-God-not-self-strength-through-nothing` вЂ”[Aaron: "thy joy doth carry thee away unto boasting"; Ammon: "I know that I am nothing; as to my strength I am weak; therefore... I will boast of my God, for in his strength I can do all things"; the "all things" available only from zero]в†’ 26:10-12 (Philip 4:13; 2 Cor 12:9-10; Jer 9:24; 1 Ne 17:3)
- `doctrine:chains-of-hell-loosed` вЂ”["he has loosed our brethren from the chains of hell"; the Alma 12 binding reversed; two encirclements вЂ” "everlasting darkness" vs "the matchless bounty of his love"]в†’ 26:13-15 (Alma 12:11; 5:7-9, 26; 2 Ne 1:13)
- `doctrine:only-the-penitent-knows` вЂ”["what natural man... knoweth these things? none... save it be the penitent"; repentance is the organ by which the mysteries become visible; Amalekites couldn't, Lamanites could]в†’ 26:21-22 (1 Cor 2:11-14; Alma 12:9-11; Jacob 4:8)
- `theme:the-sword-vs-the-saving` вЂ”[the Nephites mocked ("destroy them... lest they overrun us"); Ammon: "not with the intent to destroy our brethren, but... that perhaps we might save some few"; the sword never converted a Lamanite, the saving converted thousands]в†’ 26:23-26 (Alma 24:26; Matt 5:44; Mosiah 28:1-3)
- `theme:Lamanite-love-exceeds-Nephite-love` вЂ”["has there been so great love in all the land? Nay... even among the Nephites... they would take up arms... but how many of these have laid down their lives"; the despised people out-love the covenant people]в†’ 26:33-34 (Alma 19:10; 24:21-22; John 15:13)
- `doctrine:God-mindful-of-every-people` вЂ”["God is mindful of every people... he numbereth his people, and his bowels of mercy are over all the earth"; the Lamanites a lost branch of the olive tree, remembered all along]в†’ 26:36-37 (2 Ne 26:33; Jonah 4:11; Acts 10:35; Jacob 5:25) вЂ” 5:21-study datapoint
- `event:Ammon-almost-turned-back` вЂ”["when our hearts were depressed, and we were about to turn back, the Lord comforted us... bear with patience thine afflictions, and I will give unto you success"]в†’ 26:27 (Alma 17:10-11; 1 Ne 17:3; D&C 6:36)

### from Alma 27
- `theme:protect-the-pacifist-without-arming-him` вЂ”[facing a second slaughter, Ammon doesn't arm them (breaking their covenant) but removes them to a refuge; "Get this people out of this land, that they perish not"]в†’ 27:3-12 (Alma 24:17-19; Matt 10:23; D&C 98:32-38)
- `doctrine:you-cannot-repay-murder-only-be-received` вЂ”[the king offers his people as slaves "until we repair... the many murders"; Ammon refuses (no slaves), "rely upon the mercies of our brethren"; repentance can't square the account, only throw itself on mercy]в†’ 27:6-9 (Mosiah 29:32; Luke 7:42; Eph 2:8-9)
- `theme:the-armed-bear-the-sword-for-the-unarmed-by-conscience` вЂ”[the Nephites vote to give Jershon and "set our armies between" the people of Ammon and danger, so the pacifists never break their vow; the armed bleed so the unarmed can keep conscience]в†’ 27:21-24 (Alma 43:11-13; 53:11-17; 56:47)
- `doctrine:joy-proportional-to-repentance` вЂ”[Ammon "swallowed up in the joy of his God, even to the exhausting of his strength... fell again to the earth"; only his joy exceeded his strength; "joy which none receiveth save it be the truly penitent"; the most-forgiven feels it hardest]в†’ 27:17-18 (Alma 26:21; 18:42; Luke 7:47)
- `doctrine:resurrection-empties-death-of-terror` вЂ”["they never did look upon death with any degree of terror, for their hope and views of Christ and the resurrection; therefore, death was swallowed up to them by the victory of Christ"; why they could lie down and die]в†’ 27:28 (1 Cor 15:54-57; Mosiah 16:7-8; Alma 24:22)
- `event:new-name-the-people-of-Ammon` вЂ”[named for the missionary who brought them; the identity reconstruction (Anti-Nephi-Lehi в†’ people of Ammon) completed вЂ” named, finally, for the love that found them]в†’ 27:26 (Alma 23:17; Mosiah 1:11-12; 5:7-12)
- `theme:firm-in-the-faith-even-unto-the-end` вЂ”["perfectly honest and upright in all things... firm in the faith of Christ, even unto the end"; the never-fall-away of 23:6 confirmed as settled fact]в†’ 27:27 (Alma 23:6; Hel 15:8; 3 Ne 6:14)

### from Alma 28
- `doctrine:the-two-mournings-fear-vs-hope` вЂ”[same death: some mourn "because they have reason to fear... a state of endless wo," others "rejoice and exult in the hope... raised to dwell at the right hand of God"; the variable is whether the gospel reached the dead]в†’ 28:11-12 (Alma 11:41; D&C 42:45; 1 Thes 4:13)
- `theme:Mormon-lingers-on-the-cost` вЂ”["the cry of widows mourning for their husbands... fathers mourning for their sons"; the protection pledge of ch 27 paid in Nephite blood; the record won't rush past grief]в†’ 28:4-6 (Alma 27:23; Matt 5:4; Gen 50:10)
- `doctrine:inequality-is-self-made-not-God-imposed` вЂ”["how great the inequality of man is because of sin and transgression, and the power of the devil... cunning plans"; eternal outcomes diverge by agency + the snare, not divine favoritism (cf. God esteems all flesh in one)]в†’ 28:13 (1 Ne 17:35; 2 Ne 9:28; Alma 3:19) вЂ” 5:21-study thread: self-authored, not God-imposed
- `theme:sorrow-and-joy-held-together` вЂ”["the great reason of sorrow, and also of rejoicing вЂ” sorrow because of death... and joy because of the light of Christ unto life"; both carried, neither cancels]в†’ 28:14 (Eccl 3:4; John 16:20-22; 2 Cor 6:10)
- `theme:the-call-to-labor-in-the-vineyard` вЂ”["the great call of diligence of men to labor in the vineyards of the Lord"; conversion is the labor of changing which mourning a family will one day do]в†’ 28:14 (Jacob 5:61-72; D&C 4:4; Alma 26:5)

### from Alma 29
- `doctrine:wanting-more-than-your-allotment-is-sin` вЂ”["O that I were an angel... cry repentance unto every people!" в†’ "I am a man, and do sin in my wish; for I ought to be content with the things which the Lord hath allotted unto me"; even holy ambition becomes sin when it refuses the bounds of stewardship]в†’ 29:1-6 (Mosiah 4:27; D&C 107:99; 1 Cor 12:14-18) вЂ” the pacing covenant from the inside
- `doctrine:God-grants-according-to-desire` вЂ”["he granteth unto men according to their desire... according to their wills, whether they be unto salvation or unto destruction"; judgment as God ratifying the desire a life cultivated; why angelic compulsion would be wrong вЂ” it overrides agency]в†’ 29:4-5 (2 Ne 2:27; Ps 37:4; Alma 41:5)
- `doctrine:God-teaches-every-nation-in-its-own-tongue` вЂ”["the Lord doth grant unto all nations, of their own nation and tongue, to teach his word... all that he seeth fit"; the distributed work вЂ” you are not the only instrument; relief not defeat]в†’ 29:8 (2 Ne 29:12; 3 Ne 26:8; D&C 90:11; Acts 2:6) вЂ” 5:21-adjacent
- `theme:scale-ambition-to-one-soul-through-your-calling` вЂ”["why should I desire more than to perform the work to which I have been called?... this is my glory, that perhaps I may be an instrument... to bring some soul to repentance"; "some soul" replaces "every people"]в†’ 29:6-9 (Alma 26:12; D&C 18:15-16; Luke 15:7)
- `theme:joy-fuller-in-others-success` вЂ”["I do not joy in my own success alone, but my joy is more full because of the success of my brethren... my soul is carried away, even to the separation of it from the body"; the corrected ambition rejoices hardest in what others did]в†’ 29:14-16 (Alma 27:17; Philip 1:18; 3 John 1:4)

### from Alma 30
- `doctrine:no-law-against-belief-punish-crimes-not-faith` вЂ”["there was no law against a man's belief... a man was punished only for the crimes which he had done; therefore all men were on equal grounds"; the God-ordained order refuses to criminalize unbelief вЂ” compelled belief is no belief]в†’ 30:7-11 (Alma 1:17; Josh 24:15; D&C 134:4; A of F 1:11)
- `theme:the-complete-anti-Christ-creed` вЂ”[no prophecy, "ye cannot know of things which ye do not see," faith as "a frenzied mind," "every man conquered according to his strength... whatsoever a man did was no crime," "when a man was dead, that was the end"; the full secular-materialist package]в†’ 30:13-18 (2 Ne 28:5-9; Jacob 7:7; Morm 8:31; Alma 1:4)
- `theme:accusation-by-projection-priestcraft` вЂ”[Korihor charges the true priests with Nehor's actual crime ("glut yourselves with the labors of their hands"); refuted: "I have never received so much as even one senine for my labor"]в†’ 30:27-35 (Alma 1:4, 16; Mosiah 18:24; Acts 20:34; 1 Thes 2:9)
- `doctrine:all-things-denote-there-is-a-God` вЂ”["what evidence have ye that there is no God... ye have none, save it be your word only"; "all things denote there is a God... the planets which move in their regular form do witness"; design argument + burden of proof on the denier]в†’ 30:40-44 (Ps 14:1; Job 12:7-10; Moses 6:63; Hel 12:11-15; Rom 1:20)
- `doctrine:argument-before-sign-reason-first` вЂ”[Alma engages the evidence ("thou hast had signs enough") and gives the sign only when Korihor demands it + danger is clear; "better that thy soul should be lost than... bringing many souls down to destruction"]в†’ 30:37-47 (Matt 12:39; John 6:30; D&C 46:9; Jacob 7:13-21)
- `doctrine:unbelief-as-chosen-lie-believed-through-success` вЂ”["I know that thou believest, but thou art possessed with a lying spirit" в†’ "I always knew that there was a God... pleasing unto the carnal mind... until... I verily believed that they were true"; success laundered the lie into conviction]в†’ 30:42, 52-53 (2 Cor 11:14; Jacob 7:14; 2 Ne 28:5-9)
- `theme:the-devil-abandons-his-children` вЂ”[Korihor begging house to house, then "run upon and trodden down"; "the devil will not support his children at the last day, but doth speedily drag them down to hell"; paid by the master you serve]в†’ 30:56-60 (Alma 3:27; 5:41-42; D&C 29:45; Jacob 7:20)

### from Alma 31
- `theme:false-worship-as-inversion-of-true` вЂ”[fixed memorized prayer, one-man high stand, "a chosen and a holy people," elect/damned decree, "no Christ"/"a spirit forever," home and silent till next week; a perfect negative image of the gospel]в†’ 31:12-23 (Matt 6:5-7; Luke 18:11; Isa 29:13; James 1:22)
- `doctrine:election-by-pride-vs-mercy` вЂ”["thou hast elected us that we shall be saved, whilst all around us are elected to be cast... down to hell"; double-predestination as the rich man's self-justification вЂ” wealth proof of election, poverty proof of damnation]в†’ 31:16-18, 24-25 (Luke 18:9-14; Alma 32:2-5; Jacob 2:13-21)
- `theme:the-two-prayers-self-vs-others` вЂ”[the Rameumptom prays against the outsider; Alma prays for the people who pray against him вЂ” "their souls are precious, and many of them are our brethren"; true worship told from false by which way the prayer points]в†’ 31:16-18 vs 31:30-35 (Matt 5:44; Luke 23:34; Alma 26:26)
- `doctrine:the-word-more-powerful-than-the-sword` вЂ”["the preaching of the word had... more powerful effect upon the minds of the people than the sword"; a missionary answer to a military threat]в†’ 31:5 (Alma 26:26; Hel 5:50-52; Heb 4:12)
- `doctrine:affliction-swallowed-in-the-joy-of-Christ` вЂ”[they "suffer no manner of afflictions, save it were swallowed up in the joy of Christ... because he prayed in faith"; absorbed not removed]в†’ 31:36-38 (Mosiah 24:13-15; Matt 5:10-12; Alma 33:23)

### from Alma 32
- `doctrine:faith-is-hope-in-unseen-things-which-are-true` вЂ”["faith is not to have a perfect knowledge of things... if ye have faith ye hope for things which are not seen, which are true"; the object matters вЂ” hope aimed at unseen *realities*, not credulity about anything invisible]в†’ 32:21 (Heb 11:1; Ether 12:6; John 20:29)
- `doctrine:the-entry-bar-is-only-desire` вЂ”["even if ye can no more than desire to believe, let this desire work in you, even until ye believe"; faith democratized вЂ” accessible to the poor, requiring only a desire + willingness to experiment]в†’ 32:27 (Mark 9:24; Alma 22:15; Matt 5:6)
- `doctrine:the-seed-experiment` вЂ”[plant the word; if good it "will begin to swell within your breasts... enlarge my soul... enlighten my understanding"; "is not this real? Yea, because it is light... discernible"; inward evidence answers Korihor's empiricism]в†’ 32:28-35 (Matt 13:3-8; Luke 8:11; Alma 30:43-48)
- `doctrine:experimental-knowledge-of-that-thing-not-all` вЂ”["your knowledge is perfect in that thing, and your faith is dormant"; the experiment yields real knowledge of the tested thing, faith remains for the rest]в†’ 32:34-36 (Ether 3:19; Alma 32:21)
- `doctrine:faith-must-be-nourished-or-it-withers` вЂ”[neglected, the tree withers вЂ” "not because the seed was not good... but because your ground is barren, and ye will not nourish the tree"; a failed faith is usually untended ground, not a false word]в†’ 32:37-41 (Matt 13:5-6, 20-21; Col 1:6; 1 Ne 8:10-18)
- `theme:worship-not-confined-to-building-or-week` вЂ”["do ye suppose that ye cannot worship God save it be in your synagogues only?... that ye must not worship God only once in a week?"; the Rameumptom cage broken in two questions]в†’ 32:10-11 (Alma 31:13-23; 33:3-11; John 4:21-24)
- `doctrine:compelled-vs-voluntary-humility` вЂ”["compelled to be humble blessed are ye... but blessed are they who humble themselves without being compelled"; affliction is humility's teacher of last resort; the wise choose it first]в†’ 32:13-16 (Matt 5:3-5; Ether 12:27; Hel 12:3)
- `theme:the-word-comes-through-the-overlooked` вЂ”[God imparts his word "by angels unto men, yea, not only men but women also... little children... confound the wise and the learned"; faith bypasses the elect's hierarchy]в†’ 32:23 (Matt 11:25; Luke 10:21; 1 Cor 1:27; 3 Ne 26:14-16)

### from Alma 33
- `doctrine:worship-is-bound-to-no-place` вЂ”[Zenos heard "in the wilderness... in my field... in my house... in my closet... in the midst of thy congregations... when I have been cast out"; God is not in the building вЂ” the Rameumptom cage refuted by the scripture the Zoramites claim to revere]в†’ 33:3-11 (Matt 6:5-6; John 4:21-24; Alma 32:10-11)
- `doctrine:every-mercy-is-because-of-the-Son` вЂ”["it is because of thy Son that thou hast been thus merciful... thou hast turned thy judgments away from me, because of thy Son"; a pre-Christian prophet grounds all answered prayer in the Atonement]в†’ 33:11-16 (Jacob 4:4; Mosiah 3:13; 1 Ne 19:10; Alma 34:7)
- `doctrine:the-scandal-of-the-simple-look` вЂ”[the brazen serpent "that whosoever would look upon it might live," yet "many were so hardened that they would not look, therefore they perished... because they did not believe that it would heal them"; the proud refuse the cure because it is too easy]в†’ 33:19-21 (Num 21:9; John 3:14; 1 Ne 17:41; 2 Ne 25:20; Hel 8:14)
- `doctrine:the-seed-is-the-word-of-Christ` вЂ”["begin to believe in the Son of God, that he will come to redeem his people, and that he shall suffer and die to atone for their sins; and that he shall rise again"; the ch 32 seed named specifically вЂ” the atoning, dying, rising Christ]в†’ 33:22-23 (Alma 32:28; 34:8-16; 2 Ne 25:26)
- `theme:burdens-made-light-through-the-joy-of-the-Son` вЂ”["may God grant unto you that your burdens may be light, through the joy of his Son... even all this can ye do if ye will"; the Mosiah 24 promise offered to the cast-out poor, on agency]в†’ 33:23 (Mosiah 24:13-15; Alma 31:38; Matt 11:28-30)

### from Alma 34
- `doctrine:the-atonement-must-be-infinite` вЂ”[a finite sacrifice (man/beast/fowl) pays only a finite debt вЂ” the law takes one life for one life; "there can be nothing which is short of an infinite atonement which will suffice for the sins of the world"; only the Son, "infinite and eternal"]в†’ 34:9-14 (2 Ne 9:7; 2 Ne 2:10; D&C 20:17; Heb 5:9)
- `doctrine:mercy-satisfies-justice-encircles-in-safety` вЂ”["mercy can satisfy the demands of justice, and encircles them in the arms of safety, while he that exercises no faith unto repentance is exposed to the whole law"; mercy pays justice in full, doesn't cancel it; conditional on faith unto repentance]в†’ 34:15-16 (Alma 42:13-25; Mosiah 15:27; 2 Ne 2:7-9)
- `doctrine:the-law-every-whit-points-to-the-sacrifice` вЂ”["this is the whole meaning of the law, every whit pointing to that great and last sacrifice"; the forms collapse without the Christ they prefigure вЂ” Zoramites kept forms, denied the referent]в†’ 34:13-14 (2 Ne 25:24-27; Mosiah 13:29-32; Alma 25:15-16)
- `theme:prayer-everywhere-over-everything-continually` вЂ”[cry over fields, flocks, household morning-midday-evening, against enemies + the devil, in closets + wilderness; "when you do not cry... let your hearts be full, drawn out in prayer continually for your welfare, and also... those around you"; the anti-Rameumptom]в†’ 34:17-27 (Alma 33:4-11; Matt 6:5-6; 1 Thes 5:17; 2 Ne 32:9)
- `doctrine:prayer-without-mercy-to-the-needy-is-hypocrisy` вЂ”["if ye turn away the needy... your prayer is vain... ye are as hypocrites who do deny the faith"; "if ye do not remember to be charitable, ye are as dross"; the Zoramites' own "dross" insult (32:3) reversed onto the uncharitable]в†’ 34:28-29 (Isa 58:3-7; Matt 15:7-8; James 2:15-16; Moroni 7:6-8; Alma 32:3)
- `doctrine:this-life-is-the-time-to-prepare` вЂ”["this life is the time for men to prepare to meet God... do not procrastinate the day of your repentance... then cometh the night of darkness wherein there can be no labor"]в†’ 34:31-33 (2 Cor 6:2; John 9:4; Eccl 9:10; Hel 13:38; D&C 45:2)
- `doctrine:the-spirit-you-die-with-persists` вЂ”["that same spirit which doth possess your bodies at the time that ye go out of this life... will have power to possess your body in that eternal world"; no deathbed reset вЂ” the character built here carries across]в†’ 34:34-35 (Mosiah 3:19; Rom 6:16; 2 Ne 28:19-23; Alma 40:14)
- `theme:dont-let-the-casting-out-make-you-like-them` вЂ”["do not revile against those who do cast you out because of your exceeding poverty, lest ye become sinners like unto them"; the oppressed warned not to let oppression turn their hearts bitter]в†’ 34:40-41 (Matt 5:44; Rom 12:21; Alma 24:17-19)

### from Alma 35
- `theme:the-word-destroys-craft` вЂ”["they were angry because of the word, for it did destroy their craft"; the leaders threatened in their priestcraft revenue, not their theology; a secret loyalty-poll and purge follow]в†’ 35:3-6 (Acts 19:23-27; Alma 1:16; 30:27-31)
- `theme:the-sheltered-become-shelterers` вЂ”[the people of Ammon, themselves once refugees given Jershon (ch 27), now "receive all the poor of the Zoramites... nourish them... clothe them... give unto them lands"; mercy received becomes mercy extended]в†’ 35:8-9 (Alma 27:21-26; Mosiah 4:26; 34:28; Matt 10:8)
- `theme:pacifism-was-a-covenant-not-a-blanket-rule` вЂ”[the people of Ammon (under the buried-weapons oath) give place to the Nephite armies; the new Zoramite converts (not under it) "have taken up arms to defend themselves, and their wives, and children"]в†’ 35:13-14 (Alma 24:17-19; 27:23-24; 43:45-47; 48:14)
- `theme:offended-by-the-strictness-of-the-word` вЂ”["the hearts of the people began to wax hard, and... began to be offended because of the strictness of the word"; the gospel that destroyed Zoramite craft also scandalizes Nephite comfort]в†’ 35:15 (John 6:60-66; Matt 13:21; 1 Ne 16:2; 2 Ne 9:40)
- `theme:pivot-from-public-mission-to-private-stewardship` вЂ”[grieved that the wide field is hardening, Alma "caused that his sons should be gathered together, that he might give unto them every one his charge, separately"; when you cannot soften a people, tend the few entrusted to you]в†’ 35:16 (Alma 36-42; Deut 6:6-7; D&C 68:25; 93:40-44)

### from Alma 36
- `structure:chiasmus-centered-on-the-cry` вЂ”[the chapter is a large chiasm вЂ” prosper/captivity/trials/born-of-God/destroy-the-church/racked... PIVOT (cry to Jesus vv17-18) ...joy/throne-vision/born-again/delivered/captivity/prosper; the bottom of the soul and its turning are the same moment, placed at the center not the end]в†’ 36:1-30 (Hebrew poetic form; Mosiah 5:10-12)
- `doctrine:pains-of-hell-are-memory-in-Gods-presence` вЂ”["harrowed up by the memory of my sins... the very thought of coming into the presence of my God did rack my soul with inexpressible horror"; wished to "become extinct both soul and body" rather than be judged; hell = the unendurable clarity of your own record in perfect light]в†’ 36:13-16 (Alma 12:14; Rev 6:16; D&C 19:11-18; 2 Ne 9:14)
- `doctrine:a-different-memory-is-the-rescue` вЂ”["I remembered also to have heard my father prophesy... concerning... Jesus Christ... to atone"; memory was the torment, a different memory the rescue; the word a parent planted surfaces when the child is drowning]в†’ 36:17 (Enos 1:3; 1 Ne 10:17-19; 2 Cor 7:10; Prov 22:6)
- `doctrine:the-cry-stripped-to-the-name-and-mercy` вЂ”["O Jesus, thou Son of God, have mercy on me, who am in the gall of bitterness, and am encircled about by the everlasting chains of death"; no bargain, no amends вЂ” just the name of Christ and a plea for mercy; the publican's prayer]в†’ 36:18 (Luke 18:13; Matt 15:22; Mosiah 4:2; Alma 12:11)
- `doctrine:joy-exactly-as-deep-as-the-pain` вЂ”["nothing so exquisite and bitter as were my pains... nothing so exquisite and sweet as was my joy"; the joy is the precise measure of the sorrow; the harrowing was the excavation that made room for it]в†’ 36:19-22 (Alma 27:17; 2 Cor 7:10; Ps 30:5; John 16:20-22)
- `event:longing-replaces-the-wish-to-be-banished` вЂ”[v15 wished to "become extinct... that I might not be brought to stand in the presence of my God"; v22 "my soul did long to be there"; the cry reversed the deepest direction of desire]в†’ 36:15, 22 (1 Ne 1:8; Isa 6:1-3; Rev 22:4)
- `doctrine:conversion-becomes-vocation` вЂ”["from that time even until now, I have labored without ceasing... that I might bring them to taste of the exceeding joy of which I did taste"; the joy is the engine of the life, not a private possession]в†’ 36:24-26 (Alma 29:9; Luke 22:32; 1 Pet 2:3)
- `doctrine:reproducible-conversion-tasted-eye-to-eye` вЂ”["many have been born of God, and have tasted as I have tasted, and have seen eye to eye as I have seen"; the seed experiment (32) confirmed from the far side вЂ” conversion is verifiable, not a one-off]в†’ 36:26 (Alma 32:28; Ps 34:8; 1 Pet 2:3)

### from Alma 37
- `doctrine:by-small-and-simple-things` вЂ”["by small and simple things are great things brought to pass... by very small means the Lord doth confound the wise and bringeth about the salvation of many souls"; the great work hides in the unimpressive instrument]в†’ 37:6-7 (1 Cor 1:27; 2:14; D&C 64:33; 2 Kgs 5:13)
- `doctrine:scriptures-preserve-memory-and-convert` вЂ”[the records "enlarged the memory of this people... convinced many"; "were it not for these things... Ammon... could not have convinced so many thousands of the Lamanites"; the whole grievance-cure rode on the plates]в†’ 37:8-9 (Alma 18:36; 22:12; Mosiah 1:3-5; Omni 1:17)
- `doctrine:teach-the-fruit-of-evil-not-the-recipe` вЂ”[keep the Jaredites' secret oaths "from this people... lest... they should fall into darkness also"; teach "their wickedness and their murders" so they "abhor" it, never the method]в†’ 37:21-32 (Hel 6:25-26; Ether 8:18-26; 2 Ne 4:31) вЂ” expose consequences, withhold the manual
- `doctrine:counsel-with-the-Lord-in-all-thy-doings` вЂ”["let all thy doings be unto the Lord... let the affections of thy heart be placed upon the Lord"; "Counsel with the Lord in all thy doings, and he will direct thee for good"; night-surrender + morning-thanks]в†’ 37:35-37 (Prov 3:5-6; Ps 37:5; D&C 6:36; Eccl 12:1)
- `doctrine:the-Liahona-as-type-of-the-word` вЂ”[the compass "did work for them according to their faith"; "it is as easy to give heed to the word of Christ... as it was for our fathers to give heed to this compass... if we will look we may live forever"]в†’ 37:38-46 (1 Ne 16:10, 28-29; 18:12; 2 Ne 5:12; Ps 119:105)
- `theme:the-failure-is-despising-the-easy-way` вЂ”["they were slothful... because those miracles were worked by small means... and then those marvelous works ceased"; "do not let us be slothful because of the easiness of the way"; the serpent/seed/Liahona вЂ” the failure is to despise the simple means for being simple]в†’ 37:41-46 (1 Ne 17:41; Alma 33:19-22; Matt 11:30; Luke 6:46-49)

### from Alma 38
- `doctrine:bridle-passions-that-ye-may-be-filled-with-love` вЂ”["see that ye bridle all your passions, that ye may be filled with love"; the bridle harnesses, doesn't kill вЂ” unbridled passion crowds love out; self-mastery is the precondition for the highest feeling]в†’ 38:12 (James 3:2-3; Gal 5:22-23; D&C 121:41-42)
- `theme:three-sons-three-different-words` вЂ”[warm approving charge to steady Shiblon vs. records-trust to Helaman vs. grieved correction to Corianton; love that pays attention doesn't say the same thing to every child (35:16 "separately")]в†’ 38:2-3 (Alma 35:16; 36-37; 39-42; Eph 6:4)
- `doctrine:no-other-way-but-Christ` вЂ”["there is no other way or means whereby man can be saved, only in and through Christ... he is the life and the light of the world"; Alma's failed flight from God is his proof]в†’ 38:9 (Alma 21:9; John 14:6; 2 Ne 31:21; Mosiah 3:17)
- `doctrine:conversion-is-pain-until-the-cry-then-peace` вЂ”["never, until I did cry out unto the Lord Jesus Christ for mercy, did I receive a remission... I did cry unto him and I did find peace to my soul"; the Alma 36 chiasmus told plain]в†’ 38:6-8 (Alma 36:17-20; Mosiah 4:1-3; Enos 1:4-8)
- `theme:inoculate-the-faithful-son-against-pride` вЂ”["Do not say: O God, I thank thee that we are better than our brethren; but rather... O Lord, forgive my unworthiness... acknowledge your unworthiness before God at all times"; the most faithful son warned against pride вЂ” it grows best in good soil]в†’ 38:11-14 (Alma 31:16; Luke 18:9-14; 1 Cor 10:12)

### from Alma 39
- `doctrine:the-sin-started-in-pride-not-appetite` вЂ”["thou didst go on unto boasting in thy strength and thy wisdom" precedes "forsake the ministry... after the harlot Isabel"; the exact warning Shiblon heeded (38:11); pride cleared the ground]в†’ 39:2-3 (Alma 38:11; Prov 16:18; 1 Cor 10:12)
- `doctrine:sexual-sin-ranks-third-because-of-the-power-it-misuses` вЂ”["most abominable above all sins save it be the shedding of innocent blood or denying the Holy Ghost"; the three gravest sins misuse life/light at the source вЂ” procreation is the power humans share most directly with God]в†’ 39:5-6 (D&C 64:10; Moroni 8:28; Gen 1:28)
- `doctrine:the-representatives-sin-costs-others-their-belief` вЂ”["how great iniquity ye brought upon the Zoramites; for when they saw your conduct they would not believe in my words"; the missionary's private sin has a body count of unbelief]в†’ 39:11 (2 Sam 12:14; Rom 2:21-24; 1 Cor 9:14; Matt 18:6)
- `theme:harrowing-the-soul-for-its-good` вЂ”["I would not dwell upon your crimes, to harrow up your soul, if it were not for your good"; the man harrowed three days himself knows the pain is the door to the cry; love that says the hard true thing]в†’ 39:7-8 (Alma 36:12-21; 2 Cor 7:8-10; Heb 12:6; Prov 27:6)
- `doctrine:repentance-includes-restitution-and-counsel` вЂ”["return unto them, and acknowledge your faults"; "counsel with your elder brothers... ye stand in need to be nourished by your brothers"; the proud son sent to submit to the brothers he outshone]в†’ 39:10-13 (Mosiah 27:35; Ezek 33:15; James 5:16; Prov 11:14)
- `theme:rebuild-the-belief-under-the-behavior` вЂ”[Corianton "marvels" at the doctrine; Alma discerns the sin had roots in doubt and answers it (40-42); a son falls when the framework that would hold him stops seeming real; rebuke + doctrine = one act of reclamation]в†’ 39:15-19 (Alma 40-42; Alma 29:8; Jacob 4:4-6)

### from Alma 40
- `doctrine:the-space-and-the-intermediate-state` вЂ”[at death spirits "taken home to that God who gave them life"; righteous to "paradise, a state of rest... peace," wicked to "outer darkness... awful, fearful looking for the fiery indignation"; both wait until the resurrection]в†’ 40:11-14 (Eccl 12:7; Luke 16:19-26; D&C 138; Alma 34:34)
- `doctrine:the-resurrection-restores-the-perfect-frame` вЂ”["every limb and joint shall be restored... even a hair of the head shall not be lost; but all things shall be restored to their proper and perfect frame"; the body redeemed not discarded вЂ” spirit + body reunited, glorified together]в†’ 40:23 (1 Cor 15:42-54; 2 Ne 9:13; Alma 11:43-45; Philip 3:21)
- `theme:prophetic-intellectual-honesty-revelation-vs-opinion` вЂ”["whether... one time, or a second... it mattereth not; for God knoweth"; "I do not say... I give it as my opinion"; a prophet flags the line between revealed and inferred вЂ” honesty makes the certainty more trustworthy]в†’ 40:5, 20-21 (D&C 9:8-9; 1 Cor 7:25; Jacob 4:13)
- `doctrine:resurrection-certain-the-floor-under-repentance` вЂ”[answering the doubt that death is the end (Korihor); "there is a time appointed that all shall rise... be reunited, both soul and body, and be brought to stand before God, and be judged"; re-laying the floor that makes repentance make sense]в†’ 40:4-21 (Alma 30:18; John 5:28-29; Alma 11:41-45)
- `theme:resurrection-makes-mortality-matter-forever` вЂ”["the righteous shall shine forth in the kingdom of God" vs the wicked "drink the dregs of a bitter cup"; all rise in a perfect frame but to divergent destinies, "judged according to their works"; the resurrection makes the stakes of now eternal]в†’ 40:25-26 (Dan 12:3; Matt 13:43; 1 Cor 6:9-10; Alma 41:3-5)

### from Alma 41
- `doctrine:wickedness-never-was-happiness` вЂ”["wickedness never was happiness" вЂ” not "won't be" but never WAS; the carnal state is "contrary to the nature of happiness"; sin and happiness are contradictory categories вЂ” the route can't reach the goal]в†’ 41:10-11 (Ps 32:10; Isa 57:21; Hel 13:38; Mosiah 3:19) вЂ” four-word demolition of the lie that sin is a shortcut to joy
- `doctrine:restoration-is-reciprocity-not-reset` вЂ”["the meaning of the word restoration is to bring back again evil for evil... good for that which is good... merciful for that which is merciful"; the same kind returned, not a thing placed opposite its nature вЂ” restored to yourself, not reset to happiness]в†’ 41:12-13 (Rev 22:12; Dan 12:10; Gal 6:7)
- `doctrine:you-are-restored-to-the-self-your-desires-built` вЂ”["raised to happiness according to his desires of happiness... the other to evil according to his desires of evil"; "they are their own judges"; judgment reveals the self you chose, God ratifying it]в†’ 41:3-7 (2 Ne 2:26-27; Alma 29:4-5; Hel 14:30-31)
- `doctrine:what-you-send-out-returns` вЂ”["see that you are merciful... and ye shall have mercy restored unto you again... that which ye do send out shall return unto you again"; the sowing/reaping law made universal вЂ” restoration is a tool, not just a verdict]в†’ 41:14-15 (Gal 6:7; Matt 5:7; 7:1-2; Prov 19:17; Eccl 11:1)
- `theme:bad-theology-cleared-the-way-for-bad-behavior` вЂ”["some have wrested the scriptures, and have gone far astray"; "do not risk one more offense... upon those points of doctrine, which ye have hitherto risked to commit sin"; Corianton rationalized THEN sinned вЂ” belief corrected before behavior could be]в†’ 41:1, 9 (2 Pet 3:16; Alma 39:2; 2 Ne 28:8)
- `theme:the-doctrine-condemns-the-unrepentant-and-saves-the-repentant` вЂ”["the word restoration more fully condemneth the sinner, and justifieth him not at all" вЂ” yet the same law saves the moment he turns and sends out mercy/justice/good; you get yourself back, so change the self you build]в†’ 41:15 (Alma 41:6; 42:22-24; Ezek 18:21-22)

### from Alma 42
- `doctrine:the-expulsion-was-mercy-it-created-the-space-to-repent` вЂ”[the cherubim + flaming sword kept Adam from the tree of life "lest he should... live forever... having no space for repentance"; the cutting-off created "a probationary time" вЂ” death itself is mercy, keeping the fall from becoming permanent]в†’ 42:2-7 (Gen 3:22-24; 2 Ne 2:21; Moses 4:31; Alma 12:23-24)
- `doctrine:law-punishment-repentance-chain` вЂ”["How could a man repent except he should sin? How could he sin if there was no law? How could there be a law save there was a punishment?"; remove the penalty and there's no law, no sin, no repentance вЂ” the thing Corianton wants gone is what makes mercy possible]в†’ 42:16-22 (Rom 4:15; 5:13; 2 Ne 2:13; 9:25-26; Gal 3:13)
- `doctrine:God-himself-pays-justice-so-mercy-can-act` вЂ”["God himself atoneth for the sins of the world... to appease the demands of justice, that God might be a perfect, just God, and a merciful God also"; he doesn't waive the penalty, he pays it вЂ” the cross makes God able to forgive AND remain just]в†’ 42:15 (Alma 34:15-16; 2 Ne 9:10; Mosiah 16:8; Isa 53:5-6)
- `doctrine:mercy-cannot-rob-justice` вЂ”["justice exerciseth all his demands, and also mercy claimeth all which is her own... do ye suppose that mercy can rob justice? Nay; not one whit. If so, God would cease to be God"; both fully satisfied by the atonement; mercy is the fruit of a price paid]в†’ 42:23-25 (Alma 34:15-16; 2 Ne 2:13; Mosiah 15:27; Rom 3:26)
- `theme:attacking-Gods-justice-to-excuse-oneself` вЂ”["ye do try to suppose that it is injustice that the sinner should be consigned to a state of misery"; "do not endeavor to excuse yourself... by denying the justice of God"; the doctrinal objection was scaffolding under the sin]в†’ 42:1, 30 (Rom 3:5; 2 Ne 26:7; 28:8; Mal 2:17)
- `doctrine:two-kinds-of-trouble-destructive-vs-redemptive` вЂ”["let these things trouble you no more, and only let your sins trouble you, with that trouble which shall bring you down unto repentance"; redirect from destructive worry (avoidance) to godly sorrow]в†’ 42:29 (2 Cor 7:10; Mormon 2:13; Alma 36:17-19)
- `theme:repentance-is-the-start-of-the-real-ministry` вЂ”["go thy way, declare the word with truth and soberness, that thou mayest bring souls unto repentance"; the vocation Alma found after his own conversion (36:24) handed to the son who strayed]в†’ 42:31 (Alma 36:24; Luke 22:32; John 21:15-17; D&C 11:15)

### from Alma 43
- `doctrine:the-better-cause-defensive-not-conquest` вЂ”["not fighting for monarchy nor power but... for their homes and their liberties, their wives and their children... their rites of worship and their church"; the cause makes the fighting righteous вЂ” defense, never conquest]в†’ 43:45-47 (D&C 98:23-48; Alma 48:14-16; Matt 5:39)
- `doctrine:the-law-of-war-bear-the-offense-then-defend` вЂ”["Inasmuch as ye are not guilty of the first offense, neither the second, ye shall not suffer yourselves to be slain... Ye shall defend your families even unto bloodshed"; bloodshed licensed only to the non-aggressor who has borne the provocation]в†’ 43:46-47 (D&C 98:23-36; 3 Ne 3:20-21; Morm 3:10-11)
- `theme:Moroni-prepares-armor-as-a-moral-act` вЂ”[breastplates/shields vs. the "naked" Lamanites; armor terrifies the larger army + saves lives ("now and then a man fell among the Nephites" vs. Lamanite death "almost at every stroke"); foresight is moral]в†’ 43:18-21, 37-38 (Alma 49:24; Eph 6:11-17; Prov 22:3)
- `theme:revelation-and-strategy-together` вЂ”[Moroni inquires of the Lord through Alma where to defend, AND "thought it no sin that he should defend them by stratagem"; divine guidance + lawful cunning, neither despised]в†’ 43:23-24, 30 (Judg 7:16-25; 2 Kgs 6:8-18; Josh 8:13)
- `theme:mercy-in-victory-stop-when-the-threat-is-contained` вЂ”[with the Lamanites surrounded and "struck with terror," Moroni "commanded his men that they should stop shedding their blood"; a war for protection sheathes the sword the instant protection is achieved]в†’ 43:54 (Alma 44:1-2; Deut 20:10-12; Prov 24:17)
- `theme:dissenters-drive-the-war` вЂ”[Zerahemnah appoints Amalekite/Zoramite apostates as chief captains "that he might preserve their hatred"; the dissenters "more wicked and murderous" than the native Lamanites вЂ” the 24:30 principle in arms]в†’ 43:6-8 (Alma 24:30; 47:36; 21:3-4)

### from Alma 44
- `doctrine:conditional-protection-faithful-or-fall` вЂ”["God will support, and keep, and preserve us, so long as we are faithful unto him... never will the Lord suffer that we shall be destroyed except we should fall into transgression and deny our faith"; the war is a barometer of national righteousness, not firepower]в†’ 44:3-4 (1 Ne 2:20-21; Alma 9:13; 2 Ne 1:20; Mosiah 1:7)
- `theme:two-readings-of-the-same-victory` вЂ”[Moroni: "the Lord is with us"; Zerahemnah: "it is your cunning... your breastplates and your shields that have preserved you"; the unbeliever stops at the visible cause and refuses the Author; the difference is in the eyes, not the evidence]в†’ 44:3, 9 (Alma 30:44; 18:35; 1 Cor 2:14; John 12:28-29)
- `theme:Moronis-word-binds-him` вЂ”[Moroni returns the weapons but then "I cannot recall the words which I have spoken... ye shall not depart except ye depart with an oath"; his own prior word binds him even to his constraint]в†’ 44:10-11 (Num 30:2; Matt 5:33-37; Eccl 5:4-5; Josh 9:18-20)
- `theme:mercy-with-a-limit-spare-the-person-not-the-threat` вЂ”[life freely offered for an oath, but no release without it вЂ” an enemy freed without a covenant will "come again to war"; mercy spares the person without pretending the threat isn't real]в†’ 44:6, 11 (Alma 43:54; Deut 20:10-12; Luke 14:31-32)
- `theme:repeated-mercy-stop-the-killing-when-the-enemy-yields` вЂ”[the sword goes up + comes down three times the moment the threat relents (43:54; 44:17, 20); "the work of death should cease again"; a war for peace keeps offering the off-ramp]в†’ 44:20 (Alma 43:54; Prov 24:17; Matt 5:7; Rom 12:18)

### from Alma 45
- `prophecy:Nephite-extinction-400-years` вЂ”["four hundred years from the time that Jesus Christ shall manifest himself... shall dwindle in unbelief... even until the people of Nephi shall become extinct... because they shall sin against so great light and knowledge"; the 24:30 principle at civilizational scale; Mormon records his own people's obituary]в†’ 45:10-14 (1 Ne 12:10-15; Hel 13:9; Morm 8:6; Alma 24:30)
- `event:Almas-translation-like-departure` вЂ”["he departed... and was never heard of more... taken up by the Spirit, or buried by the hand of the Lord, even as Moses"; the converted persecutor leaves the stage as Moses did]в†’ 45:18-19 (Deut 34:5-6; 2 Kgs 2:16; Mosiah 27:8-10)
- `doctrine:the-conditional-land-covenant` вЂ”["Cursed shall be the land... unto destruction, which do wickedly, when they are fully ripe... for the Lord cannot look upon sin with the least degree of allowance"; a standing condition re-triggered by each generation]в†’ 45:16 (2 Ne 1:7; Ether 2:8-12; D&C 1:31)
- `theme:the-prophecy-sealed-until-fulfilled` вЂ”["what I prophesy unto thee ye shall not make known... even until the prophecy is fulfilled; therefore write the words"; some truths sealed to be vindicated later, not proclaimed now]в†’ 45:9 (Dan 12:4, 9; Isa 29:11; Ether 4:5-7)
- `theme:the-pride-cycle-reignites-the-moment-deliverance-passes` вЂ”[v1 "exceedingly rejoiced... fast much and pray much" в†’ v24 "grew proud, being lifted up... because of their exceedingly great riches"; gratitude curdles into pride within one chapter; the Nephites survive the armies but not their own success]в†’ 45:1, 23-24 (Hel 12:1-3; 4 Ne 1:24-26; Deut 8:11-14; Alma 46:1-7)

### from Alma 46
- `doctrine:the-inner-threat-of-flattery-and-ambition` вЂ”[Amalickiah, "cunning device and many flattering words," wins the power-seeking lower judges by promising rulership; "the great wickedness one very wicked man can cause"; the internal demagogue more dangerous than the external army]в†’ 46:4-10 (Prov 29:5; Mosiah 29:17-18; Hel 2:4-5; 2 Sam 15:1-6)
- `theme:how-quick-to-forget-after-deliverance` вЂ”["thus we see how quick the children of men do forget the Lord their God, yea, how quick to do iniquity"; the forgetting follows the deliverance almost instantly]в†’ 46:7-8 (Hel 12:1-5; Deut 8:11-14; 4 Ne 1:24; Judg 2:10-12)
- `theme:prayer-before-the-banner` вЂ”[Moroni rends the coat, dons armor, names the title вЂ” then "bowed himself to the earth, and prayed mightily" BEFORE waving it; the cause consecrated in prayer before proclaimed in public]в†’ 46:12-13 (Alma 43:23; 1 Sam 7:9; 2 Chr 20:5-12)
- `doctrine:the-self-maledictory-covenant-of-liberty` вЂ”[the people rend their garments "as a covenant" вЂ” "the Lord should rend them even as they had rent their garments" if they transgress; enacting on a symbol what they invite on themselves; liberty bound to accountability, not unconditional]в†’ 46:19-22 (Gen 15:9-18; Jer 34:18-20; Alma 44:4)
- `theme:the-Joseph-remnant-typology-refuses-to-flatter` вЂ”[the rent coat of Joseph в†’ rent garments в†’ Moroni's rent coat; "a remnant of the seed of Joseph... preserved by the hand of God" вЂ” but "even it shall be ourselves if we do not stand fast"]в†’ 46:23-27 (Gen 37:31-36; 2 Ne 3:5; Jacob 5:43-45; Ether 13:6-7)
- `event:Christians-named` вЂ”[the true believers "took upon them, gladly, the name of Christ, or Christians as they were called"; the name given by outsiders, worn gladly by the faithful]в†’ 46:14-15 (Acts 11:26; Mosiah 5:7-12; Alma 48:10)
- `theme:the-hard-edge-of-wartime-liberty` вЂ”[the Amalickiahites who "would not enter into a covenant to support the cause of freedom... he caused to be put to death"; wartime sedition law with Amalickiah fleeing to raise the Lamanites вЂ” the record doesn't present its heroes as flawless]в†’ 46:35 (Mosiah 29:32; Alma 51:19-20; 62:9-10)

### from Alma 47
- `theme:come-down-from-the-mount` вЂ”[Lehonti safe "upon the top of the mount"; Amalickiah cannot reach him, so he sends four times "desiring him to come down... and bring his guards"; the fourth descent is his death вЂ” the adversary lures you off secure ground by small guarded compromises]в†’ 47:7-13 (Neh 6:2-3; Matt 4:5-7; Prov 4:14-15)
- `theme:poison-by-degrees` вЂ”[Amalickiah "caused that one of his servants should administer poison by degrees to Lehonti, that he died"; gradual hidden destruction, fatal before noticed вЂ” how corruption works on a soul that left its ground]в†’ 47:18 (Alma 54:7; 2 Pet 2:1-3; Song 2:15)
- `theme:treachery-weaponizes-trust` вЂ”[the king's command, Lehonti's deal, the token of peace, the pursuers' grief, the queen's witnesses вЂ” every trust converted into the means of destruction; ambition without conscience harvests trust rather than breaking it openly]в†’ 47:10-35 (2 Sam 13:3-14; Ps 41:9; Luke 22:48)
- `theme:accuse-the-innocent-of-your-own-crime` вЂ”[Amalickiah stabs the king, then "pretended to be wroth," blames the king's servants, sends the loyal to pursue the innocent; the murderer becomes the chief mourner and avenger]в†’ 47:24-30 (Gen 37:31-33; 1 Kgs 21:8-13; Prov 6:16-19)
- `doctrine:apostate-worse-strange-to-relate` вЂ”["instructed in the same knowledge of the Lord, nevertheless, it is strange to relate... they became more wild, wicked and ferocious than the Lamanites"; the rejected light becomes its own fuel; the most dangerous enemy is a Nephite who left]в†’ 47:36 (Alma 24:30; Heb 10:26; 2 Pet 2:20-21; Matt 12:43-45)
- `theme:Amalickiah-as-anti-Moroni` вЂ”[Amalickiah works by secret embassy, poison, lying servants; Moroni rends his coat in public + prays before he acts; treachery vs transparency, the two faces of leadership in the war record]в†’ 47:10, 34 (Alma 46:11-13; John 3:20-21; Prov 10:9)

### from Alma 48
- `theme:greatness-is-character-not-capacity` вЂ”["while Amalickiah had... been obtaining power by fraud and deceit, Moroni, on the other hand, had been preparing the minds of the people to be faithful"; same capacity, opposite direction вЂ” the will's object, not the talent, separates them]в†’ 48:7 (Alma 47:4; D&C 121:39-40; Luke 16:10)
- `doctrine:if-all-men-were-like-Moroni-hell-would-be-shaken` вЂ”["if all men had been... like unto Moroni... the very powers of hell would have been shaken forever; yea, the devil would never have power over the hearts of the children of men"; not skill but character вЂ” a world of Moronis gives the devil nowhere to land]в†’ 48:17 (1 Ne 22:26; 3 Ne 6:15; D&C 35:24; Moroni 1:1) вЂ” Mormon names his son after this man
- `doctrine:the-Nephite-war-faith-defense-never-offense` вЂ”["never to give an offense... never to raise the sword except it were against an enemy, except it were to preserve their lives"; "his heart did glory... not in the shedding of blood but in doing good, in preserving his people"]в†’ 48:14-16 (D&C 98:16, 23-33; Alma 43:46-47; 3 Ne 3:21)
- `theme:the-general-and-the-preacher-are-equals` вЂ”["Helaman and his brethren were no less serviceable unto the people than was Moroni"; saving souls by the word and saving lives by the shield are the same order of service]в†’ 48:18-19 (Alma 28:8; 1 Cor 12:4-7; D&C 4:2)
- `theme:the-reluctant-warrior-grieves-the-unprepared-dead` вЂ”[the Nephites "sorry to be the means of sending so many of their brethren... unprepared to meet their God" вЂ” yet "could not suffer" their families to be massacred; fight without ever loving it, grieving the souls you take]в†’ 48:23-24 (Alma 28:11-12; Ezek 33:11; D&C 42:45; Luke 19:41)
- `theme:competence-in-service-of-love-not-the-reverse` вЂ”[Moroni's strength, understanding, labor all aimed at "the welfare and safety of his people"; the competence serves the love, not the love the competence; a great general who does not love war]в†’ 48:11-13 (Matt 20:25-28; John 15:13; Alma 43:45)

### from Alma 49
- `theme:preparation-defeats-numbers-and-is-how-God-works` вЂ”[the Lamanites bring superior numbers AND new armor, but Moroni's ridges/entrance/ditch nullify both: "more than a thousand of the Lamanites were slain; while... there was not a single soul of the Nephites which was slain"; preparation is the form providence takes]в†’ 49:2-23 (Alma 48:8-9; Prov 21:31; 2 Chr 32:5)
- `theme:anticipate-the-enemys-logic-fortify-the-weak-point-most` вЂ”["he had supposed that they would be frightened at... Ammonihah; and as the city of Noah had hitherto been the weakest part... they would march thither"; Moroni fortified the soft target most вЂ” the enemy probes the "weakest part"]в†’ 49:14-15 (Alma 48:9; Matt 26:41; 1 Pet 5:8)
- `theme:two-responses-to-one-deliverance` вЂ”[Amalickiah "did curse God, and also Moroni... because Moroni had kept the commandments of God"; the Nephites "did thank the Lord their God"; same event, gratitude in one heart, blasphemy in the other]в†’ 49:27-28 (Alma 44:3, 9; Ex 8:15; John 11:45-48)
- `theme:Amalickiah-hates-God-because-faithfulness-works` вЂ”[he curses God for the very thing that should have converted him вЂ” the Nephites won because Moroni was faithful; a heart running from the obvious would rather curse God than admit he was in it]в†’ 49:27 (Acts 23:12; Rev 16:9-11; Mosiah 3:12)
- `event:Corianton-restored-among-the-preachers` вЂ”[the prosperity came by the word "declared by Helaman, and Shiblon, and Corianton, and Ammon"; the son who strayed (ch 39) now preaches beside his faithful brothers вЂ” repentance was the beginning of his ministry, not the end]в†’ 49:30 (Alma 39:1-11; 42:31; Luke 15:22-24; 22:32)

### from Alma 50
- `doctrine:the-Lehi-covenant-verified-as-historical-law` вЂ”["we see how merciful and just are all the dealings of the Lord... their quarrelings and their contentions... brought upon them their wars... and those who were faithful... were delivered at all times"; the wars track righteousness вЂ” the war record's thesis]в†’ 50:19-22 (2 Ne 1:20; Alma 9:13; 37:13; 41:10)
- `theme:the-happiest-time-was-readiness-plus-faithfulness` вЂ”["there never was a happier time among the people of Nephi, since the days of Nephi, than in the days of Moroni"; the happiest era was war-readiness AND righteousness вЂ” flourishing is preparation + faithfulness, not absence of threat]в†’ 50:23 (2 Ne 5:27; Mosiah 2:41; 4 Ne 1:16; Prov 21:31)
- `theme:private-cruelty-betrays-the-public-scheme` вЂ”[Morianton's plan "would lead to the overthrow of their liberty," but "being a man of much passion... he fell upon her and beat her much," and she exposed everything; unbridled passion leaks вЂ” can't govern yourself in private, undone in public]в†’ 50:30-31 (Alma 38:12; 47:18; Luke 12:2-3; Num 32:23)
- `theme:the-overlooked-person-is-the-hinge` вЂ”[an abused maidservant, the most powerless person in the tyrant's household, becomes the hinge on which the nation's liberty turns; God's deliverance through the discounted (cf. Abish)]в†’ 50:31 (Alma 19:16-29; Esther 4:14; 1 Cor 1:27-28)
- `reference:the-oath-of-good-governance` вЂ”[Pahoran takes the seat "with an oath... to judge righteously, and to keep the peace and the freedom of the people, and to grant unto them their sacred privileges to worship the Lord their God... and to bring the wicked to justice"]в†’ 50:37-40 (Mosiah 29:25-29; Alma 4:16-17; D&C 134:1-5)

### from Alma 51
- `theme:sedition-born-from-factional-spite` вЂ”[the king-men, having lost "by the voice of the people," are "glad in their hearts" the Lamanites are coming and "would not take up arms... so wroth with the chief judge"; hatred of opponents exceeding love of country вЂ” preferring the catastrophe that vindicates the grievance to the cooperation that wins]в†’ 51:7-13 (Mosiah 29:25-32; 3 Ne 6:30; Judg 12:1-6)
- `theme:internal-division-opens-the-door-to-conquest` вЂ”[while Moroni must put down the king-men, Amalickiah captures a string of cities; "this had been hitherto a cause of all their destruction"; the enemy within enabled the enemy without]в†’ 51:9-27 (Matt 12:25; 1 Kgs 16:21; Alma 51:16)
- `theme:the-nations-own-fortifications-turned-against-it` вЂ”[the captured cities were "strongly fortified after the manner of the fortifications of Moroni; all of which afforded strongholds for the Lamanites"; the defenses built to protect now shelter the invader, because division stripped the defenders]в†’ 51:27 (Alma 48:8; Ps 127:1; Hag 1:6)
- `theme:the-hard-edge-of-wartime-sedition-law` вЂ”[Moroni given power to "compel those dissenters to defend their country or to put them to death"; 4,000 hewn down, leaders jailed "no time for their trials"; martial law in an existential invasion вЂ” the record lets the hard thing stand]в†’ 51:15-21 (Alma 46:35; 62:9-10; D&C 134:1-5)
- `theme:the-pit-digger-falls-into-his-own-pit` вЂ”[Amalickiah swore the "rash" oath to "drink the blood of Moroni" but never reaches him; Teancum "put a javelin to his heart" in his sleep вЂ” the man who rose by poison and the mid-handshake stab dies asleep, silently; he dies as he killed]в†’ 51:9-10, 33-37 (Eccl 10:8; Prov 26:27; Alma 47:18, 24; Matt 26:52)

### from Alma 52
- `theme:organized-evil-outlives-its-leader` вЂ”[Amalickiah dead, but "Ammoron, the brother of king Amalickiah, was appointed to reign in his stead" and prosecutes the same war; cutting off the head rarely ends the body вЂ” institutional evil outlasts its founder]в†’ 52:3-4 (Alma 48:1-6; 54:5; Judg 8:33-9:6)
- `theme:dont-fight-on-the-enemys-terms` вЂ”[twice the commanders refuse to assault the forts ("impossible... while they were in their fortifications; therefore he abandoned his designs"); wait, prepare, decoy instead вЂ” the harder courage is to NOT attack when attacking is heroic and futile]в†’ 52:5, 17 (Eccl 7:8; Prov 21:31; Luke 14:31-32)
- `theme:the-decoy-and-the-pincer` вЂ”[Moroni can't get Jacob "out upon fair grounds," so Teancum baits a pursuit, the hidden army takes the emptied Mulek, fresh forces catch the wearied pursuers in a pincer; the ambush of Ai вЂ” Nephites think while the enemy reacts]в†’ 52:21-31 (Josh 8:3-22; Alma 43:30; Judg 7:16-22)
- `theme:mercy-maximizes-surrenders-not-kills` вЂ”["If ye will bring forth your weapons of war... we will forbear shedding your blood"; "the number of prisoners... exceeded more than the number of those who had been slain"; a war for protection maximizes surrenders]в†’ 52:37-40 (Alma 43:54; 44:20; Deut 20:10-12)
- `theme:the-dissenters-ferocity-destroys-him` вЂ”[Jacob the Zoramite, "having an unconquerable spirit," fights to the death and is killed, while the native Lamanites surrender and live; the apostate's hardness destroys him, the one who relents is spared]в†’ 52:33-40 (Alma 24:30; 47:36; Matt 16:25)

### from Alma 53
- `doctrine:keeping-the-covenant-while-watching-others-bleed-for-it` вЂ”[the people of Ammon, "moved with compassion," want to take up arms for the Nephites dying for them, but Helaman stops them "lest... they should lose their souls"; "compelled to behold their brethren wade through their afflictions" вЂ” the hardest faithfulness; the impulse to break came from love and was still refused]в†’ 53:13-15 (Alma 24:17-19; Num 30:2; Eccl 5:4-5)
- `theme:the-next-generation-takes-up-what-the-parents-could-not` вЂ”[the sons "had not entered into a covenant," so two thousand covenant to fight "unto the laying down of their lives"; the oath bound the fathers, not the children вЂ” the pacifists' covenant produced sons willing to die for liberty]в†’ 53:16-18 (Alma 27:23-24; 56:47-48; Judg 2:7-10; John 15:13)
- `doctrine:faithfulness-true-in-whatsoever-entrusted-is-the-defining-trait` вЂ”["valiant for courage... but this was not allвЂ”they were true at all times in whatsoever thing they were entrusted... for they had been taught to keep the commandments"; the most formidable force defined by reliability, taught at home вЂ” not prowess]в†’ 53:20-21 (Alma 18:10; 56:47-48; Luke 16:10; 2 Tim 2:2)
- `theme:internal-dissension-costs-ground-again` вЂ”["because of iniquity amongst themselves... dissensions and intrigue among themselves they were placed in the most dangerous circumstances"; even after victory, division immediately costs ground]в†’ 53:8-9 (Josh 7:4-5; Alma 51:9; 31:8)
- `theme:the-captives-build-their-own-prison-wall` вЂ”[the Lamanite prisoners "encircle the city of Bountiful... within a wall which they had caused them to build with their own hands"; the work of the captured strengthens the structure that holds them]в†’ 53:4-5 (Alma 55:25-26; Ex 1:11-14)

### from Alma 54
- `theme:two-foundations-conscience-vs-grievance` вЂ”[Moroni appeals to God, justice, repentance, defensible cause; Ammoron to grievance, revenge, the claim to rule; the war rests on incompatible foundations, not a negotiable dispute]в†’ 54:5-24 (Alma 43:46-47; Mosiah 10:12-17; Matt 7:24-27)
- `theme:agnosticism-as-moral-evasion` вЂ”["concerning that God... we know not such a being; neither do ye... but behold these things matter not"; not Korihor's flat denial but agnosticism deployed to render God irrelevant вЂ” an irrelevant God makes no demands]в†’ 54:21-22 (Alma 30:48; Ps 14:1; 2 Pet 3:3-5; Rom 1:21)
- `theme:the-tell-of-half-belief` вЂ”["if it so be that there is a devil and a hell, will he not send you there to dwell with my brother"; he scoffs at hell and uses it as an insult in the same breath вЂ” you don't taunt with a place you're sure doesn't exist]в†’ 54:22 (Acts 26:28; Mark 5:7; James 2:19)
- `theme:grievance-mutated-into-a-political-claim` вЂ”["your fathers did wrong their brethren... rob them of their right to the government when it rightly belonged unto them"; the Mosiah-10 grievance refined into a constitutional claim to rule]в†’ 54:17, 24 (Mosiah 10:12-17; 2 Ne 5:3; 2 Sam 15:2-6)
- `theme:the-borrowed-grievance` вЂ”[Ammoron, "a descendant of Zoram," calls himself "a bold Lamanite" avenging Lamanite wrongs; a Nephite dissenter of Zoramite stock wears Lamanite grievance as a costume вЂ” grievance ideologies outlive the injury and get adopted by whoever finds them useful]в†’ 54:23-24 (1 Ne 4:35; Jacob 1:13; Alma 47:35-36)
- `theme:honest-anger-vs-cold-dismissal` вЂ”[Moroni names his state ("I am in my anger") while grounding the cause in defense; Ammoron's "these things matter not" is the colder thing; transparent fierceness vs studied detachment]в†’ 54:13, 22 (Eph 4:26; Ps 4:4; Matt 5:37)

### from Alma 55
- `doctrine:refusing-to-kill-the-helpless-even-when-you-could` вЂ”["the Nephites could have slain them. But... this was not the desire of Moroni; he did not delight in murder or bloodshed... he would not fall upon the Lamanites and destroy them in their drunkenness"; slaughtering the defenseless "would bring upon him injustice" вЂ” winning isn't worth becoming unjust]в†’ 55:18-19 (1 Sam 26:7-12; Alma 48:16; Matt 5:44-45; Rom 12:21)
- `theme:the-stratagem-that-serves-mercy` вЂ”[Moroni takes Gid by the wine trick + silently arming the prisoners; the cleverness designed to AVOID bloodshed, not enable it вЂ” the city taken without a death]в†’ 55:4-24 (Alma 43:30; Josh 8:3-22; Prov 24:6)
- `theme:the-enemys-own-appetite-is-the-weapon` вЂ”["let us keep of our wine till we go against the Nephites... this saying only made them more desirous to drink"; the guards' undisciplined craving is the weapon вЂ” Moroni only offers and lets their weakness do the rest]в†’ 55:10-14 (Prov 20:1; 23:31-32; Mosiah 22:6-11)
- `theme:angriest-at-the-knowingly-false` вЂ”["he knew that Ammoron had a perfect knowledge of his fraud... that it was not a just cause"; Moroni enraged not by an honest enemy but by one who knows he's wrong and fights anyway вЂ” the knowingly false, not the deceived]в†’ 55:1 (Alma 54:17-24; John 9:41; James 4:17)
