- `theme:remember-God-and-dont-fall-for-your-own-trick` вЂ”[the Lamanites try the wine trick back, but "the Nephites were not slow to remember the Lord their God... they would not partake... save they had first given to some of the Lamanite prisoners"; vigilance + remembering God travel together]в†’ 55:30-32 (Hosea 5:15; Alma 62:49-51; 1 Pet 5:8)

### from Alma 56
- `doctrine:faith-taught-by-believing-mothers` вЂ”["they had been taught by their mothers, that if they did not doubt, God would deliver them"; the most formidable faith in the war record cultivated in childhood by believing women вЂ” mothers (people of Ammon) who taught what they had themselves staked everything on]в†’ 56:47 (Alma 23:6-7; 2 Tim 1:5; 3:14-15; Prov 22:6; Deut 6:6-7)
- `doctrine:believing-on-the-words-of-a-trusted-witness` вЂ”["we do not doubt our mothers knew it"; not independent knowledge but confidence in their mothers' knowledge вЂ” faith resting on a trustworthy loving witness is real enough to march into battle on; the D&C 46:14 gift]в†’ 56:48 (D&C 46:14; John 4:39-42; 1 John 1:1-3)
- `theme:courage-that-is-a-function-of-faith-not-bravado` вЂ”["never had I seen so great courage... our God is with us, and he will not suffer that we should fall"; fearlessness resting on trust in God's deliverance, not their own arms]в†’ 56:45-47 (Matt 17:20; Mark 9:23; Ps 27:1; Alma 57:26)
- `theme:reluctance-even-in-the-young-warriors` вЂ”["we would not slay our brethren if they would let us alone"; even the untested boys keep the family-not-enemy frame вЂ” fighting only because Antipus's army would be destroyed otherwise]в†’ 56:46 (Alma 48:23; 24:18; Matt 5:9)
- `event:not-one-of-the-two-thousand-slain` вЂ”["there had not one soul of them fallen to the earth... they had fought as if with the strength of God; never were men known to have fought with such miraculous strength"; the empty casualty list is the divine signature on a faith taught and trusted]в†’ 56:55-56 (Alma 57:25; 58:39; Ex 14:13-14; 2 Chr 20:17)

### from Alma 57
- `doctrine:obedience-with-exactness-as-the-form-of-faith` вЂ”["they did obey and observe to perform every word of command with exactness; yea, and even according to their faith it was done unto them"; exactness is the outward form of inward trust вЂ” faith freed them from the fear that makes people cut corners]в†’ 57:21 (Matt 9:29; Mark 9:23; Alma 53:20; 18:10)
- `doctrine:faith-preserves-through-the-wounds-not-from-them` вЂ”[this time "not one soul among them who had not received many wounds," 200 faint from blood loss, yet "not one soul... did perish"; faith carried them through the slaughter alive вЂ” through the fire, not around it]в†’ 57:25-26 (Dan 3:25-27; Ps 23:4; Isa 43:2) вЂ” truer + harder than "the faithful don't get hurt"
- `doctrine:preservation-is-a-particular-sign-not-a-universal-rule` вЂ”[spared "while there was a thousand of our brethren who were slain"; the thousand were no less faithful вЂ” "entered into the rest of their God"; the unscathed 2000 are a sign, not a promise to all]в†’ 57:26, 36 (Alma 28:11-12; Heb 11:32-40; D&C 42:46)
- `theme:minds-firm-trust-continually` вЂ”["they are young, and their minds are firm, and they do put their trust in God continually"; a permanent orientation produced by the mothers' teaching, not a one-time act]в†’ 57:27 (Jacob 3:2; Alma 58:40; Prov 3:5-6)
- `theme:the-honest-horror-of-even-a-righteous-war` вЂ”["we did slay upwards of two thousand of them after they had surrendered"; the prisoners "run upon our swords" in rebellion; surrendered prisoners slain вЂ” forced by their armed revolt + the army's lack of capacity, reported plainly without applause]в†’ 57:14, 32-33 (Alma 51:19; 2 Sam 11:14-17; Eccl 9:11)

### from Alma 58
- `doctrine:God-speaks-peace-to-the-soul-before-the-deliverance` вЂ”[the abandoned, starving army prays, and "the Lord... did speak peace to our souls, and did grant unto us great faith, and did cause us that we should hope for our deliverance in him"; the inner gifts come BEFORE the external rescue вЂ” and they ARE the answer]в†’ 58:10-11 (D&C 6:22-23; Philip 4:6-7; John 14:27; Ex 14:13-14)
- `doctrine:peace-and-faith-are-the-strengthening-not-a-consolation-prize` вЂ”["we did take courage with our small force... fixed with a determination to conquer"; God answered the prayer for deliverance by first delivering them from despair, so they could go win it]в†’ 58:11-12 (Ps 27:1; Isa 41:10; Alma 57:26)
- `theme:refuse-to-murmur-when-your-own-side-fails-you` вЂ”[abandoned by the government with no explanation, Helaman considers the charitable cause first ("if so, we do not desire to murmur") and lands on "it mattereth notвЂ”we trust God"; assume the best, refuse the murmur, anchor in God not the institution]в†’ 58:34-37 (Num 14:27-29; Philip 2:14; 1 Cor 13:7)
- `theme:Helaman-vs-Moroni-two-responses-to-neglect` вЂ”[same neglect (denied support), opposite responses: Helaman refuses to murmur + trusts God (58:35-37); Moroni writes a furious accusatory letter (ch 60); Mormon places them side by side, and ch 61 vindicates the assume-the-best instinct]в†’ 58:35-37 (Alma 60:6-11; 61:1-9; Matt 7:1-2)
- `theme:wisdom-adapts-against-a-learning-enemy` вЂ”["they remembered that which we had hitherto done; therefore we could not decoy them"; the old trick won't work twice, so Helaman invents a new stratagem вЂ” and takes Manti "without the shedding of blood"]в†’ 58:1, 13-28 (Josh 8:13; Alma 52:21; Eccl 1:9)
- `theme:preservation-was-the-sign-daily-faithfulness-the-substance` вЂ”["not one soul has been slain. But... they stand fast in that liberty wherewith God has made them free; and they are strict to remember the Lord their God from day to day"; the miracle was the sign, daily faithfulness the substance]в†’ 58:39-40 (Alma 57:26-27; Gal 5:1; 1 Cor 16:13)

### from Alma 59
- `theme:even-Moroni-doubts` вЂ”["Moroni... began to doubt, because of the wickedness of the people, whether they should not fall"; the man Mormon praised above all others wavers under repeated loss вЂ” the faithful doubt too; permission, not disqualification]в†’ 59:11-12 (Matt 11:2-3; 1 Kgs 19:4; Ps 73:2-3)
- `doctrine:prevention-is-cheaper-than-recovery` вЂ”["it was easier to keep the city... than to retake it"; the city could have been held cheaply if help had come вЂ” "someone will handle it" is how the holdable thing is lost]в†’ 59:9-10 (Prov 22:3; Luke 14:28-32; Alma 50:1-6)
- `theme:doubt-curdling-into-anger-at-the-wrong-target` вЂ”["Moroni was angry with the government, because of their indifference"; he infers indifference from the missing help вЂ” but Pahoran wasn't indifferent, he'd been driven from his seat by rebels; righteous anger aimed wrong, judging before hearing]в†’ 59:13 (Alma 61:3-9; Prov 18:13; Prov 16:32)
- `theme:Helaman-vs-Moroni-two-responses-to-neglect` вЂ”[Helaman, equally abandoned, "did not desire to murmur" and trusted God (58:35-37); Moroni grows "angry with the government" and assumes indifference (59:13); Mormon places them side by side]в†’ 59:13 (Alma 58:34-37; 60:1-11; 61:9; Matt 7:1-2)

### from Alma 60
- `doctrine:the-righteous-slain-are-not-lost-and-not-proof-of-their-wickedness` вЂ”["Do ye suppose that... so many... have been killed... because of their wickedness? ye have supposed in vain... the Lord suffereth the righteous to be slain that his justice... may come upon the wicked... they do enter into the rest of the Lord"; death is not God's verdict against the faithful]в†’ 60:12-13 (Luke 13:1-5; Job 1-2; D&C 42:46; Rev 14:13)
- `doctrine:death-of-the-righteous-condemns-the-negligent-not-the-dead` вЂ”["the blood of thousands shall come upon your heads for vengeance... it is to your condemnation"; when the righteous die through others' neglect, the guilt is on the living who failed them, not on the dead at rest]в†’ 60:10-13 (Ezek 33:6-8; Gen 4:10; Matt 18:6)
- `doctrine:cleanse-the-inward-vessel-first` вЂ”["the inward vessel shall be cleansed first, and then shall the outer vessel be cleansed also"; the corruption at the head must be fixed before the outward war can be won вЂ” inside before outside]в†’ 60:23-24 (Matt 23:25-26; Alma 60:15; Ps 51:6)
- `doctrine:fear-God-not-power-seek-to-pull-power-down` вЂ”["I seek not for power, but to pull it down... it is my God whom I fear"; the rare man who threatens force only to destroy power-seeking, not to seize power вЂ” the inversion of unrighteous dominion; incorruptible even in error]в†’ 60:28, 36 (D&C 121:39; Acts 5:29; Alma 48:17)
- `theme:right-doctrine-pure-heart-wrong-judgment-of-a-person` вЂ”[Moroni is right about the doctrine, the king-men, his motives, and even claims revelation вЂ” yet his judgment of Pahoran ("thoughtless stupor," "traitors," threatening to march) is false; being right + pure doesn't guarantee you're right about the person]в†’ 60:7, 18, 33 (Prov 18:13; 16:32; Alma 61:9; John 7:24)

### from Alma 61
- `doctrine:receive-false-accusation-by-blessing-the-heart-behind-it` вЂ”[falsely called a traitor + threatened with insurrection, Pahoran answers "it mattereth not; I am not angry, but do rejoice in the greatness of your heart"; he skips his own vindicated innocence and celebrates the accuser's good heart вЂ” charity not easily provoked]в†’ 61:9 (1 Cor 13:4-7; Prov 15:1; 1 Pet 2:23; Matt 5:11-12)
- `theme:the-assume-the-best-instinct-vindicated` вЂ”[Pahoran had been "driven out" by rebels who "withheld our provisions"; Helaman's charitable "maybe they're in trouble too" (58:35) was kinder AND more accurate than Moroni's "thoughtless stupor... traitors"]в†’ 61:3-8 (Alma 58:35; 1 Cor 13:7; Prov 18:13)
- `doctrine:a-flawed-message-can-still-carry-a-true-word` вЂ”["I was somewhat worried... whether it should be just... to go against our brethren. But ye have said... the Lord hath commanded"; the letter wrong about the person was right about the principle, and resolved Pahoran's real doubt]в†’ 61:19-20 (Rom 8:28; Num 22:28-31; Phil 1:18)
- `theme:take-the-truth-let-the-tone-go` вЂ”[Pahoran reads Moroni's harsh letter as counsel not insult вЂ” taking the true word and letting the wounding tone go; the difference between offense and benefit is in the reader's charity]в†’ 61:9, 19-20 (Prov 9:8-9; 27:6; D&C 121:43)
- `doctrine:liberty-subordinated-to-obedience-to-God` вЂ”["we would subject ourselves to the yoke of bondage if it were requisite with the justice of God... But behold he doth not command us... but that we should put our trust in him"; freedom is not the highest value вЂ” obedience to God is, and God commands resistance here]в†’ 61:12-13 (Acts 5:29; Mosiah 7:21; Matt 6:33)
- `theme:conflict-that-deepens-the-friendship` вЂ”[sharp reproof (Moroni) + gracious reception (Pahoran, "my beloved brother") в†’ united again in the same cause; D&C 121:43 lived вЂ” reproving with sharpness, then an increase of love, here supplied by the one wrongly reproved]в†’ 61:9, 21 (D&C 121:43; Prov 27:17; Eccl 4:9-12)

### from Alma 62
- `doctrine:the-same-affliction-hardens-some-and-softens-others` вЂ”["because of the exceedingly great length of the war... many had become hardened... and many were softened because of their afflictions... in the depth of humility"; the same suffering produced opposite results вЂ” affliction is a catalyst that intensifies the heart's existing direction, not a cause that sets it; the furnace that hardens clay melts wax]в†’ 62:41 (2 Cor 2:15-16; Heb 6:7-8; Matt 13:5-6; Ex 9:34-35)
- `doctrine:remembering-is-the-antidote-to-the-pride-cycle` вЂ”["notwithstanding their riches... they were not lifted up in the pride of their eyes; neither were they slow to remember the Lord... they did remember how great things the Lord had done for them"; the cycle broke because they remembered their deliverance вЂ” prosperity is safe in a people who remember; forgetting, not wealth, is the problem]в†’ 62:48-50 (Deut 8:11-18; Alma 45:24; 4 Ne 1:23-26)
- `doctrine:the-prayers-of-the-righteous-spare-the-many` вЂ”["for the righteous' sake, yea, because of the prayers of the righteous, they were spared"; the faithful few hold up the roof over everyone, including the hardened вЂ” the salt of the earth]в†’ 62:40 (Gen 18:23-32; Matt 5:13; Mosiah 27:14; James 5:16)
- `theme:righteous-anger-unbridled-carries-a-cost` вЂ”[Teancum, "exceedingly angry with Ammoron," goes alone "in his anger" to kill him and succeeds, but the king wakes his servants and they slay Teancum; the man of fierce anger dies on anger's errand вЂ” even righteous anger, unbridled, costs]в†’ 62:35-37 (Alma 38:12; 51:34; Eph 4:26; Prov 16:32)
- `theme:the-great-captain-exits-in-peace-not-glory` вЂ”[Moroni "yielded up the command of his armies into the hands of his son... and he retired to his own house that he might spend the remainder of his days in peace"; the greatest captain exits not in triumph but in rest вЂ” fitting the man who never delighted in war and only ever wanted to save his people]в†’ 62:43 (Alma 48:11-16; 2 Tim 4:7; Luke 2:29)

### from Alma 63
- `doctrine:the-sacred-record-passes-through-chosen-faithful-hands` вЂ”[Shiblon "a just man... did observe to do good continually" receives the records, then confers them on Helaman before death; the book closes "the account of Alma, and Helaman his son, and also Shiblon" вЂ” three generations, the trust handed on as Alma charged in 37]в†’ 63:1-2, 11-17 (Alma 37:1-12; 2 Tim 2:2; Deut 6:6-7)
- `theme:the-restored-son-serves-the-steady-son-keeps` вЂ”[the records go to steady Shiblon (Alma 38), while restored Corianton (Alma 39-42) "had gone forth to the land northward... to carry forth provisions" вЂ” laboring honestly though not given the sacred trust; repentance real, stewardship to proven steadiness, both loved]в†’ 63:2, 10 (Alma 38:2-3; 42; Luke 15:11-32)
- `theme:the-great-are-remembered-by-deeds-not-death-notices` вЂ”[Moroni, of whom "the very powers of hell would have been shaken" (48:17), dies in one line "Moroni died also"; the footnote sends to "43-63 for his great contributions" вЂ” the deeds are the monument, the eulogy was given mid-life]в†’ 63:3 (Alma 48:17; 2 Tim 4:7)
- `theme:a-record-honest-about-the-limits-of-its-knowledge` вЂ”[Hagoth's ships sail north and "were never heard of more. And we suppose that they were drowned... and whither she did go we know not"; the record admits where its knowledge stops rather than inventing an ending вЂ” honesty over false omniscience]в†’ 63:5-8 (Alma 22:31-32; Hel 3:3-12)

## вЂ” END OF ALMA (63 chapters) В· BOOK OF HELAMAN BEGINS вЂ”

### from Helaman 1
- `doctrine:the-secret-combination-is-the-anti-covenant` вЂ”[the assassins "all entered into a covenant, yea, swearing by their everlasting Maker, that they would tell no man that Kishkumen had murdered Pahoran"; the sacred form вЂ” a solemn oath in God's name вЂ” hijacked to sanctify and conceal murder; the dark mirror of every holy covenant, "most abominable above all"]в†’ 1:11-12 (Ether 8:13-25; Hel 6:21-30; Ether 8:18)
- `theme:the-deadliest-threat-is-internal-not-external` вЂ”[the war over, Pahoran dead, his sons "contend for the judgment-seat" and split the people into "three divisions"; external enemy beaten by blood, internal enemy ambition walks in the moment the strong hand is gone вЂ” the Nephites begin to die of themselves]в†’ 1:1-9 (Matt 12:25; Alma 51:5-21; Mosiah 29:7)
- `theme:complacency-leaves-the-center-undefended` вЂ”[because of "so much contention" they "had not kept sufficient guards... for they had supposed that the Lamanites durst not come into the heart of their lands"; the danger always assumed to be "out there" walks into the undefended interior]в†’ 1:18, 26-27 (Alma 48:7-9; 1 Cor 10:12; Mark 13:35-37)
- `theme:audacity-without-depth-of-position-destroys-itself` вЂ”[Coriantumr's bold central thrust takes Zarahemla, but "supposing that their greatest strength was in the center," he plunges deeper until he "had plunged the Lamanites into the midst of the Nephites" вЂ” surrounded, cut off, slain; speed without security is self-destruction]в†’ 1:22-32 (Prov 16:18; Alma 48:7-9; Luke 14:31)

### from Helaman 2
- `doctrine:flattery-and-craft-are-the-combination's-door` вЂ”[Gadianton "exceedingly expert in many words, and also in his craft"; he rises not by strength or merit but by the silver tongue and hidden scheme, flattering the band with promises of "power and authority" вЂ” words before violence, the consistent mechanism of every dissension in the record]в†’ 2:4-5 (Mosiah 27:8; Alma 50:35; Hel 1:7; Ether 8:2; Moses 5:29-31)
- `theme:the-combination's-program-is-to-capture-the-state-for-the-insiders` вЂ”["if they would place him in the judgment-seat he would grant unto those who belonged to his band that they should be placed in power and authority"; the naked logic of corruption вЂ” seize public office, convert it into spoils for the faction, conceal it by oath]в†’ 2:5 (Ether 8:22-25; Hel 6:38-39; Mosiah 29:21-23)
- `theme:the-counter-to-the-secret-is-one-faithful-person-who-enters-it` вЂ”[Helaman's servant defeats the assassination not by force but by going into the secret: "through disguise" he learns the plans, exchanges the band's sign, draws out "all the heart of Kishkumen," then stops it вЂ” light penetrates the dark by entering it]в†’ 2:6-9 (John 3:19-21; Eph 5:11-13; Luke 8:17)
- `theme:anonymous-faithfulness-saves-what-the-named-cannot` вЂ”[the servant who saves the chief judge and buys the nation years is never named вЂ” the dramatic figures get the names, but society is held together by the unrecorded faithful one out "by night"; most faithfulness that saves is unseen]в†’ 2:6-9 (Matt 6:1-4; Mark 12:42-44; 1 Cor 12:22-24)
- `theme:Mormon-names-the-ending-in-advance` вЂ”["this Gadianton did prove the overthrow, yea, almost the entire destruction of the people of Nephi"; the narrator tells the ending before the story develops вЂ” we read every chapter knowing the hunted band fleeing in defeat is the seed that eventually wins; only Kishkumen died, not the idea]в†’ 2:12-14 (Hel 6:18-30; 3 Ne 4:1; Ether 8:21)

### from Helaman 3
- `doctrine:the-word-of-God-divides-asunder-the-snares-of-the-devil` вЂ”["whosoever will may lay hold upon the word of God, which is quick and powerful, which shall divide asunder all the cunning and the snares and the wiles of the devil, and lead the man of Christ in a strait and narrow course"; the word named as the exact antidote to the combination's craft (2:4) вЂ” the iron rod that cuts a straight line through the maze of snares]в†’ 3:29-30 (Heb 4:12; 1 Ne 8:19-24; 15:23-25; Hel 2:4)
- `doctrine:sanctification-comes-by-yielding-the-heart-to-God` вЂ”[the persecuted humble "did wax stronger and stronger in their humility... even to the purifying and the sanctification of their hearts, which sanctification cometh because of their yielding their hearts unto God"; sanctification is surrender not exertion вЂ” the heart purified by being handed over, not scrubbed]в†’ 3:35 (Alma 22:18; Rom 6:13; 2 Chr 30:8) вЂ” the give-away-all-my-sins core
- `doctrine:the-gate-of-heaven-is-open-unto-all-who-will` вЂ”["the Lord is merciful unto all who will, in the sincerity of their hearts, call upon his holy name... the gate of heaven is open unto all, even to those who will believe on the name of Jesus Christ"; the barrier is never God's side, only whether a person will]в†’ 3:27-29 (Acts 10:34-35; Rom 2:11; 2 Ne 26:33)
- `theme:two-growths-in-one-season-rot-and-word` вЂ”[Gadianton's combinations spread "not known unto those at the head of government, therefore not destroyed" (v23) while the church has "exceedingly great prosperity," tens of thousands baptized; light and rot grow simultaneously in the same soil вЂ” peace real on the surface, hollow underneath]в†’ 3:23-26 (Matt 13:24-30; Eph 5:11-13; Hel 6:38)
- `theme:persecution-is-the-occasion-of-the-humble's-sanctification` вЂ”[the proud "professors" persecute the humble, who respond not with retaliation but "did fast and pray oft" and grew "firmer and firmer in the faith"; the same pressure that puffs the proud sanctifies the humble вЂ” Alma 62:41 from the inside]в†’ 3:34-35 (Alma 62:41; Matt 5:10-12; 1 Pet 4:12-14)
- `theme:pride-enters-the-professors-not-the-church` вЂ”[the pride entered "not into the church of God, but into the hearts of the people who professed to belong to the church of God"; pride is always individual hearts, not the institution вЂ” and it grew "because of their exceedingly great riches... from day to day"]в†’ 3:33-36 (Alma 45:24; 4 Ne 1:24-26; D&C 112:26)

### from Helaman 4
- `doctrine:boast-in-your-own-strength-and-you-are-left-in-it` вЂ”["because of... their boastings in their own strength, they were left in their own strength"; God's response to a people who boast they don't need Him is not lightning but withdrawal вЂ” He grants the request, and self-sufficiency proves catastrophically insufficient (man-for-man, v26); the punishment for self-reliance is to be granted it]в†’ 4:13, 26 (2 Ne 4:34; Jer 17:5; Prov 3:5-6)
- `doctrine:the-Spirit-dwells-not-in-unholy-temples` вЂ”["the Spirit of the Lord did no more preserve them... it had withdrawn from them because the Spirit of the Lord doth not dwell in unholy temples"; the Spirit leaves not in anger but by incompatibility вЂ” holiness cannot occupy a defiled space; we are the temple (1 Cor 3:16), so the remedy is to clean it, not placate an angry God]в†’ 4:24 (1 Cor 3:16-17; 6:19; Mosiah 2:37; Alma 34:36)
- `doctrine:defeat-is-traced-to-wickedness-not-the-enemy` вЂ”["this great loss... would not have happened had it not been for their wickedness"; the enemy was the instrument, the cause was internal sin that withdrew the covenant protection вЂ” D&C 82:10, bound when kept, void when broken]в†’ 4:11 (D&C 82:10; Mosiah 27:13; Judg 2:14-15)
- `doctrine:repentance-immediately-restores-prosperity` вЂ”["they did repent, and inasmuch as they did repent they did begin to prosper"; the same covenant that withdrew the help restores it the moment they turn вЂ” Moronihah regains half the lands at once; mercy as immediate as judgment]в†’ 4:15-16 (Hel 3:27; Mosiah 29:20; 2 Chr 7:14)
- `theme:the-pride-that-destroys-is-the-pride-that-oppresses-the-poor` вЂ”[the catalog of wickedness leads with social sin: "oppression to the poor, withholding their food from the hungry, withholding their clothing from the naked, and smiting their humble brethren upon the cheek"; the surest sign of a society under judgment is how it treats its poor вЂ” to God, mocking the sacred and withholding from the hungry are the same breath]в†’ 4:12 (Mosiah 4:16-26; Jacob 2:17-19; Matt 25:42-45; Ezek 18:12)
- `theme:in-the-space-of-not-many-years` вЂ”["thus had they become weak, because of their transgression, in the space of not many years"; the golden age of ch 3 collapses to near-destruction within a generation вЂ” righteousness is a daily yielding, not a position held, and its loss is fast; the speed is the warning]в†’ 4:26 (1 Ne 8:28; Hel 6:32; 12:2; Mosiah 26:6)

### from Helaman 5
- `doctrine:build-on-the-rock-of-the-Redeemer-and-the-storm-cannot-drag-you-down` вЂ”["remember... it is upon the rock of our Redeemer... that ye must build your foundation; that when the devil shall send forth his mighty winds... it shall have no power over you to drag you down... a foundation whereon if men build they cannot fall"; the storm still beats every bit as hard вЂ” the rock changes not whether it hits but whether it can sweep you away; Christ is not the absence of the whirlwind but the thing it cannot move you off of]в†’ 5:12 (Matt 7:24-27; Isa 28:16; D&C 6:34)
- `doctrine:Christ-redeems-from-sins-not-in-sins` вЂ”["he should not come to redeem them in their sins, but to redeem them from their sins... to redeem them from their sins because of repentance"; the death of cheap grace in a single preposition вЂ” redemption is rescue out of the pit, not a pardon that lets you keep the crime; transformation not exemption]в†’ 5:10-11 (Alma 11:34-37; 42:24)
- `doctrine:remembering-is-the-foundation-of-discipleship` вЂ”[Helaman's charge hammers "remember, remember" вЂ” Benjamin's words, Amulek's words, the names they carry; the fall of ch 4 came from forgetting (4:21-26), so the cure is active remembering; memory is the working foundation of faith, not nostalgia]в†’ 5:6-12 (Hel 4:21-26; Deut 8:11-18; Mosiah 2:9)
- `doctrine:names-are-a-call-to-remember-and-become` вЂ”["when you remember your names ye may remember them; and when ye remember them ye may remember their works... that they were good"; Helaman named his sons Nephi and Lehi so identity itself would be a daily summons вЂ” we become who we understand ourselves named toward]в†’ 5:6-7 (1 Ne 1:1; Prov 22:1; Rev 2:17)
- `doctrine:the-still-voice-of-perfect-mildness-shakes-the-earth` вЂ”["not a voice of thunder... but a still voice of perfect mildness, as if it had been a whisper, and it did pierce even to the very soul... notwithstanding the mildness of the voice, the earth shook exceedingly"; the most powerful voice is the gentlest вЂ” God's power is not in the volume; the mildness is the form of the power, not its weakness]в†’ 5:30-31 (1 Kgs 19:11-12; D&C 85:6; 3 Ne 11:3)
- `theme:the-fire-that-protects-instead-of-burns` вЂ”[Nephi and Lehi, starving and about to be killed, "encircled about as if by fire" that does not burn; later every convert encircled the same way, "filled with that joy which is unspeakable and full of glory" вЂ” in a prison; the fire that should destroy becomes the thing that protects]в†’ 5:23-24, 43-44 (Dan 3:23-27; Ex 3:2; 1 Pet 1:8)
- `theme:cry-unto-the-voice-until-the-darkness-disperses` вЂ”[Aminadab the dissenter вЂ” the one who fell furthest вЂ” shows the way: "repent, and cry unto the voice, even until ye shall have faith in Christ"; they "did cry even until the cloud of darkness was dispersed"; the persistence is the point вЂ” the darkness lifts for those who keep crying through it]в†’ 5:40-42 (Acts 2:37; Luke 18:1-8; Mosiah 4:2)
- `theme:the-word-recovers-what-the-sword-could-not` вЂ”[the Lamanites who took half the Nephite lands by the sword in ch 4 now "lay down their weapons of war, and also their hatred and the tradition of their fathers" and "yield up... the lands of their possession" through conversion; two unarmed brothers in a prison undid a war the army could not]в†’ 5:50-52 (Hel 4:5; Alma 23-24; 2 Cor 10:4)

### from Helaman 6
- `doctrine:the-Spirit-follows-the-heart-not-the-lineage` вЂ”["the Spirit of the Lord began to withdraw from the Nephites, because of the wickedness and the hardness of their hearts... the Lord began to pour out his Spirit upon the Lamanites, because of their easiness and willingness to believe"; the Spirit crosses the supposed racial line entirely вЂ” lineage gives nothing if the heart is hard, its absence costs nothing if soft; the final answer to the 2 Ne 5 curse question]в†’ 6:34-36 (2 Ne 26:33; Acts 10:34-35; Hel 15:7-8)
- `doctrine:secret-combinations-are-Satan's-one-continuous-project` вЂ”[five times "that same being" вЂ” who tempted Eve, plotted with Cain, built Babel, destroyed the Jaredites, "put it into the heart of Gadianton"; "he is the author of all sin," handing the same plot "from generation to generation according as he can get hold upon the hearts"; organized evil has continuity and a single author]в†’ 6:26-30 (Moses 5:29-31; Gen 4:8; Gen 11:4; Ether 8:9-19)
- `theme:prolonged-prosperity-not-affliction-is-the-occasion-of-the-fall` вЂ”["the Lord had blessed them so long with the riches of the world that they had not been stirred up to anger... therefore they began to set their hearts upon their riches... to be lifted up one above another"; the length and ease of the blessing was the corrosive вЂ” the dark twin of Alma 62:41; the season to fear most is the long comfortable one]в†’ 6:16-17 (Alma 62:41; Deut 8:11-18; Hel 12:2)
- `theme:same-cancer-opposite-responses-opposite-fates` вЂ”[the robbers appeared among both peoples; the Lamanites "did hunt the band... and did preach the word of God among the more wicked part of them" until it was "utterly destroyed," while the Nephites "did build them up and support them" until they ran the government; the fate is decided not by whether evil arises but by whether you hunt-and-convert it or build it up and join it]в†’ 6:37-39 (Alma 23-26; Hel 5:50-52; Rom 12:21)
- `theme:the-combination-offers-escape-from-consequence` вЂ”[the oath is specifically "that they should not suffer for their murders, and their plunderings, and their stealings"; trial "according to the laws of their wickedness" not the country's вЂ” the whole appeal is escape from accountability, the exact inverse of the gospel which redeems you FROM sin by facing it (5:10)]в†’ 6:21, 24 (Hel 5:10; John 3:19-21; Prov 28:13)
- `doctrine:easiness-and-willingness-to-believe-is-the-whole-qualification` вЂ”[the Spirit poured on the Lamanites "because of their easiness and willingness to believe in his words"; not lineage, not law-keeping pedigree, but an open and willing heart is the entire condition вЂ” available to anyone, costing the formerly-cursed nothing]в†’ 6:36 (Ex 25:2; Alma 32:27; Matt 18:3)

### from Helaman 7
- `theme:these-are-my-days-faithfulness-in-the-age-you-are-given` вЂ”["Oh, that I could have had my days in the days when my father Nephi first came out of the land of Jerusalem... But behold, I am consigned that these are my days"; the ache of every disciple in a dark age, answered by accepting the assignment вЂ” the time you were given, not the romanticized past (he glosses Laman and Lemuel), is the time you're called to]в†’ 7:7-9 (Esth 4:14; D&C 64:33-34; 2 Ne 5:27)
- `theme:the-prophet's-grief-becomes-the-sermon` вЂ”[Nephi climbs the tower "that I might pour out my soul unto my God," not to preach; the crowd gathers "because of my mourning and lamentation" вЂ” a man visibly broken over their sin reaches the hardened where argument failed; the rebuke is love, sharp and soaked in grief at once]в†’ 7:11-15 (Jer 9:1; Luke 19:41-44; 3 Ne 17:21-22)
- `doctrine:greater-knowledge-greater-accountability` вЂ”["it shall be better for the Lamanites than for you... they are more righteous than you, for they have not sinned against that great knowledge which ye have received"; the Nephites MORE condemned because of their greater light, not despite it вЂ” light received is a weight of accountability; the principle that explains the whole reversal]в†’ 7:23-24 (Luke 12:47-48; Alma 9:19-23; D&C 82:3)
- `doctrine:God's-forsaking-is-self-caused-by-hardened-hearts` вЂ”["Why has he forsaken you? It is because you have hardened your hearts; yea, ye will not hearken unto the voice of the good shepherd"; God never forsakes arbitrarily вЂ” the abandonment is people walking away and experiencing the absence they chose; the shepherd is still calling, but the sheep won't follow]в†’ 7:17-18 (Ezek 18:23, 31-32; John 10:14; Hel 4:24)
- `theme:forgetting-God-in-the-very-day-of-deliverance` вЂ”["O, how could you have forgotten your God in the very day that he has delivered you?"; gratitude evaporating the instant after rescue вЂ” remember was the cure in ch 5, forget is the death here, the distance "the space of not many years" (six)]в†’ 7:20-21 (Hel 5:9-12; Deut 8:11-18; Judg 8:34)
- `theme:judicial-corruption-when-the-combination-captures-the-courts` вЂ”[the robbers in the judgment-seats "condemning the righteous because of their righteousness; letting the guilty and the wicked go unpunished because of their money"; when the combination captures the courts, justice inverts вЂ” the collapse of justice is the mark of a captured state]в†’ 7:4-5 (Isa 5:8, 23; Amos 5:12; Mic 7:3)

### from Helaman 8
- `doctrine:all-the-prophets-testified-of-Christ` вЂ”[Nephi widens the charge past himself: "ye also deny all the words... spoken by our fathers" вЂ” then walks the whole line (Moses, Abraham who "saw his coming and rejoiced," the pre-Abrahamic patriarchs "after the order of his Son," Zenos, Zenock, Ezias, Isaiah, Jeremiah, Lehi, Nephi); the entire scriptural record across millennia and two hemispheres is one unbroken testimony of one Redeemer]в†’ 8:13-23 (Jacob 4:4; Luke 24:27; Acts 10:43; John 8:56)
- `doctrine:look-upon-the-Son-of-God-and-live` вЂ”["as he lifted up the brazen serpent in the wilderness, even so shall he be lifted up... as many as should look upon the Son of God with faith, having a contrite spirit, might live"; the dying only had to look вЂ” the offense of the cure is its simplicity (Alma 33: many perished "because of the simpleness of the way"); the gaze of faith gives nothing to be proud of]в†’ 8:14-15 (Num 21:6-9; John 3:14-15; Alma 33:19-22)
- `doctrine:fulfilled-prophecy-is-evidence-for-prophecy-not-yet-fulfilled` вЂ”["now we know that Jerusalem was destroyed according to the words of Jeremiah. O then why not the Son of God come, according to his prophecy?"; the Mulekites вЂ” Zedekiah's seed among them вЂ” are living proof Jerusalem fell as foretold; if God was right about the checkable thing, trust him about the unverifiable one]в†’ 8:20-21 (Jer 26:18; Omni 1:15; Hel 6:10)
- `doctrine:unbelief-against-total-evidence-is-willful-not-honest` вЂ”["seeing ye know these things and cannot deny them except ye shall lie... ye have received all things, both things in heaven, and all things which are in the earth, as a witness"; their rejection is not a failure of evidence but a refusal of it вЂ” to deny it they must lie; willful rejection of known truth is graver than honest searching]в†’ 8:24 (Alma 30:44; Rom 1:20; John 3:19-20)
- `theme:corruption-fears-the-people-not-God-and-acts-through-the-mob` вЂ”[the judges "durst not lay their own hands upon him, for they feared the people"; corruption cannot act in the open, so it manufactures public anger to do its work вЂ” the cowardice of the secret combination needs both concealment and a mob]в†’ 8:4-7 (Matt 26:4-5; Acts 5:26; Prov 29:25)
- `theme:brother-kills-brother-for-the-seat-Cain-runs-again` вЂ”["your judge is murdered... by his brother, who seeketh to sit in the judgment-seat... they both belong to your secret band, whose author is Gadianton"; fratricide for power, concealed by the band вЂ” Cain and Abel running again, the exact lineage Mormon traced in ch 6; Nephi drags the secret crime into the light before they can hide it]в†’ 8:27-28 (Gen 4:8; Hel 6:26-30; Hel 9:6)

### from Helaman 9
- `theme:overwhelming-evidence-met-with-a-manufactured-alternative` вЂ”[the murder happened exactly as prophesied, which should settle it; instead the judges invent "this Nephi must have agreed with some one to slay the judge... that he might raise himself to be a great man" вЂ” a theory far harder to believe than the obvious one; the natural mind would rather believe the prophet a murderer than admit he's a prophet, because the second belief demands repentance]в†’ 9:16 (John 11:47-48; Matt 28:11-15; John 12:9-11)
- `doctrine:true-prophecy-is-specific-and-falsifiable` вЂ”[Nephi answers the charge not by protest but by raising the stakes: a precise, sequential, instantly-testable prediction вЂ” Seantum will deny, then act astonished, then you'll find blood on his cloak, then go pale, then confess; the fraud speaks in vagueness, the true prophet stakes his life on a checkable sequence and invites the test]в†’ 9:25-37 (Deut 18:21-22; 1 Kgs 22:28; 1 Sam 9:6)
- `doctrine:the-faithful-messenger-deflects-glory-to-God` вЂ”[Nephi embeds the disclaimer into the sign itself вЂ” "he shall say... that I, Nephi, know nothing concerning the matter save it were given unto me by the power of God"; about to do something impressive, he scripts in advance the moment that credits God not himself; the more impressive the gift, the more carefully he points past himself]в†’ 9:36 (John 7:16-18; 1 Cor 2:4-5; Hel 5:36)
- `theme:the-crowd-deifies-the-messenger` вЂ”["others who said: Behold, he is a god, for except he was a god he could not know of all things"; the exact error Nephi tried to prevent happened anyway вЂ” faced with a man God works through, some deify the man rather than worship the God; you can deflect glory perfectly and still have it pressed on you]в†’ 9:41 (Acts 14:11-15; Acts 12:22-23; Rev 19:10)
- `theme:the-corrupt-assume-everyone-has-a-price` вЂ”["Behold here is money; and also we will grant unto thee thy life if thou wilt tell us"; they try to buy a false confession вЂ” the native logic of the Gadianton world where everything is transactional; they cannot imagine a man who can't be bought or frightened, and his incorruptibility is itself a witness of a power outside their marketplace]в†’ 9:20 (1 Sam 8:3; Ether 9:11; Matt 26:15)
- `theme:judgment-by-appearance-convicts-the-innocent` вЂ”[the five who came to verify are mistaken for the murderers вЂ” "God has smitten them that they could not flee"; the crowd reasons from appearance to a confident wrong verdict, jailing the witnesses while the killer walks; only the prophet's word and the murderer's confession sort truth from appearance вЂ” an argument for why revelation matters]в†’ 9:6-9 (Prov 18:13; John 7:51; Isa 11:3-4)

### from Helaman 10
- `doctrine:the-condition-of-unlimited-power-is-a-will-that-will-not-ask-amiss` вЂ”["all things shall be done unto thee according to thy word, for thou shalt not ask that which is contrary to my will"; God hands a blank check only because Nephi's will is so unified with His that he will never ask wrongly вЂ” the condition of unlimited power is a will that won't misuse it; the power follows the surrender, not the reverse]в†’ 10:5 (James 4:3; 2 Ne 4:35; D&C 46:30; John 5:30)
- `doctrine:the-sealing-power-bind-and-loose-on-earth-and-in-heaven` вЂ”["whatsoever ye shall seal on earth shall be sealed in heaven; and whatsoever ye shall loose on earth shall be loosed in heaven"; the keys given to Peter (Matt 16:19) given here to Nephi вЂ” power to rend the temple, cast down the mountain, smite the people]в†’ 10:7-10 (Matt 16:19; D&C 132:46-49; Matt 17:20)
- `doctrine:unwearyingness-is-the-commended-virtue` вЂ”[twice God names it вЂ” "thou hast with unwearyingness declared the word"; not a single heroic act but sustained tireless faithfulness, declaring the word again to people who keep rejecting it; the man who doesn't quit is the man God can trust with everything]в†’ 10:4-5 (Acts 20:31; Gal 6:9; 1 Cor 15:58)
- `theme:the-blessing-comes-in-the-valley-not-the-mountaintop` вЂ”[Nephi "much cast down," alone, the crowd scattered, by every visible measure having failed вЂ” and THAT is when "Blessed art thou, Nephi" comes; God's greatest affirmation arrives in the lonely aftermath of apparent defeat (Elijah under the juniper), measuring by the faithfulness the failure obscured]в†’ 10:2-4 (1 Kgs 19:4-12; Acts 23:11; 2 Cor 12:9)
- `theme:the-power-serves-the-ministry-not-the-prophet` вЂ”[given power to rend temples and cast down mountains, the first command is "go and declare... Except ye repent ye shall be smitten" вЂ” preach, plead; the power serves the ministry, doesn't replace it or exalt its holder; he spends world-altering power on calling his enemies to repent]в†’ 10:11-12 (Matt 28:18-20; 2 Cor 10:8; 13:10)
- `theme:thou-art-Nephi-and-I-am-God-the-line-that-humbles-and-protects` вЂ”["Behold, thou art Nephi, and I am God"; God himself draws the line the ch 9 crowd erased ("he is a god") вЂ” even delegating heaven's sealing power, the order is kept absolute; the one who never forgets which side of the line he stands on is the only one who can hold God's power without being destroyed by it]в†’ 10:6 (Hel 9:41; Matt 4:10; Acts 14:15)

### from Helaman 11
- `doctrine:the-prophet-asks-for-affliction-as-mercy` вЂ”["do not suffer that this people shall be destroyed by the sword; but rather let there be a famine... to stir them up in remembrance... and perhaps they will repent"; holding power to smite however he wills, Nephi chooses a lesser redemptive suffering over a greater fatal one вЂ” the sword only kills, the famine leaves time to turn; affliction as the tourniquet that stops a fatal slide]в†’ 11:4-5 (Amos 4:6-10; 1 Kgs 17:1; Alma 62:41)
- `doctrine:affliction-drives-to-remembrance-where-the-word-could-not` вЂ”["the people saw that they were about to perish by famine, and they began to remember the Lord their God"; they wouldn't hearken to the prophet on the tower but they hearkened to hunger вЂ” God prefers the word, uses the famine when the word won't land, and the famine is still mercy because remembering-through-pain beats perishing-in-comfort]в†’ 11:7 (Amos 4:6-10; Hosea 5:15; Ps 119:67, 71)
- `doctrine:real-repentance-sweeps-the-cancer-away-not-just-the-consequence` вЂ”[under famine they "swept away the band of Gadianton from amongst them insomuch that they have become extinct"; true repentance removes the sin that caused the judgment, not just begs the judgment to lift вЂ” they finally did what the Lamanites did in ch 6 and the Nephites wouldn't]в†’ 11:10 (Hel 6:37-38; 2 Cor 7:10-11; Prov 28:13)
- `doctrine:the-intercessor-reasons-from-God's-own-promise` вЂ”[Nephi prays boldly without presumption: "thou saidst that: If this people repent I will spare them... try again if they will serve thee?"; the confidence of the intercessor is grounded not in the people's merit but in God's faithfulness to His own covenant word]в†’ 11:13-16 (Gen 18:23-32; Ex 32:13; 1 Kgs 18:36-45)
- `theme:the-pride-cycle-in-fast-forward` вЂ”[the chapter turns the whole wheel in one span: wars в†’ famine в†’ remembrance в†’ repentance в†’ rain в†’ prosperity в†’ the robbers rise again в†’ "they began again to forget the Lord their God... ripening again for destruction"; the entire cycle revolves in 38 verses, the speed itself the diagnosis]в†’ 11:1-37 (Judg 2:11-19; Hel 4:26; 4 Ne 1:23-39)
- `theme:the-tragedy-of-temporary-remembrance` вЂ”["in the eighty and second year they began again to forget the Lord their God"; the affliction produced remembrance but the remembrance didn't survive the relief вЂ” external pressure can produce repentance, only a converted heart can sustain it; the famine bought remembrance it could not make stick]в†’ 11:34-37 (2 Cor 7:10; Ps 78:34-37; Hel 12:3-4)
- `theme:the-combination-cannot-be-defeated-by-force-alone` вЂ”[entrenched in the mountains and "receiving daily an addition to their numbers" from dissenters, the robbers "defy the whole armies of the Nephites, and also of the Lamanites"; force can't kill an idea that recruits faster than it dies вЂ” only the spiritual remedy (Hel 6:37, hunt AND preach) ever worked; the real war is never the one the armies fight]в†’ 11:24-33 (Hel 6:37; 2 Cor 10:3-4; Eph 6:12)

### from Helaman 12
- `doctrine:man-is-less-than-the-dust-because-the-dust-obeys` вЂ”["how great is the nothingness of the children of men; yea, even they are less than the dust of the earth. For behold, the dust... moveth hither and thither... at the command of our great and everlasting God"; man is lower than dust not because he's smaller but because the dust obeys and man won't вЂ” the one part of creation given a will uses it to refuse the obedience the rest gives freely]в†’ 12:7-8 (Mosiah 4:5; Moses 1:10; Isa 40:15-17; Gen 18:27)
- `doctrine:prosperity-is-the-moment-of-forgetting` вЂ”["at the very time when he doth prosper his people... then is the time that they do harden their hearts, and do forget the Lord their God... because of their ease, and their exceedingly great prosperity"; ease is the solvent вЂ” the moment of greatest blessing is the moment of greatest forgetting, the structure behind the whole pride cycle]в†’ 12:2 (Deut 8:11-18; Hosea 13:6; Hel 11:36)
- `doctrine:chastening-is-the-only-reliable-teacher-of-the-forgetful-heart` вЂ”["except the Lord doth chasten his people with many afflictions... they will not remember him"; the definitive answer to "why affliction" вЂ” chastening is the only thing that reliably reaches a heart that forgets the moment it's comfortable; why Nephi asked for the famine, why a loving God afflicts]в†’ 12:3 (Amos 4:6-11; Ps 78:34; Heb 12:5-11; Hel 11:4)
- `doctrine:the-heart's-asymmetry-quick-to-evil-slow-to-good` вЂ”["how quick to do iniquity, and how slow to do good... how quick to be lifted up in pride... how slow are they to remember"; the natural heart isn't neutral, it's tilted вЂ” sin is the downhill drift requiring no effort, righteousness the uphill work against the grain; why "unwearyingness" is the commended virtue]в†’ 12:4-5 (Rom 7:18-23; Gen 6:5; Mosiah 3:19; Hel 10:4)
- `doctrine:the-root-rebellion-is-not-wanting-God-to-rule` вЂ”["they do not desire that the Lord their God... should rule and reign over them... they will not that he should be their guide"; under every specific sin is one refusal вЂ” the will insisting on its own sovereignty; the exact inverse of Nephi's surrendered will (10:5), and the thing conversion must yield]в†’ 12:6 (Judg 8:23; 1 Sam 8:7; Hel 10:5)
- `doctrine:the-creation-obeys-God's-voice-instantly` вЂ”[at God's voice the mountains break and become smooth, the earth shakes to its center, the earth turns back to lengthen the day ("it appeareth unto man that the sun standeth still... surely it is the earth that moveth"), the sea dries, a mountain buries a city; all creation instantly obeys вЂ” the indicting mirror held up to disobedient man]в†’ 12:8-17 (Job 38-39; Ps 33:6-9; Josh 10:12-13; 3 Ne 8:5-23)
- `doctrine:repentance-was-declared-that-men-might-be-saved` вЂ”["wo unto him to whom he shall say this... he cannot be saved; therefore, for this cause, that men might be saved, hath repentance been declared"; read the *therefore* вЂ” the whole terrible weight of man's nothingness exists to set up this turn; because the doom is real, repentance was deliberately provided; the nothingness of man and the mercy of God held in one hand, mercy the louder note]в†’ 12:22-26 (2 Pet 3:9; Dan 12:2; Alma 42:13)

### from Helaman 13
- `doctrine:happiness-sought-in-iniquity-is-structurally-impossible` вЂ”["ye have sought all the days of your lives for that which ye could not obtain; and ye have sought for happiness in doing iniquity, which thing is contrary to the nature of that righteousness which is in our great and Eternal Head"; happiness IS the nature of God's righteousness, sin is contrary to that nature вЂ” seeking happiness in iniquity is like seeking dryness in the ocean; not forbidden but impossible, a category error]в†’ 13:38 (Alma 41:10-11; 2 Ne 2:13; Ps 16:11)
- `theme:the-slippery-treasures` вЂ”["he curseth your riches, that they become slippery, that ye cannot hold them... we lay a tool here and on the morrow it is gone... we have hid up our treasures and they have slipped away"; the curse fits the sin вЂ” what you set your heart on instead of God becomes the thing you cannot hold, betraying you in the moment you reach for it; fulfilled literally in Mormon 1:18]в†’ 13:31-37 (Luke 12:34; Mormon 1:18; Jer 48:36; Prov 23:5)
- `doctrine:the-curse-is-the-heart-set-on-riches-not-the-riches` вЂ”["ye are cursed because of your riches, and also are your riches cursed because ye have set your hearts upon them... ye do always remember your riches"; the riches aren't the curse (the righteous hides his "unto the Lord") вЂ” the heart set on them is; they remembered the gift and forgot the Giver]в†’ 13:18-22 (Luke 12:15-34; 1 Tim 6:9-10; Deut 8:17-18)
- `theme:the-outsider-prophet-God-sends-the-messenger-you'd-reject` вЂ”[a Lamanite вЂ” the despised race вЂ” stands on the wall of Zarahemla the Nephites won't open, and he is the prophet God sends; their contempt for the messenger sealed their ears to the message; God's truth keeps arriving from the quarter we're most certain it couldn't]в†’ 13:2-4 (Luke 10:33; Matt 8:10; 2 Kgs 5:1-14; Hel 6:1)
- `theme:tomb-builders-honor-dead-prophets-kill-living-ones` вЂ”["If our days had been in the days of our fathers of old, we would not have slain the prophets... Behold ye are worse than they"; the people most certain they'd have honored the old prophets reject the living one вЂ” the dead prophet makes no demands, the living one "testifieth of your sins"]в†’ 13:24-26 (Matt 23:29-37; Luke 11:47-51; Acts 7:51-52)
- `theme:the-flatterer-is-welcomed-the-truth-teller-killed` вЂ”[the man who says "do whatsoever your heart desireth... all is well" they "lift up... give of your gold... clothe with costly apparel," while the prophet who testifies their deeds are evil they stone; the eternal market for the comforting lie over the convicting truth вЂ” the test is which voice you reward]в†’ 13:27-28 (2 Tim 4:3-4; Isa 30:9-10; Micah 2:11; Jer 5:31)
- `doctrine:the-righteous-are-what-hold-back-destruction` вЂ”["it is for the righteous' sake that it is spared... when ye shall cast out the righteous from among you, then shall ye be ripe for destruction"; the righteous are the salt holding back the fire (Abraham for Sodom), and the tipping point is not when the wicked grow numerous but when the righteous are driven out вЂ” Samuel's own casting-out enacts the ripening]в†’ 13:12-14 (Gen 18:23-32; Matt 5:13; Hel 62:40)

### from Helaman 14
- `doctrine:the-two-deaths-and-the-two-tiered-redemption` вЂ”[two deaths handled differently: "this death... redeemeth all mankind from the first death вЂ” that spiritual death" of the Fall, "even all mankind... back into the presence of the Lord" (universal, free); but the "second death" falls only on "whosoever repenteth not... cut off again as to things pertaining to righteousness" (conditional); Christ undoes Adam's wound to all unconditionally, our self-wounds only as we repent]в†’ 14:16-18 (2 Ne 9:6-15; Alma 42:6-15; 1 Cor 15:21-22)
- `doctrine:the-resurrection-redeems-all-mankind-unconditionally` вЂ”["the resurrection of Christ redeemeth mankind, yea, even all mankind, and bringeth them back into the presence of the Lord"; the Fall cut all off through no choice of theirs, so the resurrection brings all back through no merit of theirs вЂ” pure gift to every soul, the universal tier of the atonement]в†’ 14:16-17 (1 Cor 15:21-22; Rom 5:18; 2 Ne 9:21-22)
- `doctrine:ye-are-free-God-hath-made-you-free` вЂ”["ye are free; ye are permitted to act for yourselves; for behold, God hath given unto you a knowledge and he hath made you free... that ye might choose life or death"; everything converges on agency вЂ” the signs remove the excuse, the first death is removed for all, so the only death left is the one you choose; God respects agency enough to let you choose death because freedom that couldn't wouldn't be freedom]в†’ 14:30-31 (2 Ne 2:26-27; Gal 5:1; Moses 6:56; Alma 41:7)
- `doctrine:agency-requires-knowledge-freedom-and-real-consequence` вЂ”[God gave three things to make the choice real: knowledge ("know good from evil"), freedom ("made you free"), the law of restoration ("do good and be restored unto that which is good... or do evil, and have that which is evil restored"); you can't meaningfully choose without knowing the options, being free to take either, and the choice mattering]в†’ 14:30-31 (Alma 41:3-15; 2 Ne 2:5; Gal 6:7)
- `doctrine:whosoever-perisheth-perisheth-unto-himself` вЂ”["whosoever perisheth, perisheth unto himself; and whosoever doeth iniquity, doeth it unto himself"; perdition is never imposed but self-administered by a free creature who knew good from evil and chose evil вЂ” the most sobering and most dignifying truth at once]в†’ 14:30 (3 Ne 3:11; Ezek 18:20; Deut 30:19)
- `theme:the-dated-falsifiable-signs-leave-no-cause-for-unbelief` вЂ”[precise dated signs вЂ” five years to the birth (a day-night-day with no darkness, a new star), three days of darkness and the rent rocks at the death вЂ” "to the intent that there should be no cause for unbelief"; God over-provides the evidence so unbelief can only be a choice, converting the verdict into self-condemnation; all fulfilled in 3 Ne 1 + 8]в†’ 14:2-29 (3 Ne 1:15-21; 3 Ne 8:5-23; Matt 27:45-53; Hel 9:25-37)
- `theme:remember-that-you-are-free` вЂ”["remember, remember, my brethren, that whosoever perisheth, perisheth unto himself"; the Helaman refrain (ch 5, 12) landing on agency вЂ” a free creature who forgets it's free drifts into blaming circumstance; to remember you are free is to own your choices, the beginning of being able to choose differently]в†’ 14:30 (Hel 5:9-12; Hel 12:3; Deut 30:19)

### from Helaman 15
- `doctrine:chastening-is-the-proof-of-love-not-its-absence` вЂ”["the people of Nephi hath he loved, and also hath he chastened them; yea, in the days of their iniquities hath he chastened them because he loveth them"; the whole affliction arc resolves вЂ” the famine, the wars, the chastening were all love, expressed AS the discipline not withheld during it; the resolution of "why affliction" is fatherly love]в†’ 15:3 (Heb 12:5-11; Prov 3:11-12; Rev 3:19)
- `doctrine:the-converts-from-darkness-hold-the-light-more-firmly-than-the-born-in` вЂ”[the converted Lamanites are "firm and steadfast in the faith... because of their firmness when they are once enlightened" вЂ” more steadfast than the chosen Nephites ever were; those who had to cross the most ground to reach the truth hold it most fiercely; the faith you never had to choose is the one you can most easily lose]в†’ 15:5-10 (Alma 23:6-7; 24:17-26; Luke 7:47)
- `doctrine:the-curse-tracks-deeds-rooted-in-tradition-not-blood` вЂ”["the Lamanites hath he hated because their deeds have been evil continually, and this because of the iniquity of the tradition of their fathers. But behold, salvation hath come unto them"; what God hated was evil DEEDS traced to false TRADITION вЂ” the moment the tradition was replaced, the disfavor reversed; if it were blood, conversion couldn't lift it; because it's tradition-and-deeds, conversion lifts it completely]в†’ 15:4 (2 Ne 5:21; Alma 3:11-19; Hel 6:34-36) вЂ” with-Michael 2 Ne 5 thread
- `doctrine:the-latter-day-mercy-and-restoration-of-the-Lamanite-remnant` вЂ”["notwithstanding they shall be driven to and fro... hunted... scattered abroad... the Lord shall be merciful unto them... they shall again be brought to the true knowledge... and be numbered among his sheep"; a Lamanite prophet promises his own scattered descendants the scattering won't be the end вЂ” the Book of Mormon's stated purpose (Title Page: not cast off forever)]в†’ 15:11-13 (1 Ne 13:31; 2 Ne 10:18-19; 3 Ne 16:11-12; Morm 5:20)
- `doctrine:less-light-more-faith-the-privileged-convicted-by-the-deprived` вЂ”["had the mighty works been shown unto them which have been shown unto you... they never would again have dwindled in unbelief"; the Lamanites given less light would have done more with it than the Nephites did with more вЂ” Christ's Tyre-and-Sidon principle; the most damning judgment is what someone with fewer advantages would have made of yours]в†’ 15:14-15 (Matt 11:20-24; Luke 10:13-14; Hel 7:23-24)
- `theme:love-fully-exercised-can-still-end-in-the-beloved's-destruction` вЂ”[He "loved" and "chastened" the very people He's about to let be destroyed; the chastening was the long patient mercy that failed only because they would not receive it; the destruction isn't the failure of God's love but the exhaustion of a love that respected their freedom to the end]в†’ 15:3, 16-17 (Matt 23:37-38; Luke 19:41-44; Hel 14:30)

### from Helaman 16
- `doctrine:when-the-miracle-cannot-be-denied-the-hardened-heart-reassigns-its-source` вЂ”[unable to hit Samuel, the unbelievers re-credit the protection to the devil: "he hath a devil; and because of the power of the devil... we cannot hit him"; the Pharisees' Beelzebub move (Matt 12:24) вЂ” admit the miracle, invert its meaning; unfalsifiable unbelief, because every miracle becomes more evidence of the devil's reach; the problem was never the evidence but a will already decided]в†’ 16:6 (Matt 12:24-32; Mark 3:22-30; Hel 9:16)
- `theme:the-modern-rationalizations-against-prophecy` вЂ”[the contemporary catalog: "some things they may have guessed right" (lucky guesses, v16); "why will he not show himself unto us as well as unto them at Jerusalem" (show-me-on-my-terms, v18-19); "a wicked tradition... they can keep us in ignorance" (v20) вЂ” the anti-faith arguments of every age, spoken 2000 years ago]в†’ 16:16-21 (Alma 30:13-28; 2 Pet 3:3-4; Matt 12:38-39)
- `theme:religion-as-a-control-mechanism-the-clerical-control-suspicion` вЂ”["they will... work some great mystery which we cannot understand, which will keep us down to be servants to their words, and also servants unto them"; the suspicion that religion exists to keep the masses dependent and subservient вЂ” a remarkably modern critique voiced by Nephite skeptics; faith recast as a tool of clerical power]в†’ 16:20-21 (Alma 30:23-28; Isa 5:21)
- `theme:depending-on-one's-own-wisdom-is-the-root-of-the-rationalizing` вЂ”[the people "began to depend upon their own strength and upon their own wisdom" вЂ” and the rationalizations followed; the cause isn't the arguments but the prior choice to make one's own reasoning the measure over revelation (Isa 5:21); once self-wisdom is the standard, endless reasons not to believe can be generated]в†’ 16:15 (Isa 5:21; Prov 3:5-7; Hel 4:13)
- `doctrine:the-purpose-of-prophecy-is-remembrance-that-becomes-future-faith` вЂ”[Nephi tells them of things "which must shortly come, that they might know and remember at the time of their coming that they had been made known unto them beforehand, to the intent that they might believe"; prophecy is a seed planted now so fulfillment later waters it into faith вЂ” the same event a witness to one heart, a coincidence to another]в†’ 16:4-5 (3 Ne 1:4-22; John 13:19; 14:29)
- `theme:opposition-intensifies-as-the-evidence-intensifies` вЂ”[in the very year the signs begin вЂ” angels appearing, "the words of the prophets began to be fulfilled" вЂ” Satan works hardest, "spreading rumors and contentions... that he might harden the hearts"; the closer the manifestation, the fiercer the counter-effort; the brightest light draws the hardest opposition]в†’ 16:13-23 (3 Ne 1:22; Matt 13:19; 1 Pet 5:8)

## вЂ” END OF HELAMAN (16 chapters) В· 3 NEPHI BEGINS (the signs fulfilled в†’ the great destruction в†’ Christ descends) вЂ”

### from 3 Nephi 1
- `doctrine:the-God-who-speaks-from-heaven-is-the-God-about-to-be-born` вЂ”["on the morrow come I into the world, to show unto the world that I will fulfil all that which I have caused to be spoken by the mouth of my holy prophets"; the premortal Christ speaks from heaven the night before His birth вЂ” fully God on the night before becoming fully an infant, entering by His own will; the voice from heaven and the cry from the manger are one Person]в†’ 1:13-14 (Luke 2:10-11; John 1:11; Mosiah 3:5)
- `doctrine:Christ-is-both-Father-and-Son` вЂ”["I come... to do the will, both of the Father and of the Son вЂ” of the Father because of me, and of the Son because of my flesh"; the Mosiah 15 Christology spoken by Christ Himself the night before His birth вЂ” Father by His divinity, Son by the flesh He's about to take; the divinity established before the manger]в†’ 1:14 (Mosiah 15:1-5; Ether 3:14; D&C 93:3-4)
- `theme:faith-tested-to-the-death-deadline-and-the-last-hour-deliverance` вЂ”[the believers under a death sentence with a date вЂ” killed "except the sign should come to pass" вЂ” and the Lord answers the very day Nephi prays "all that day," execution imminent: "on this night shall the sign be given"; deliverance at the last possible moment, not before, because faith can only be tested in the gap between promise and fulfillment]в†’ 1:9-15 (Ex 14:13-14; Gen 22:10-13; Dan 3:17-25)
- `theme:the-sign-fulfilled-every-whit-prophecy-vindicated` вЂ”["at the going down of the sun there was no darkness... it was as light as though it was mid-day... all things, every whit, according to the words of the prophets"; Samuel, the Lamanite on the wall they drove away, right to the detail; the believers who held through the deadline vindicated, the rejected prophet proven by the heavens]в†’ 1:15-21 (Hel 14:3-5; Josh 10:13; 1 Kgs 8:56)
- `theme:the-persecutor's-plan-of-destruction-frustrated` вЂ”[the unbelievers who set the death-deadline "fell to the earth and became as if they were dead, for they knew that the great plan of destruction which they had laid... had been frustrated"; the trap built for the righteous sprang on its makers]в†’ 1:16 (Esth 7:9-10; Ps 7:15-16; Prov 26:27)
- `theme:Satan-works-to-make-people-disbelieve-what-they-saw` вЂ”[the instant the sign is given, "there began to be lyings sent forth among the people, by Satan... that they might not believe in those signs and wonders which they had seen"; Satan works to revise the memory of an undeniable event вЂ” the miracle doesn't end the battle; but this time "the more part did believe"]в†’ 1:22 (Hel 16:22-23; Moses 5:13; 2 Thes 2:9-11)
- `theme:the-rising-generation-lost-to-flattery-righteousness-not-inherited` вЂ”[the rising generation of the righteous Lamanites "led away by... lyings and flattering words" to join the robbers, so "the Lamanites began to decrease as to their faith"; even at the threshold of Christ's coming the next generation slips вЂ” righteousness is never inherited]в†’ 1:29-30 (Judg 2:10; Mosiah 26:1-4; 4 Ne 1:38)

### from 3 Nephi 2
- `doctrine:familiarity-dulls-the-miracle-the-three-stage-forgetting` вЂ”[a three-stage collapse: "less and less astonished at a sign or a wonder from heaven" в†’ "hard in their hearts, and blind in their minds" в†’ "disbelieve all which they had heard and seen"; the night with no darkness became unremarkable within years вЂ” habituation drained the wonder the scoffers' arguments never could; once astonishment dies the doubt has an open door]в†’ 2:1-2 (Ex 14:31; 16:2-3; Ps 78:11-32; Heb 3:12-15)
- `doctrine:the-curse-is-lifted-on-covenant-affiliation` вЂ”["those Lamanites who had united with the Nephites were numbered among the Nephites; And their curse was taken from them... and were called Nephites"; the change tracks covenant-affiliation вЂ” joining the people of God вЂ” exactly as every other treatment frames it; the literal "skin became white" phrasing still sits unreconciled against the belief-and-allegiance framing, the residue left for Michael + the Spirit]в†’ 2:14-16 (2 Ne 5:21; 30:6; Jacob 3:8; Alma 3:6; Hel 15:4) вЂ” with-Michael 2 Ne 5 thread
- `theme:the-calendar-remembers-what-the-heart-forgets` вЂ”["the Nephites began to reckon their time from this period when the sign was given, or from the coming of Christ"; time itself got a new center вЂ” a structural confession of faith built into dating a year (as AD/BC) вЂ” even as the same people forget the signs; the structures of faith keep pointing at Christ when the heart has gone dull]в†’ 2:7-8 (Ex 12:2; Luke 2:1-7)
- `theme:the-dissolution-of-race-into-covenant` вЂ”[the two peoples who warred six centuries "take up arms" together to defend "the privileges of their church and of their worship, and their freedom and their liberty"; the converted Lamanites "numbered among the Nephites, and were called Nephites" вЂ” race dissolved into covenant, the line was always belief not blood]в†’ 2:11-16 (Alma 23:16-18; Hel 6:34-36; Gal 3:28; Eph 2:14-19)
- `theme:Christ-comes-to-a-people-who-forgot-the-sign` вЂ”["the sword of destruction did hang over them... because of their iniquity"; even as the calendar marks the years since His coming, the majority slides back вЂ” and it is into exactly this forgetful, hardening, war-torn people that Christ will descend; He comes not to those who earned it by remembering well, but anyway]в†’ 2:19 (Rom 5:8; 4 Ne 1:38-39; Luke 19:41-44)

### from 3 Nephi 3
- `theme:the-inverted-conscience-calling-evil-good` вЂ”["I am the governor of this the secret society of Gadianton; which society and the works thereof I know to be good"; Giddianhi sincerely believes murder is good and cites its "ancient date" as a credential вЂ” Isaiah's "woe unto them that call evil good" walking; more frightening than open villainy because it has lost the line entirely; the most dangerous evil experiences itself as virtue]в†’ 3:9 (Isa 5:20; 2 Ne 15:20; Hel 6:26-30)
- `theme:the-aggressor-reframes-himself-as-the-victim` вЂ”[Giddianhi recasts the robbers as "recovering their rights... who have dissented away from you because of your wickedness"; the murderers the wronged party вЂ” but Mormon corrects: they "had received no wrong, save it were they had wronged themselves by dissenting"; the oldest move in grievance, manufacturing an injury to justify aggression]в†’ 3:10-11 (3 Ne 1:10; Hel 14:30; Prov 19:3)
- `doctrine:God-delivers-the-defender-not-the-aggressor` вЂ”[the people propose to "go up... and fall upon the robbers and destroy them in their own lands"; Gidgiddoni forbids: "if we should go up against them the Lord would deliver us into their hands... we will wait till they shall come against us"; the same God who delivers the robbers to a waiting defender would deliver the Nephites to the robbers if they attack вЂ” the righteousness of the cause does not license the preemptive strike; even against murderers, become the aggressor and you forfeit the protection]в†’ 3:20-21 (Alma 43:46-47; 48:14; Morm 3:10-11)
- `doctrine:the-righteous-response-to-threat-is-prayer-plus-preparation-plus-repentance` вЂ”[Lachoneus refuses fear and negotiation, and does BOTH: fortifies, gathers, arms вЂ” AND commands "except ye repent... and cry unto the Lord, ye will in nowise be delivered"; fortifications without repentance trust the arm of flesh, repentance without fortifications tempt God; faith and works held together]в†’ 3:12-16 (2 Chr 20:1-17; Neh 4:9; James 2:17-18; Ps 20:7)
- `theme:the-prophet-general-military-command-joined-to-spiritual-gift` вЂ”[Gidgiddoni was "a great prophet," and "it was the custom among all the Nephites to appoint for their chief captains... some one that had the spirit of revelation and also prophecy"; strategy by revelation, so he could overrule the popular war-plan because he relayed what the Lord forbade, not a military opinion]в†’ 3:18-19 (Alma 48:11-16; 16:5-8; Num 27:18-21)
- `theme:the-combination-recruits-as-brotherhood` вЂ”["unite with us... become our brethren that ye may be like unto usвЂ”not our slaves, but our brethren and partners of all our substance"; the recruitment pitch dressed as brotherhood and shared spoils вЂ” the flattering offer of belonging-plus-gain the secret oath always extends]в†’ 3:6-7 (Hel 6:21-22; Prov 1:11-14)

### from 3 Nephi 4
- `doctrine:fear-of-God-displaces-fear-of-men-the-un-terrorizable-heart` вЂ”[the robbers come in terror-paint "dyed in blood" and the Nephites fall to the earth; the robbers misread it, shouting for joy вЂ” "they did not fear them; but they did fear their God"; what looked like terror was prayer; the heart that has given its ultimate fear to God cannot be ruled by the fear of men вЂ” terror works only on those with no greater fear to displace the lesser]в†’ 4:8-10 (Prov 29:25; Isa 51:12-13; Matt 10:28; Dan 3:16-18)
- `doctrine:in-the-strength-of-the-Lord-not-their-own` вЂ”["in the strength of the Lord they did receive them"; the explicit answer to Hel 4:13 вЂ” there they "boasted in their own strength" and were "left in" it and lost; here they fight in the Lord's strength and prevail against a more numerous foe; same nation, opposite outcome, the difference being whose strength they trusted]в†’ 4:10, 33 (Hel 4:13; 1 Sam 17:45-47; Ps 44:3-6)
- `doctrine:the-delivered-give-all-the-glory-to-God-and-credit-repentance` вЂ”[after victory they "break forth, all as one, in singing, and praising their God... Hosanna to the Most High God"; and "they knew it was because of their repentance and their humility that they had been delivered" вЂ” crediting the spiritual posture and God's goodness, not their own competence; the reversal of the pride that destroyed them, the shape that keeps a victory]в†’ 4:31-33 (Ex 15:1-21; 2 Chr 20:21-28; Hel 12:2; Ps 124)
- `theme:starve-the-parasite-deny-the-host` вЂ”[the robbers lived by plunder, so the Nephites gathered everything to one place and left the land "desolate" вЂ” "the robbers could not exist save it were in the wilderness, for the want of food"; a band that lives by robbery cannot survive with nothing to rob; defeat what feeds on you not by chasing it into its strongholds but by denying it what it feeds on]в†’ 4:1-6, 16-22 (Gen 41:33-57; Rom 13:14; Gal 5:16)
- `theme:provisioning-as-the-prudence-that-makes-deliverance-possible` вЂ”[the Nephites "reserved for themselves provisions... that they might subsist for the space of seven years"; the siege backfired because they were the provisioned ones вЂ” the Joseph-in-Egypt prudence; deliverance came through God, but God worked through a people who had prepared]в†’ 4:4, 18 (Gen 41:33-57; D&C 4:4; Prov 6:6-8)
- `theme:vigilance-not-victory-is-the-permanent-posture-against-the-combinations` вЂ”[they hang Zemnarihah and "fell the tree to the earth," praying to "fell to the earth all who shall seek to slay them because of power and secret combinations"; the felled tree symbolizes the felled combination, and the prayer is for ongoing vigilance вЂ” the combination has one ancient author and rises again, so the only safety is to keep felling it "in righteousness and in holiness of heart"]в†’ 4:28-29 (Hel 6:26-30; Ether 8:18-25; 1 Pet 5:8)

### from 3 Nephi 5
- `doctrine:the-record-is-a-disciple's-testimony-for-a-salvific-purpose` вЂ”["I am called Mormon... Behold, I am a disciple of Jesus Christ, the Son of God. I have been called of him to declare his word among his people, that they might have everlasting life"; the abridger steps out from behind the record, identifying himself as a disciple first, not a neutral historian вЂ” the record is a follower's testimony made for salvation; "I know the record which I make to be a just and a true record" (provenance in Mormon's own voice)]в†’ 5:12-18 (W of M 1:1-11; Morm 1:1-4; 3 Ne 30:1)
- `doctrine:the-combination-is-ended-by-the-dual-method-mercy-to-the-repentant-justice-to-the-unrepentant` вЂ”[the robber prisoners preached to: "as many as would repent... and enter into a covenant that they would murder no more were set at liberty," while those with "secret murders in their hearts" were "punished according to the law" вЂ” "thus they did put an end to all those... combinations"; neither all-force nor all-mercy could end it, only the real choice offered to all вЂ” the Hel 6:37 method the Nephites had refused, finally applied]в†’ 5:4-6 (Hel 6:37-38; Alma 62:16-17; Rom 11:22)
- `doctrine:the-gathering-of-Israel-is-the-book's-purpose` вЂ”[after naming himself Mormon declares the covenant: God "shall again bring a remnant of the seed of Joseph to the knowledge of the Lord... will he gather in from the four quarters of the earth all the remnant of the seed of Jacob"; the title-page mission stated at the book's midpoint вЂ” the record exists to gather scattered Israel back to Christ]в†’ 5:21-26 (1 Ne 22:8-12; 2 Ne 30:1-8; 3 Ne 16:6-13; Title Page)
- `doctrine:the-spiritual-gathering-precedes-the-geographic` вЂ”["then shall they know their Redeemer, who is Jesus Christ... and then shall they be gathered in... unto their own lands"; the knowing comes first, the gathering-to-lands follows вЂ” the restoration of Israel is first coming to know Christ, the physical gathering flowing from the spiritual]в†’ 5:26 (2 Ne 30:7; 3 Ne 20:29-34; Deut 30:1-5)
- `theme:the-abridger-writes-toward-a-future-scattered-reader` вЂ”[Mormon, writing from a civilization he knows will be destroyed, looks past its destruction to "a remnant of the seed of Joseph" in a distant day; he engraves a record his people will lose, for descendants scattered across the earth, so they will one day "know their Redeemer" вЂ” the whole labor an act of covenant faith across millennia, aimed at that future reader]в†’ 5:14-26 (Morm 8:34-41; 2 Ne 3:12; Moro 10:3-5)

### from 3 Nephi 6
- `doctrine:the-only-thing-that-can-stop-a-prospering-people-is-their-own-sin` вЂ”["there was nothing in all the land to hinder the people from prospering continually, except they should fall into transgression"; nothing external could stop them вЂ” the only enemy left was themselves, and the "except" names the one exception that would in fact occur; the deadliest threat is never the enemy at the border but the corruption in the heart]в†’ 6:5, 10 (Hel 4:11-13; Deut 8:11-18; Luke 12:15)
- `doctrine:inequality-of-wealth-and-learning-breaks-up-the-church` вЂ”[the most explicit class-analysis in the book: riches в†’ "pride and boastings" в†’ merchants/lawyers/officers в†’ "distinguished by ranks, according to their riches and their chances for learning... some ignorant because of poverty, others great learning because of riches" в†’ "great inequality... insomuch that the church began to be broken up"; the exact inverse of the 4 Nephi Zion ("no rich and poor") вЂ” the breakup of the church begins not with heresy but with inequality]в†’ 6:11-14 (4 Ne 1:2-3, 15-17; Jacob 2:13-21; James 2:1-9; Acts 4:32-35)
- `doctrine:willful-rebellion-against-known-light-is-the-graver-sin` вЂ”["they did not sin ignorantly, for they knew the will of God concerning them... therefore they did wilfully rebel against God"; not the sin of a people who never heard but the willful rebellion of a people who knew вЂ” Mormon removes the excuse of ignorance; greater light makes the sin heavier]в†’ 6:18 (Hel 7:23-24; Luke 12:47-48; Num 15:30-31)
- `theme:the-same-railing-makes-some-rail-back-and-others-grow-penitent` вЂ”["some did return railing for railing, while others would receive railing and persecution... and would not turn and revile again, but were humble and penitent"; the same pressure sorts people by how they respond вЂ” the proud retaliate, the humble absorb and turn to God; the persecution doesn't determine the response, the heart's existing direction does (Alma 62:41 again)]в†’ 6:13 (Matt 5:39; 3 Ne 12:39; Rom 12:17-21; Alma 62:41)
- `theme:the-establishment-is-angriest-at-the-prophets` вЂ”[those angriest were "chiefly the chief judges, and they who had been high priests and lawyers"; the religious-legal establishment most resists the truth-tellers and murders them "secretly by the judges" bypassing the law; it is the establishment, not an outside invader, that destroys the truth]в†’ 6:21-23 (Hel 13:24-28; Matt 23:29-37; Acts 7:51-52; John 11:47-53)
- `theme:the-combination's-endgame-is-to-overthrow-the-republic-and-install-a-king` вЂ”[the murderers' kindred "enter into a covenant... given and administered by the devil" to free the guilty and "destroy the governor, and to establish a king over the land, that the land should no more be at liberty"; the ancient covenant traced to Cain (Hel 6) revived for its ultimate prize вЂ” capture the state, abolish freedom, install monarchy; the direct assault on Mosiah 29's reign of judges]в†’ 6:28-30 (Hel 6:26-30; Ether 8:9-19; Mosiah 29:13-23; 1 Sam 8:5)

### from 3 Nephi 7
- `doctrine:society-fragments-into-tribalism-when-the-binding-loyalty-is-lost` вЂ”[the government destroyed, the people "separate one from another into tribes, every man according to his family and his kindred and friends"; when the larger order fails вЂ” first the church (ch 6), then the civil order вЂ” people retreat to the smallest reliable loyalty, blood and kin; a people united by covenant can be one body across family lines, a people who've lost it have nothing left but blood, which divides as easily as it bonds]в†’ 7:2-6 (Judg 17:6; 21:25; 1 Sam 8:5-7)
- `doctrine:the-relapse-is-worse-than-never-having-known-the-dog-to-its-vomit` вЂ”["six years had not passed away since the more part of the people had turned from their righteousness, like the dog to his vomit, or like the sow to her wallowing in the mire"; the horror is not that they fell but that they RETURNED to the wickedness they'd been cleansed from вЂ” a special wretchedness that despises the cleansing (2 Pet 2:21, better not to have known); the speed plus the revulsion]в†’ 7:8 (2 Pet 2:20-22; Prov 26:11; Heb 6:4-6)
- `doctrine:order-without-righteousness-civil-peace-with-stoned-prophets` вЂ”[the tribes establish "very strict laws... insomuch that in some degree they had peace in the land; nevertheless, their hearts were turned from the Lord their God, and they did stone the prophets"; a society can be peaceful, law-abiding, orderly, AND killing the prophets вЂ” outward stability is no measure of spiritual health, and is more dangerous than open chaos because the functioning order masks the inward apostasy]в†’ 7:14 (Isa 48:22; 57:21; Jer 6:14; Matt 23:27-29)
- `doctrine:undeniable-power-provokes-anger-not-faith-in-the-hardened` вЂ”["they were angry with him, even because he had greater power than they, for it were not possible that they could disbelieve his words"; faced with a man who raises the dead, the hardened heart turns to rage rather than belief вЂ” you cannot argue with a man who raises the dead, so you hate him; the greatest evidence produces fury, because the obstacle was never the evidence but a will already set against God]в†’ 7:18-20 (Hel 16:6; 3 Ne 1:22; John 11:47-53)
- `theme:faith-so-great-that-angels-minister-daily` вЂ”["so great was his faith on the Lord Jesus Christ that angels did minister unto him daily"; the heavens continuously open вЂ” not in occasional crises but as a constant condition, the fruit of the "unwearyingness" God commended in the earlier Nephi; a faith sustained without wavering opens heaven daily, and he raised his own martyred brother from the dead]в†’ 7:15, 18-19 (Hel 10:4; John 11:43-44; Moro 7:29-37)
- `theme:the-gospel's-ordinances-hold-even-when-the-society-collapses` вЂ”[amid anarchy and stoned prophets, "there were none who were brought unto repentance who were not baptized with water," and Nephi "ordained men unto this ministry"; the covenant ordinances don't depend on a functioning society вЂ” when the nation fragments and the church breaks up, baptism and the priesthood still stand, administered by the faithful few for the few who come; the kingdom of God is not the order of the land]в†’ 7:24-25 (2 Ne 31:5-13; D&C 20:37; Acts 8:36-38)

### from 3 Nephi 8
- `doctrine:the-record's-reliability-rests-on-the-moral-purity-of-its-keeper` вЂ”["we know our record to be true, for behold, it was a just man who did keep the record... there was not any man who could do a miracle in the name of Jesus save he were cleansed every whit from his iniquity"; the reliability of the testimony rests on the proven holiness of the witness вЂ” Nephi's miracles prove his cleansed state, which vouches for his honesty; God doesn't work miracles through the unclean, so the miracles are retroactively the warrant for the record]в†’ 8:1 (3 Ne 7:19-20; John 21:24; Acts 3:6-16)
- `doctrine:power-in-Christ's-name-requires-purity` вЂ”["there was not any man who could do a miracle in the name of Jesus save he were cleansed every whit from his iniquity"; power in Christ's name flows only through a cleansed channel вЂ” you cannot wield His power while clutching your iniquity]в†’ 8:1 (Morm 9:18-25; Moro 7:33-37; D&C 121:36-37)
- `doctrine:the-creation-convulses-at-the-death-of-its-Creator` вЂ”[at Christ's death a storm "such an one as never had been known," earthquake "as if it was about to divide asunder," the rocks rent "in seams and in cracks" вЂ” the same convulsion that on the other hemisphere rent the temple veil and split the rocks (Matt 27:51); the crucifixion was not a local event but a cosmic one, the earth recoiling at the death of the God who made it]в†’ 8:5-18 (Matt 27:45-54; Luke 23:44-45; Hel 12:8-17)
